# Bestiary

## Humanoids

## Threat Rating 1/4

#### Commoner (Human)
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 40 (Con 5 × 8)
**DR:** 0 (no armor)
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 5 / Agi 3 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Background:** Laborer
**Skills:** Might 2, Athletics 2, Constitution saves 1, Craft 1
**Senses:** Normal
**Creature Type:** Humanoid (no special immunities)
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Languages:** Common

**Attacks:**
- **Club [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 0), Reach: 5 ft
  - ***Margin 1:*** 4 damage, Margin 2: 8 damage (4 + 4 Str)

**Alternative Actions:**
- **Grapple/Shove:** Str 4 + Athletics 2 (opposed by target's Str + Athletics)
  - On success, can grapple (restrain) or shove (knock prone or push 5 ft)

**Feats:**
- **Starting Feats:** None (0 feats - untrained civilian)
- **Purchased Feats:** None (0 maximum at TR 1/4)

**Description:** Everyday working people - laborers, dockworkers, farmers in off-season, craftspeople, servants. No combat training whatsoever. Strong and hardy from physical work (hence Con 5) but completely inexperienced in fighting. When encountered, they're typically going about their business and want nothing to do with adventurers or violence. May be intimidated, bribed, or reasoned with easily. Form angry mobs only when pushed to desperation by tyranny or injustice. Loyal to their community but not suicidal.

**Tactics:** Commoners avoid combat whenever possible. If forced to fight, they use improvised weapons (clubs, tools, pitchforks) and rely on numbers. More likely to grapple, shove, or flee than engage in actual weapon combat. Will break and run if taking casualties. May fight to defend their homes/families but otherwise have no combat training or courage. In groups of 5+, may gain confidence and use mob tactics (surrounding, grappling to hold enemies for others to strike).

**Equipment:** Club (improvised weapon), work clothes, work gloves, work boots

**Variants:**
- **Farmer:** Replace Athletics 2 with Wilderness 2, use Farmer background (Wilderness 2, Might 2, Athletics 1, Craft 1)
- **Dock Worker:** Same stats, carries cargo hook instead of club (same damage)
- **Servant:** Use Servant background (Empathy 3, Society 3, Perception 3, Stealth 3, Deception 3, Pattern A with +40 XP), lower Str to 3, raise Dex to 4
- **Craftsperson:** Replace Might 2 with Craft 3, use appropriate artisan tools

---

### Threat Rating 1/2

#### Militia Member (Human)
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 24 (Con 3 × 8)
**DR:** S: 2, P: 1, B: 3 (aketon)
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 3, Athletics 2, Intimidate 1, Perception 2
**Background:** Soldier
**Senses:** Normal
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Humanoid (no special immunities)
**Languages:** Common

**Attacks:**
- **Spear [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
  - One-handed:
    - ***Margin 1:*** 6 damage
    - ***Margin 2:*** 10 damage (6 + 4 Str)
  - Two-handed (versatile):
    - ***Margin 1:*** 7 damage
    - ***Margin 2:*** 11 damage (7 + 4 Str)

**Reactions:**
- **Shield Block (from Buckler):** Attacker must reroll one of their success dice. This is a [Free] action, usable once per round (no reaction cost).
- **Shield Master:** Once per combat as a [Reaction], completely negate one attack that would hit you.
- **Force Reroll:** [Reaction] once per round, Attacker must reroll one of their success dice
- **Increase DR:** [Reaction] once per round, Gain +2 DR against this attack only

**Feats:**
- **Defensive Stance** (Agi 3, Melee 3): Can enter a defensive stance as a toggle. While in defensive stance, opponents add 1 to both attack dice when attacking you. Can enter or leave this stance at the start of your turn.
- **Danger Sense** (Wis 3): Subtract 1 from both dice on Reflex saves against effects you can see.
- **Shield Master** (Str 3, Melee 3, must use shield - 40 XP): Subtract 1 from both dice on Reflex saves while using a shield.

**Description:** Local militia members called to defend their town or region. Part-time soldiers - farmers, craftsmen, merchants, and workers who train together regularly for local defense. More disciplined and organized than bandits but less professional than full-time soldiers. Loyal to their community and willing to defend it, though they may break and flee if facing overwhelming odds or supernatural threats. They know the local area well and can call for reinforcements from fellow militia or town guards.

**Tactics:** Militia members use defensive tactics, forming shield walls with Defensive Stance when outnumbered. They use spears to maintain reach, keeping enemies at bay while supporting each other. Shield Master allows them to negate one devastating attack per fight - typically saved for critical moments. They fight in coordinated groups when possible, using their numbers and defensive training to overcome individual skill gaps. Against ranged attackers, they advance in formation, shields raised.

**Equipment:** Spear, buckler, aketon armor, uniform, bedroll, high boots, common clothes

**Variants:**
- **Militia Archer:** Replace Melee Combat 3 with Ranged Combat 3, use shortbow instead of spear, replace Shield Master with Precise Shot
- **Militia Sergeant:** Add +1 to Cha (becomes 3), add Intimidating Presence as a purchased feat (requires Cha 4 - would need to adjust attributes or wait for TR 1 version)

---

#### Thug (Human)
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 24 (Con 3 × 8)
**DR:** 0 (no armor)
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 3 / Con 3 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Stealth 3, Thievery 2, Deception 2, Intimidate 2, Melee Combat 3
**Background:** Criminal
**Senses:** Normal
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Humanoid (no special immunities)
**Languages:** Common

**Attacks:**
- **Dagger [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
  - ***Margin 1:*** 4 damage
  - ***Margin 2:*** 9 damage (4 + 5 Agi)
- **With Exploit Weakness:** When ally within 5 ft of target OR subtracting from attack dice, add Dex 4 to damage
  - ***Margin 1:*** 8 damage (4 + 4 Dex)
  - ***Margin 2:*** 13 damage (4 + 5 Agi + 4 Dex)
- **Thrown (Range 30/60 ft):** Use Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 0
  - ***Margin 1:*** 4 damage
  - ***Margin 2:*** 9 damage (4 + 3 Str)

**Feats:**
- **Swift Movement** (Agi 4): Can Disengage or Hide using only 1 [Minor] action instead of a full action. Perfect for hit-and-run tactics.
- **Danger Sense** (Wis 3): Subtract 1 from both dice on Reflex saves against effects you can see. Represents street-smart reflexes.
- **Exploit Weakness** (Agi 4, Stealth or Thievery 3, 40 XP): Once per round, when attacking with an ally within 5 feet of target OR subtracting from attack dice (from any source), add Dexterity score (4) to damage.

**Description:** Street criminals - muggers, gang members, hired muscle for criminal organizations. More dangerous than commoners due to actual combat training (Melee 3) and willingness to use violence. Operate in rough neighborhoods, extorting shopkeepers, robbing travelers, collecting debts for loan sharks. Cowards at heart - fight dirty, gang up on isolated victims, flee when facing real danger. May be redeemed or may be irredeemably vicious depending on circumstances. Criminal background gives them underworld contacts for fencing stolen goods.

**Tactics:** Thugs rely on numbers and dirty fighting. They use Swift Movement to dart in, attack with allies nearby (triggering Exploit Weakness for +4 damage), then Disengage as a [Minor] action to avoid retaliation. Prefer ambushes from stealth (Stealth 3) and will flee if facing organized opposition or taking heavy damage. Use Intimidate 2 to cow victims into submission rather than fighting. Will throw daggers only when fleeing or unable to close to melee. In groups of 3+, they surround enemies to constantly trigger Exploit Weakness. One thug distracts while others stab from behind. If one goes down, the rest typically flee unless led by someone more dangerous (like a gang leader or TR 1 Enforcer).

**Equipment:** Dagger, crowbar, common clothes, belt pouch, wool hood, low boots

**Variants:**
- **Pickpocket:** Raise Thievery 2→4 (20 XP), lower Melee Combat 3→2 (saves 12 XP), more focused on theft than combat, use Swift Movement to escape after stealing
- **Enforcer:** Use Mercenary background for better combat training, represents gang muscle who collects debts and intimidates
- **Burglar:** Raise Stealth 3→4 (24 XP), replace Danger Sense with Supreme Stealth feat when qualified at TR 2, focused on breaking and entering

---

### Threat Rating 1

#### Town Guard (Human)
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 32 (Con 4 × 8)
**DR:** S: 6, P: 5, B: 2 (chain mail)
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Perception 3, Intimidate 3, Society 1, Athletics 2
**Background:** Guard
**Senses:** Normal
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Humanoid (no special immunities)
**Languages:** Common

**Attacks:**
- **Longsword [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
  - One-handed:
    - ***Margin 1:*** 8 damage
    - ***Margin 2:*** 12 damage (8 + 4 Str)
  - Two-handed (versatile):
    - ***Margin 1:*** 9 damage
    - ***Margin 2:*** 13 damage (9 + 4 Str)
  - **With Power Attack (declared before roll):** Add 1 to both dice, deal +1d8 damage on hit

**Reactions:**
- **Shield Block (requires wielding a shield):**
  - **Shield Block (from heater shield):** [Reaction] once per round, force Misfortune on one ranged attack (up to 60 ft range)
  - **Shield Master Negation:** Once per combat as [Reaction], completely negate one attack that would hit you
  - **Force Reroll:** [Reaction] once per round, Attacker must reroll one of their success dice
  - **Increase DR:** [Reaction] once per round, Gain +2 DR against this attack only

**Feats:**
- **Defensive Stance** (Agi 3, Melee 3): Can enter defensive stance where opponents add 1 to both attack dice when attacking you. Toggle on/off at start of turn. Used when outnumbered or protecting others.
- **Danger Sense** (Wis 3): Subtract 1 from both dice on Reflex saves against effects you can see. Represents trained awareness.
- **Power Attack** (Str 3, Melee 3, 40 XP): Declare before rolling - add 1 to both die results and deal +1d8 damage on hit. Risk/reward for ending fights quickly.
- **Shield Master** (Str 3, Melee 3, must use shield, 40 XP): Subtract 1 from both dice on Reflex saves while using shield.

**With Heater Shield:** Gains Fortune on defensive melee rolls

**Description:** Professional city guards - trained, disciplined, paid soldiers who take their duty seriously. Unlike militia (part-timers) or thugs (criminals), these are career guardsmen with years of experience. They know the law, recognize troublemakers, and maintain order. Respect from citizens, feared by criminals. Will show mercy to those who surrender but are hardened enough to use lethal force when necessary. Loyal to their city and fellow guards - won't abandon posts or comrades easily.

**Tactics:** Town guards are professional soldiers who patrol cities and enforce laws. They use formation tactics, working in pairs or small groups. When facing threats, they use Defensive Stance to protect citizens while calling for backup. Against dangerous foes, they use Power Attack to end fights quickly before reinforcements arrive. The heater shield provides excellent defense against both melee (Fortune on defense rolls) and ranged attacks (force Misfortune on attackers).
Guards prioritize de-escalation and arrest over lethal force when possible, using Intimidate 3 to command compliance. They know the local area (Society 1) and can quickly summon help. Against multiple weak opponents, they hold defensive positions. Against single strong opponents, they use Power Attack aggressively while one guard runs for help.
Shield Master's once-per-combat negation is saved for critical moments - blocking a potentially fatal blow to themselves or buying time for civilians to escape.

**Equipment:** Longsword, heater shield, chain mail, uniform, manacles, work gloves, work boots

**Variants:**
- **Gate Guard:** Replace Intimidate 3 with Investigate 3, focused on spotting smugglers and checking papers
- **Archer Guard:** Replace Melee 4 with Ranged 4, use longbow instead of longsword, swap Power Attack for Precise Shot
- **Sergeant:** Add +1 Cha (becomes 3), can lead 4-6 guards effectively

---

## Daemons

These monsters follow the Bestiary Framework guidelines and demonstrate proper monster design for the Legends system.


## Threat Rating 1/8

### Giant Rat
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 12 (Con 2 × 6, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 2 / Con 2 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 1 / Wis 3 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 2, Stealth 3, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Keen Smell
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Beast
- **Attacks:**
  - **Bite [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 5 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 3 damage (Small size, light natural weapon: 4 - 1 = 3)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 5 damage (3 + 2 Str)

- **Special Abilities:**
  - **Pack Tactics:** When an ally is within 5 feet of the target, subtract 1 from both attack dice
  - **Keen Smell:** Scent-based Perception checks have Fortune
  - **Disease Carrier:** On hit with margin 2, target must make Fortitude save (1 success needed) or contract Filth Fever
    - ***Incubation:*** 1d8 days
    - ***Effect:*** Poisoned condition until cured
    - ***Cure:*** Two consecutive successful Fortitude saves (1/day) OR magical healing

**Tactics:** Giant rats rely on Pack Tactics and numbers. They swarm lone targets, attempting to spread disease through repeated bites.

---

## Threat Rating 1/4

---

### Goblin
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
**DR:** S: 3, P: 1, B: 4 (leather armor)
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 2 / Con 2 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 2 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 3, Ranged Combat 2, Stealth 4, Perception 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Humanoid (no special immunities)
- **Attacks:**
  - **Scimitar [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 5 damage (Small size, standard weapon: 6 - 1 = 5)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 7 damage (5 + 2 Str)
- **Shortbow [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 80/320 ft
  - Short range (80 ft):
    - ***1 success*** = 5 damage
    - ***2 successes*** = 8 damage (5 + 3 Dex)
  - Medium range (160 ft):
    - ***2 successes*** = 8 damage
  - Long range (320 ft):
    - ***2 successes*** needed, add 1 to both dice, 8 damage
- **Reactions:**
  - **Shield Block:** When hit by melee attack, choose one:
    - Attacker must reroll one of their success dice
    - Gain +2 DR against this attack only

- **Special Abilities:**
  - **Nimble Escape:** Can take Disengage or Hide as a [Minor] action instead of a standard action
  - **Pack Tactics:** When an ally is within 5 feet of the target, subtract 1 from both attack dice

**Tactics:** Goblins use hit-and-run tactics. They fire arrows from cover using superior numbers, then use Nimble Escape to retreat when enemies close. Shield-wielding goblins protect archers.

**Equipment:** Scimitar (standard weapon), shortbow, leather armor, small shield

---

## Threat Rating 1/2

---

### Orc Warrior
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** S: 3, P: 1, B: 4 (leather armor)
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 3 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Ranged Combat 2, Intimidate 3, Perception 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Creature Type:** Humanoid (no special immunities)
- **Attacks (Greataxe Configuration):**
  - **Greataxe [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 10 damage (two-handed weapon)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 14 damage (10 + 4 Str)
- **Attacks (Battleaxe + Shield Configuration):**
  - **Battleaxe [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 8 damage (heavy one-handed weapon)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 12 damage (8 + 4 Str)
- **Ranged Attack:**
  - **Javelin [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 30/120 ft
    - Short range:
      - ***1 success*** = 6 damage
      - ***2 successes*** = 9 damage (6 + 3 Dex)
    - Medium range:
      - ***2 successes*** = 9 damage

- **Reactions (Shield Configuration Only):**
  - **Shield Block:** When hit by melee attack, choose one:
    - Attacker must reroll one of their success dice
    - Gain +2 DR against this attack only

- **Special Abilities:**
  - **Aggressive:** Once per turn as a [Free] action, can move up to speed toward a hostile creature it can see
  - **Relentless (1/day):** When reduced to 0 HP, make Fortitude save:
    - ***1+ successes:*** Drop to 1 HP instead of 0 HP

**Tactics:** Orcs charge aggressively using their Aggressive ability to close quickly. Greataxe wielders focus on devastating damage while shield bearers use Shield Block to protect themselves and hold the line. All orcs fight to the death using Relentless when dropped.

**Equipment:** Greataxe OR battleaxe + shield, 2 javelins, leather armor

---

## Threat Rating 1

---

### Wolf Pack Leader
- **Threat Rating:** 1
- **Size:** Medium
- **HP:** 32 (Con 4 × 8, Standard)
- **DR:** 0
- **Speed:** 50 ft
- **Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
- **Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Perception 5, Stealth 4, Survival 3
- **Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Keen Hearing and Smell
- **Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Attacks:**
- **Bite [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 5 vs opponent's defense)
  - Reach: 5 ft
  - Margin 1: 6 damage (standard natural weapon)
  - Margin 2: 10 damage (6 + 4 Str)
  - Special: On margin 2+, target must make Fortitude save (Con + Luck, 1 success) or be knocked Prone
**Special Abilities:**
- **Pack Tactics:** When an ally is within 5 feet of the target, subtract 1 from both attack dice
- **Keen Hearing and Smell:** Sound and scent-based Perception checks have Fortune
- **Coordinated Strike (1/day):** As a [Free] action when this wolf hits an enemy, all allied wolves within 5 feet of that enemy can immediately make one bite attack as a reaction
**Creature Type:** Beast (no special immunities)
**Tactics:** The pack leader coordinates wolf attacks, using Pack Tactics and Coordinated Strike to bring down large prey. It targets spellcasters and archers first, attempting to knock them prone for the pack to tear apart.

---

## Threat Rating 2

---

### Ogre
- **Threat Rating:** 2
- **Size:** Large
- **HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
- **DR:** 2 (thick hide, natural armor)
- **Speed:** 40 ft
- **Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 1 / Wis 2 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
- **Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Ranged Combat 1, Might 5, Intimidate 3
- **Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
- **Equipment:** Greatclub (two-handed weapon), 3 javelins
- **Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
- **Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Large size (10×10 ft space, 10 ft reach). Powerful Build: counts as one size larger for carrying, pushing, dragging, lifting. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.
**Attacks:**
- **Greatclub [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 10 ft (Large creature with long weapon)
  - Margin 1: 12 damage (Large size, two-handed weapon: 10 + 2 = 12)
  - Margin 2: 18 damage (12 + 6 Str)
- **Javelin [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 1)
  - Range: 30/120 ft (Large creature, increased range)
  - Short range: 1 success = 8 damage (Large size: 6 + 2), 2 successes = 10 damage (8 + 2 Dex)
  - Medium range: 2 successes = 10 damage
**Special Abilities:**
- **Powerful Build:** Counts as Huge for carrying capacity, pushing, dragging, lifting
- **Thick Hide:** Natural DR 2 (already included in stat block DR)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant)
**Tactics:** Ogres throw javelins as enemies approach, then wade into melee with their greatclub, using their reach to strike before enemies can close. They focus on one target at a time, attempting to crush them with overwhelming strength.

---

### Ghoul
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 52 (Con 4 × 13, Standard Undead)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 30 ft, Climb 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 3 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Stealth 4, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Undead (Immune to poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, exhaustion. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.)
- **Attacks:**
  - **Bite [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 6 damage (standard natural weapon)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 9 damage (6 + 3 Str)
  - **Claws [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 4 damage (light natural weapon)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 7 damage (4 + 3 Str)
    - ***Special:*** On any hit (margin 1+), target must make Fortitude save:
      - 0 successes: Paralyzed for 1 minute
      - 1+ successes: No effect
      - Paralyzed creatures can repeat save at end of each turn (2 successes ends early, 1 success adds Fortune to next save)
- **Multiattack [Combat]:** The ghoul makes one bite and two claw attacks
  - ***Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 4):*** Roll once, apply to all three attacks

- **Special Abilities:**
  - **Paralytic Claws:** Creatures hit by claw attacks must save vs paralysis (see Claws attack)
  - **Spider Climb:** Can climb difficult surfaces including upside-down on ceilings without ability checks
  - **Paralyze Immunity:** Ghouls and other undead are immune to ghoul paralysis

**Resistances/Immunities:**
- **Immunities:** Poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, exhaustion

**Tactics:** Ghouls use stealth and climbing to ambush prey from unexpected angles. They use Multiattack to maximize chances of landing paralytic claw strikes, then feast on paralyzed victims. They gang up on dangerous foes to trigger multiple paralysis saves.

---

## Threat Rating 3

---

### Owlbear
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 2 (thick hide and feathers, natural armor)
**Speed:** 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 1 / Wis 4 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Perception 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Keen Sight and Smell
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Monstrosity (no special immunities)
- **Attacks:**
  - **Beak [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft (Large creature)
    - ***Margin 1:*** 10 damage (Large size, heavy natural weapon: 8 + 2 = 10)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 16 damage (10 + 6 Str)
  - **Claws [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6 vs opponent's defense), Reach: 10 ft (Large creature)
    - ***Margin 1:*** 10 damage (Large size, standard natural weapon: 8 + 2 = 10, representing both claws)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 16 damage (10 + 6 Str)
- **Multiattack [Combat]:** The owlbear makes one beak attack and one claw attack
  - ***Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 4):*** Roll once, apply to both attacks

- **Special Abilities:**
  - **Large Size:** Occupies 10×10 ft space, 10 ft reach
  - **Keen Sight and Smell:** Vision and scent-based Perception checks have Fortune
  - **Maul:** If both attacks (beak AND claw) hit the same target in one turn, target takes additional 8 damage (no attribute modifier, represents crushing embrace)
  - **Aggressive Charge (Recharge 6-8):** If the owlbear moves at least 20 feet straight toward a target and then hits with a claw attack on the same turn, the target must make a Fortitude save (1 success) or be knocked Prone. If prone, owlbear can immediately make a beak attack as a [Free] action.

**Tactics:** Owlbears charge aggressively, attempting to trigger Aggressive Charge to knock prey prone. They use Multiattack every round, trying to trigger Maul for devastating damage. Wounded owlbears become frenzied and reckless.

---

### Basilisk
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 90 (Con 5 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 4 (thick scales, natural armor)
**Speed:** 20 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 5 / Agi 3 / Dex 2 / Int 1 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Stealth 4, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Creature Type:** Monstrosity (no special immunities)
- **Attacks:**
  - **Bite [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 8 damage (heavy natural weapon) + Poisoned
    - ***Margin 2:*** 13 damage (8 + 5 Str) + Poisoned
  **Poison Bite:**
  - On any hit, target becomes Poisoned
    - ***Duration:*** 1 hour OR until cured by Medicine check (2 successes) or magical healing

- **Special Abilities:**
  - **Petrifying Gaze (Passive, at-will):** When a creature that can see the basilisk's eyes starts its turn within 30 feet, the basilisk can force it to make a Fortitude save:
    - ***0 successes:*** Begin turning to stone - Restrained
    - At end of affected creature's next turn, make another Fortitude save:
      - ***0 successes:*** Turned to stone (Petrified - effectively dead until restored by magic)
      - ***1+ successes:*** Restrained condition ends, no longer turning to stone
  - **Averting Eyes:** Creatures can choose to avert eyes as a [Free] action. While averting:
    - Immune to petrifying gaze
    - All attacks against basilisk have Misfortune
    - Basilisk's attacks against averting creature subtract 1 from both dice
- **Thick Scales:** Natural DR 4 (already included in stat block)

**Resistances:**
- **Poison Resistance:** +1 DR against poison damage

**Tactics:** Basilisks rely on their petrifying gaze to control the battlefield. They wait for enemies to fail saves and become Restrained, then close for poisonous bites. Against multiple foes, they position to catch as many in their gaze as possible. Smart enemies avert their eyes but suffer severe combat penalties.

---

## Threat Rating 4

---

### Young Red Drake
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 5 (dragon scales, natural armor)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Climb 40 ft, Fly 80 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Perception 7, Stealth 4, Arcane 4, Intimidate 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Drake (Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 30 ft, can inspire fear, Immune to Fear)
- **Attacks:**
  - **Bite [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 12 damage + 6 fire damage
    - ***Margin 2:*** 18 damage (12 + 6 Str) + 6 fire damage
  - **Claw [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6 vs opponent's defense), Reach: 5 ft
    - ***Margin 1:*** 8 damage (Large, light weapon: 6 + 2)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 14 damage (8 + 6 Str)
- **Multiattack [Combat]:** The dragon makes one bite attack and two claw attacks
  - ***Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 4):*** Roll once, apply to all three attacks
**Breath Weapon:**
- **Fire Breath (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** 30-foot cone. Each creature in area makes Reflex save:
  - Add 1 to both Reflex save dice (represents difficulty of avoiding)
  - ***0 successes:*** 40 fire damage
  - ***1 success:*** 20 fire damage
  - ***2+ successes:*** 10 fire damage

- **Special Abilities:**
  - **Large Size:** Occupies 10×10 ft space, reach varies by attack
  - **Frightful Presence (3/day):** Each creature of dragon's choice within 60 feet that can see it must make Will save (1 success needed):
    - Failure: Frightened for 1 minute (can repeat save at end of each turn)
    - Success: Immune to this dragon's Frightful Presence for 24 hours
  - **Dragon Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 30 ft

**Resistances/Immunities:**
- **Immunity:** Fire damage, Frightened condition
- **Resilient Defense:** 2/day - When fails a saving throw, can choose to succeed instead

**Tactics:** Young dragons open with Frightful Presence to scatter weaker foes, then unleash Fire Breath on clustered enemies. They use flight to stay mobile, strafing with breath weapon when recharged. In melee, they use Multiattack to focus down dangerous spellcasters. Dragons retreat if reduced below 60 HP, remembering enemies for future vengeance.

---

## Threat Rating 5

---

### Stone Golem
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (stone body, natural armor)
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 1 / Wis 3 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Construct (Immune to poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified. Mindless: immune to mind-affecting effects (Beguiling Weave, fear, Sleep), fear, psychic effects. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.)
- **Attacks:**
  - **Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 10 ft 
    - ***Margin 1:*** 12 damage (Large, two-handed natural: 10 + 2)
    - ***Margin 2:*** 19 damage (12 + 7 Str)
- **Multiattack [Combat]:** The golem makes two slam attacks
  - ***Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 2):*** Roll once, apply to both attacks

- **Special Abilities:**
  - **Large Size:** Occupies 10×10 ft space, 10 ft reach
  - **Magic Resistance:** Subtract 1 from both dice on saving throws against magical effects
  - **Slow (Recharge 6-8) [Combat]:** Targets up to 3 creatures within 10 feet. Targets make Will save:
    - ***0 successes:*** Can only take 2 actions per turn (instead of 3) and cannot take reactions for 1 minute
    - ***1+ successes:*** No effect
    - Add 1 to both Will save dice (difficulty of resisting)
    - Affected creatures can repeat save at end of each turn (1 success ends early)
  - **Immutable Form:** Immune to any weave that would alter its form (transformation, Beastial Transformation, etc.)

**Resistances/Immunities:**
- **Immunities:** Poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, charm, fear, psychic damage, non-magical piercing and slashing damage
- **Magic Resistance:** Subtract 1 from both dice on saves vs magical effects

**Tactics:** Stone golems advance inexorably, using Slow to cripple multiple enemies before crushing them with massive slams. They ignore most damage types and magic, making them terrifying juggernauts. Golems follow orders literally and never retreat.

### Ember Mote (Fire)
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 1 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 2, Perception 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; immune to fire damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
**Attacks:**
  - **Scorch [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 5 ft
      - **Margin 1:** 2 damage (Tiny, standard natural weapon: 3 − 1 = 2) + 2 fire damage
      - **Margin 2:** 3 damage + 2 fire damage

**Special Abilities:**
  - **Illumination:** Sheds dim light in a 10-foot radius at all times.
  - **Flammable Contact:** Any flammable object the Ember Mote touches ignites at the end of the round unless held by a creature who spends 1 [Interact] action smothering it.

**Tactics:** Ember Motes dart toward flammable targets or anything the summoner points them at. They are not strategic. They burn and that is their entire agenda. Most useful for lighting torches, igniting terrain, or harrying enemies who are already engaged with something else.

### Dust Devil (Air)
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Native
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
DR: 0
Speed: 30 ft, Fly 40 ft (Hover)
Attributes: Str 2 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 1 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 2, Perception 2
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; immune to lightning damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Buffet [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 3 damage (Small, standard natural weapon)
    - Margin 2: 5 damage (3 + 2 Str)
Special Abilities:
  - Whirlwind Form: The Dust Devil can pass through spaces as narrow as 1 inch without squeezing. Creatures attempting to grab or grapple it add 1 to both dice.
  - Sand Scatter: Once per turn as a [Free] action, the Dust Devil can kick up grit and debris in a 5-foot diameter. Creatures in range make a Reflex save (1 success) or gain the Dazzled condition until the start of their next turn.
Tactics: Dust Devils harass and distract. They position to use Sand Scatter on spellcasters or archers, then slip away before retaliation. A Friendly Dust Devil takes these instructions naturally; an Indifferent one drifts toward whoever seems most interesting.

### Mud Grub (Earth)
Threat Rating: 1/8
Size: Small
HP: 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
DR: 1 (hardened clay shell)
Speed: 20 ft, Burrow 20 ft
Attributes: Str 3 / Con 2 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 1 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 2, Perception 1
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 30 ft
Initiative Bonus: +2 (Agi 2)
Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Bite [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 3 damage (Small, standard natural weapon)
    - Margin 2: 6 damage (3 + 3 Str)
Special Abilities:
  - Burrowing: Can move through earth and loose stone at its burrow speed. Movement through solid rock is not possible.
  - Drag Under: When the Mud Grub successfully grapples a creature that is standing on earth or soil, the creature sinks 1 foot into the ground. A sinking creature gains the Restrained condition until it pulls free (Might or Athletics check, Hard task, 2 successes).
Tactics: Mud Grubs burrow under enemies and attack from below, attempting to grapple and use Drag Under to immobilize. Useful for pinning a single target rather than dealing meaningful damage.

### Riptide Sprite (Water)
Threat Rating: 1/8
Size: Small
HP: 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
DR: 0
Speed: 20 ft, Swim 40 ft
Attributes: Str 2 / Con 2 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 1 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 2, Perception 2
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4) Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; immune to cold damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Water Lash [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 3 damage (Small, standard natural: 3) + 2 cold damage
    - Margin 2: 5 damage (3 + 2 Str) + 2 cold damage
Special Abilities:
  - Aqueous Form: Can enter and exit water as a [Free] action. While in water, attacks against it add 1 to both dice.
  - Slick Passage: When the Riptide Sprite moves through a space, that space becomes Difficult Terrain until the start of the Sprite's next turn (water coating the ground).
Tactics: These sprites are most effective near water or in wet environments. On dry ground they are merely annoying; in a flooded room or near a river they are genuinely threatening, using Slick Passage to create hazardous terrain and their reach to attack without closing.

### Flame Hound (Fire)
Threat Rating: 1/4
Size: Medium
HP: 20 (Con 2 × 8, Tough, rounded down from 2.5 × 8)
DR: 0
Speed: 40 ft
Attributes: Str 3 / Con 3 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 3, Perception 3, Stealth 2
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Keen Smell (Fortune on scent-based Perception)
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; immune to fire damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Bite [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 6 damage (standard natural weapon) + 2 fire damage
    - Margin 2: 9 damage (6 + 3 Str) + 2 fire damage
    - Margin 3: 9 damage + 2 fire damage; target gains Singed condition
Special Abilities:
  - Blazing Pounce (Recharge 5-8): If the Flame Hound moves at least 20 feet and hits with its Bite on the same turn, target makes a Fortitude save (1 success) or gains the Ignited condition.
  - Fire Aura: Creatures that hit the Flame Hound with a melee attack take 2 fire damage.
Tactics: Flame Hounds open with Blazing Pounce when it's available, then use their speed to stay adjacent and maintain fire aura pressure. They track by scent and pursue fleeing targets without instruction.

### Stone Soldier (Earth)
Threat Rating: 1/2
Size: Medium
HP: 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
DR: 3 (granite skin)
Speed: 25 ft
Attributes: Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 3 / Dex 2 / Int 2 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 4, Might 3, Perception 2
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 30 ft
Initiative Bonus: +3 (Agi 3)
Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Slam [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 6 damage (standard natural weapon)
    - Margin 2: 11 damage (6 + 5 Str)
    - Margin 3: 11 damage; target is knocked Prone
Reactions:
  - Stone Skin: [Reaction] once per round, Gain +2 DR against one attack.
Special Abilities:
  - Immovable Mass: The Stone Soldier cannot be knocked Prone by any non-magical forced movement. Shoves and bull rushes automatically fail unless the attacker wins an opposed Strength + Athletics check against the Soldier's Strength + Might (2 successes required).
  - Gravel Rain: Once per encounter as a [Combat] action, the Stone Soldier slams the ground, sending a spray of rock fragments in a 10-foot cone. Creatures in area make a Reflex save (1 success) or take 8 bludgeoning damage (half on success). Full DR applies.
Tactics: Stone Soldiers advance steadily and hold ground. They will not pursue at speed; they outlast opposition rather than chase it. A summoner who needs something to simply not move will find them ideal.

### Gale Specter (Air)
Threat Rating: 1
Size: Medium
HP: 32 (Con 4 × 8, Standard)
DR: 0
Speed: 20 ft, Fly 60 ft (Hover)
Attributes: Str 2 / Con 4 / Agi 6 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Ranged Combat 3, Perception 4
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 30 ft
Initiative Bonus: +6 (Agi 6)
Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; immune to lightning damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Wind Strike [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 6 damage (standard natural weapon)
    - Margin 2: 8 damage (6 + 2 Str); target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or is pushed 10 feet
    - Margin 3: 8 damage; target pushed 10 feet and knocked Prone (no save)
  - Lightning Arc [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 3), Range: 60 ft
    - Margin 1: 8 lightning damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 12 lightning damage (8 + 4 Dex) (Half DR)
Multiattack [Combat]: The Gale Specter makes one Wind Strike and one Lightning Arc.
Special Abilities:
  - Storm Body: The Gale Specter is difficult to hold. Grapple attempts add 1 to both dice. If successfully grappled, it makes a Fortitude save at the start of its turn (1 success) to break free automatically.
  - Momentum Defense: While it has moved at least half its fly speed this turn, attacks against it add 1 to both attack dice.
Tactics: Gale Specters use their fly speed aggressively, staying mobile to maintain Momentum Defense. They use Wind Strike to push melee fighters away from protected targets and Lightning Arc to pressure at range. A Cooperative Gale Specter will follow target priority; an Indifferent one picks whoever seems most challenging.

### Deep Tide (Water)
Threat Rating: 2
Size: Large
HP: 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
DR: 2 (fluid body disperses impact)
Speed: 20 ft, Swim 60 ft
Attributes: Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Might 4, Perception 3
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 30 ft (in water)
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; immune to cold damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Slam [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 12 damage (Large size, standard natural weapon: 8 + 2 = 10... + 2 water surge bonus)
    - Margin 2: 17 damage (10 + 5 Str + 2); target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or is knocked Prone
Multiattack [Combat]: The Deep Tide makes two Slam attacks. Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 4).
Special Abilities:
  - Engulf (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]: The Deep Tide surges over one creature of Medium size or smaller within 5 feet. Target makes a Reflex save (opposed by Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5). On failure, the creature is Grappled and Restrained within the elemental's body. Each round it remains engulfed, the creature takes 8 cold damage and must make a Fortitude save (Constitution + Current Luck, 1 success) or gain 1 Exhaustion level from the crushing water pressure. A creature can use an action to attempt to escape (Might or Athletics, Hard task, 2 successes).
  - Water Mastery: While in water, the Deep Tide's attacks ignore cover, and the Engulf recharge DC drops to 4-8.
Tactics: Deep Tides prioritize Engulf, targeting whoever the summoner indicates or whoever poses the greatest threat. On dry ground they are dangerous but limited; near water they become significantly more capable and will attempt to drag engulfed targets into any body of water present.

### Magma Drake (Fire)
Threat Rating: 3
Size: Large
HP: 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
DR: 5 (volcanic hide)
Speed: 30 ft, Burrow 20 ft (through earth and stone)
Attributes: Str 6 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 6, Perception 5, Intimidate 4
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Tremorsense 60 ft
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; immune to fire damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Bite [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 10 damage + 6 fire damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 16 damage (10 + 6 Str) + 6 fire damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 3: 16 damage + 6 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition
  - Claw [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 10 damage (Large, standard natural weapon)
    - Margin 2: 16 damage (10 + 6 Str)
Multiattack [Combat]: The Magma Drake makes one Bite and two Claw attacks. Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 4).
Special Abilities:
  - Magma Surge (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]: The Magma Drake vomits a torrent of lava in a 30-foot cone. Each creature in the area makes a Reflex save. Compare Drake's Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6 targeting to each target's save successes. Net 1: 12 fire damage; Net 2: 24 fire damage + Ignited; Net 3: 24 fire damage + Burning. Full DR does not apply (Half DR).
  - Living Heat: Creatures that start their turn within 5 feet of the Magma Drake take 4 fire damage (Half DR) automatically.
  - Lava Walk: The Magma Drake can move across lava or magma without penalty. Its burrowing creates a channel of superheated stone that cools within 1 minute (dealing 8 fire damage to creatures who enter the channel before it cools).
Tactics: Magma Drakes are apex hunters. They burrow beneath battlefields and surface under enemy formations when Magma Surge is available, then wade into melee. The Living Heat aura discourages sustained close combat while they churn through targets with their multiattack. They are intelligent enough to protect a summoner if clearly instructed.

### Elder Stormcaller (Air)
Threat Rating: 4
Size: Large
HP: 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
DR: 3 (diffuse air body)
Speed: 20 ft, Fly 80 ft (Hover)
Attributes: Str 4 / Con 6 / Agi 7 / Dex 5 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
Skills: Melee Combat 7, Ranged Combat 6, Perception 6
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 60 ft
Initiative Bonus: +7 (Agi 7)
Creature Type: Elemental (immune to poison, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious; immune to lightning damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Wind Blade [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 7 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
    - Margin 1: 10 damage + 8 lightning damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 14 damage (10 + 4 Str) + 8 lightning damage; target pushed 15 feet
    - Margin 3: 14 damage + 8 lightning damage; target pushed 15 feet and Stunned until end of their next turn
  - Chain Lightning [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 6), Range: 120 ft, up to 4 targets. Targets must be within 30 ft of each other
    - Margin 1: 20 lightning damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 40 lightning damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 3: 40 lightning damage + Stunned until end of their next turn
Multiattack [Combat]: The Elder Stormcaller makes two Wind Blade attacks. Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 7).
Special Abilities:
  - Storm Presence: When the Elder Stormcaller takes its turn, all creatures within 30 feet must make a Fortitude save (1 success) or be buffeted — movement speed halved until the start of their next turn as howling wind presses against them.
  - Momentum Defense: While it has moved at least half its fly speed this turn, attacks against it add 1 to both attack dice.
  - Eye of the Storm: The summoner and allies the Stormcaller designates are immune to Storm Presence's effects.
  - Lightning Immunity Aura: Creatures the Stormcaller designates as protected gain resistance to lightning damage (+4 DR) while within 30 feet.
  - Resilient Defense (2/day): When the Stormcaller fails a saving throw, it may choose to succeed instead.
Tactics: Elder Stormcallers command battlefields from altitude, using Storm Presence to slow enemy movement while delivering Chain Lightning to clustered targets. They descend for Wind Blade strikes when softening up isolated threats. A Friendly Elder Stormcaller is a genuine tactical partner; even an Indifferent one tends to find the most dramatic target and hammer it.

### Pixie (Fae)
Threat Rating: 1/8
Size: Tiny
HP: 10 (Con 2 × 5, Fragile)
DR: 0
Speed: 20 ft, Fly 30 ft
Attributes: Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
Skills: Stealth 4, Perception 3, Deception 3, Thievery 3
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Fae (Fortune on saves vs charm effects; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep in the conventional sense)
Attacks:
  - Needle [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 1), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 1 damage
    - Margin 2: 2 damage + target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains Poisoned (Weak) for 1 hour (pixie dust)
Special Abilities:
  - Invisibility (At-Will): The Pixie can become invisible as a [Minor] action. The invisibility ends if it attacks or casts a weave.
  - Natural Tiny: Has Fortune on Stealth checks.
  - Fairy Dust: Once per short rest, the Pixie can dust one willing creature or itself with faintly luminescent powder. The dusted creature gains Fortune on one saving throw of their choice within the next minute.
Tactics: Pixies are scouts and mischief-makers. They avoid combat if possible, preferring to steal, distract, or mislead. A Cooperative Pixie makes an excellent spy. An Indifferent one might interpret "distract the guard" as "steal the guard's lunch and hide in his helmet."

### Sprite (Fae)
Threat Rating: 1/4
Size: Tiny
HP: 12 (Con 2 × 6, Fragile)
DR: 0
Speed: 20 ft, Fly 40 ft
Attributes: Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 5 / Int 3 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
Skills: Stealth 4, Perception 4, Ranged Combat 4, Wilderness 3
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5) Creature Type: Fae (Fortune on saves vs charm effects)
Attacks:
  - Shortbow [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 40/80 ft
    - Margin 1: 3 damage (Tiny: 4 − 1) + Fortitude save (1 success) or Poisoned (Weak) for 1 minute
    - Margin 2: 8 damage (3 + 5 Dex) + Fortitude save or Poisoned (Weak) for 1 hour
Special Abilities:
  - Heart Sight: Once per encounter, when the Sprite looks at a creature's eyes, it automatically discerns the creature's emotional state and whether it is lying. Will saves and Deception checks against the Sprite add 1 to both dice for creatures whose heart it has read.
  - Nature's Ally: The Sprite can communicate with beasts and plants as if they share a language.
Tactics: Sprites are excellent scouts and poison delivery systems. They rarely engage in melee, preferring to shoot from concealment. A Cooperative Sprite that has used Heart Sight can report back honestly on whether an NPC is trustworthy — one of the most genuinely useful things a low-tier summoner can get.

### Boggart (Fae)
Threat Rating: 1/2
Size: Small
HP: 27 (Con 3 × 9, Tough)
DR: 2 (thick hide)
Speed: 30 ft
Attributes: Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 4, Stealth 4, Deception 3, Intimidate 3, Perception 3
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Fae (Fortune on saves vs charm effects)
Attacks:
  - Claws [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 5 damage (Small, standard natural weapon: 6 − 1 = 5)
    - Margin 2: 9 damage (5 + 4 Str)
    - Margin 3: 9 damage; target makes Will save (1 success) or gains Frightened condition for 1 round
Special Abilities:
  - Frightful Visage: As a [Combat] action, the Boggart distorts its face into something deeply wrong. One creature within 30 feet that can see it makes a Will save opposed by the Boggart's Cha 2 + Intimidate 3 (total 5). On failure, target gains the Frightened condition until end of their next turn.
  - Shadow Meld: In dim light or darkness, the Boggart has Fortune on Stealth checks.
Tactics: Boggarts prefer to ambush from shadows, using Frightful Visage to scatter formation fighters before closing. They are selfish but not suicidal — a Boggart that is clearly losing will attempt to flee. They make poor bodyguards and excellent shock troops for a single terrifying moment.

### Redcap (Fae)
Threat Rating: 1
Size: Small HP: 40 (Con 5 × 8, Tough)
DR: S: 3, P: 2, B: 4 (iron-soled boots and dense body)
Speed: 35 ft
Attributes: Str 5 / Con 5 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 2 / Cha 3 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Intimidate 4, Athletics 3, Perception 2
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Fae (Fortune on saves vs charm effects)
Attacks:
  - Scythe [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 8 damage [Slashing]
    - Margin 2: 13 damage (8 + 5 Str) [Slashing]; target gains 1 Bleeding stack
    - Margin 3: 13 damage; target gains 2 Bleeding stacks
  - Boot Stomp [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft (only against Prone targets)
    - Margin 1: 8 damage [Bludgeoning]
    - Margin 2: 13 damage; target is Pinned until the Redcap moves away
Special Abilities:
  - Blood Thirst: The Redcap's cap must be soaked in fresh blood or it loses its power. When the Redcap deals a Bleeding stack to any creature, it gains temporary HP equal to 4. This is its motivation and its obsession; a Redcap given no targets will eventually find some.
  - Iron Boots: The Redcap's kicks and stomps deal full damage to constructs that would otherwise be immune to bludgeoning.
Tactics: Redcaps charge the most vulnerable target they can reach, stack Bleeding as fast as possible, and stomp downed targets with their boots. A summoner who points a Redcap at an enemy and steps back should not expect precision; they should expect enthusiasm.

### Erlking's Scout (Fae)
Threat Rating: 2
Size: Medium
HP: 52 (Con 4 × 13, Standard)
DR: 2 (fae resilience)
Speed: 40 ft, Fly 20 ft
Attributes: Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 5 / Int 4 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Ranged Combat 5, Stealth 6, Perception 6, Wilderness 4
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision, Truesight 30 ft
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Fae (Fortune on saves vs charm effects)
Attacks:
  - Fae Blade [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 8 damage + 4 psychic damage (Ignore DR)
    - Margin 2: 12 damage (8 + 4 Str) + 4 psychic damage
  - Hunter's Arrow [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 80/160/320 ft
    - Margin 1: 8 damage
    - Margin 2: 13 damage (8 + 5 Dex); target cannot benefit from invisibility or the Hidden condition for 1 hour (marked by fae scent)
Special Abilities:
  - Hunter's Mark: As a [Minor] action, the Scout designates one creature as its quarry. Against the quarry, the Scout subtracts 1 from both attack dice. Only one quarry can be designated at a time.
  - Fae Step (1/short rest): As a [Move] action, the Scout teleports up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space it can see.
  - Truesight 30 ft: Sees through invisibility, illusory effects, shapechanges, and into the Ethereal Plane within 30 feet.
Tactics: Erlking's Scouts are methodical and patient. They designate a quarry at the start of combat and pursue that creature until it is down, switching only when directly ordered. They open from range, use Hunter's Arrow to mark their target (denying the hidden condition), then close with Fae Step when the opportunity arises.

### Forest Lord (Fae)
Threat Rating: 4
Size: Large
HP: 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
DR: 4 (bark-like skin)
Speed: 40 ft
Attributes: Str 6 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 4 / Int 6 / Wis 7 / Cha 6 / Luck 5
Skills: Melee Combat 6, Perception 7, Wilderness 7, Intimidate 5, Empathy 5
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Low-Light Vision, Truesight 60 ft, Tremorsense 120 ft (through roots and soil)
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Fae (Fortune on saves vs charm effects; immune to mind-affecting effects from non-Fae sources; does not age)
Attacks:
  - Branch Slam [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 15 ft
    - Margin 1: 12 damage (Large, two-handed natural weapon: 10 + 2)
    - Margin 2: 18 damage (12 + 6 Str); target is knocked Prone
    - Margin 3: 18 damage; target is knocked Prone and Restrained by animate roots until they succeed on an Athletics check (Hard task, 2 successes)
Multiattack [Combat]: The Forest Lord makes two Branch Slam attacks. Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 4).
Special Abilities:
  - Forest Domain: In natural terrain, the Forest Lord can communicate with all plants and beasts within 1 mile. At will, it can cause roots and vines to animate in a 30-foot diameter, making the area Difficult Terrain for all creatures it has not blessed.
  - Verdant Aura: Allies designated by the Forest Lord within 30 feet regain 4 HP at the start of their turns. This includes the summoner.
  - Ancient Authority: Once per encounter as a [Combat] action, the Forest Lord addresses all creatures within 60 feet. Each creature that can hear it makes a Will save (opposed by Wis 7 + Empathy 5). Those that fail become Charmed for 1 minute, treating the Forest Lord as a trusted authority.
  - Resilient Defense (3/day): When the Forest Lord fails a saving throw, it may choose to succeed instead.
Tactics: Forest Lords do not fight like soldiers. They reshape the battlefield, animate terrain, and compel those who oppose them to reconsider. A Friendly Forest Lord is a genuine force multiplier that will protect the summoner intelligently. Even a Cooperative one follows clear instructions well, though it will add editorial judgments about approach.

### Stone Kin (Earth Nephilim)
Threat Rating: 1/2
Size: Large
HP: 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
DR: 3 (rough stone hide)
Speed: 30 ft
Attributes: Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 4, Might 4, Perception 2
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft
Initiative Bonus: +2 (Agi 2)
Creature Type: Nephilim (Large size, Powerful Build; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Slam [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 10 damage (Large, standard natural weapon: 8 + 2)
    - Margin 2: 15 damage (10 + 5 Str)
  - Rock Throw [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 1), Range: 60/120 ft
    - Margin 1: 8 damage
    - Margin 2: 10 damage (8 + 2 Dex)
Special Abilities:
  - Powerful Build: Counts as Huge for carrying, pushing, dragging, and lifting.
  - Earth Bond: The Stone Kin regenerates 4 HP at the start of its turn while standing on natural earth or stone. This regeneration is suppressed if it was hit by magical damage this round.
Tactics: Stone Kin are straightforward. They slam things, throw rocks at things that flee, and regenerate. A summoner looking for a simple frontline blocker will find them adequate. They follow instructions as long as those instructions involve hitting something or standing somewhere.

### Ashwalker (Fire Nephilim)
Threat Rating: 1
Size: Large
HP: 40 (Con 5 × 8, Standard)
DR: 2 (heat-hardened skin)
Speed: 35 ft
Attributes: Str 5 / Con 5 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Intimidate 4, Perception 3
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Nephilim (Large size, Powerful Build; immune to fire damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Burning Fist [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 10 damage (Large, standard natural) + 4 fire damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 15 damage (10 + 5 Str) + 4 fire damage; target gains Singed condition
    - Margin 3: 15 damage + 4 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition
Special Abilities:
  - Immolation Aura: Creatures that start their turn within 5 feet of the Ashwalker take 4 fire damage (Half DR).
  - Fire Immunity.
  - Powerful Build.
Tactics: Ashwalkers stride into melee and let their aura do supplementary work while their fists deliver the primary punishment. They enjoy fighting and will pursue routed enemies without prompting, which is either useful or a problem depending on the circumstance.

### Tempest Giant (Air Nephilim)
Threat Rating: 3
Size: Huge
HP: 144 (Con 6 × 24, Tough)
DR: 2 (wind dispersal)
Speed: 40 ft, Fly 60 ft (Hover)
Attributes: Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 4 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 6, Ranged Combat 5, Perception 5, Intimidate 5
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 30 ft
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Nephilim (Huge size, Powerful Build; immune to lightning damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Wind-Forged Greatclub [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 15 ft
    - Margin 1: 14 damage (Huge, two-handed: 12 + 2 size; see note) + 8 lightning damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 8 lightning damage; target is pushed 15 feet
    - Margin 3: 21 damage + 8 lightning damage; target pushed 15 feet and knocked Prone
  - Lightning Bolt [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 120 ft, 5-foot-wide line
    - Each creature in line: Margin 1: 28 lightning damage (Half DR); Margin 2: 36 lightning damage
Multiattack [Combat]: The Tempest Giant makes two Greatclub attacks. Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 5).
Special Abilities:
  - Storm Step (Recharge 6-8): As a [Move] action, the Tempest Giant teleports up to 60 feet and arrives in a crack of thunder. All creatures within 10 feet of its arrival point make a Fortitude save (1 success) or be knocked Prone.
  - Powerful Build.
  - Wind Wall (1/day): As 2 [Combat] actions, create a 60-foot-long, 20-foot-high wall of roaring wind that persists for 1 minute. Ranged attacks through the wall add 2 to both dice. Small and Tiny creatures cannot pass through it. The Tempest Giant can dismiss it as a [Free] action.
Tactics: Tempest Giants open with Lightning Bolt to soften clustered enemies, then close to melee using Storm Step to arrive at the perfect angle. They maintain Multiattack against priority targets while using Wind Wall to close off avenues the enemy would use to support each other.

### Lantern Archon (Celestial)
Threat Rating: 1/4
Size: Tiny
HP: 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
DR: 2 (divine resilience)
Speed: 0 ft, Fly 60 ft (Hover)
Attributes: Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 5 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
Skills: Perception 4, Religion 3, Melee Combat 1
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Truesight 30 ft
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Outsider/Celestial (immune to poison, disease, fear; Fortune on saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Light Ray [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 30 ft
    - Margin 1: 4 Positive damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 8 Positive damage (Half DR); undead and fiends take double damage
Special Abilities:
  - Continual Flame: Sheds bright light in a 20-foot radius. This light suppresses magical darkness of equal or lower energy cost.
  - Detect Evil: The Archon automatically senses creatures with malicious intent within 60 feet. It communicates this information to the summoner as a [Free] action.
  - Aura of Courage: Allies within 10 feet of the Archon subtract 1 from both dice on saves against the Frightened condition.
  - Diminutive Target: Attacks against the Archon add 1 to both dice due to its tiny size.
Tactics: Lantern Archons support and illuminate rather than fight. They position to maximize their Aura of Courage benefit, report detected threats, and pepper resistant enemies with Light Ray. Against undead they are considerably more dangerous. They will refuse to enter areas where they would be asked to assist with anything they perceive as unjust.

### Hound Archon (Celestial)
Threat Rating: 1
Size: Medium
HP: 40 (Con 5 × 8, Standard)
DR: S: 4, P: 4, B: 3 (divine plate)
Speed: 40 ft
Attributes: Str 5 / Con 5 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 4 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Perception 5, Athletics 4, Intimidate 3, Religion 3
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Truesight 30 ft, Keen Hearing and Smell
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Outsider/Celestial (immune to poison, disease, fear; Fortune on saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Holy Sword [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 8 damage + 4 Positive damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 12 damage (8 + 4... using Int/Wis-based bonus: 8 + 4 Positive = 12) + 4 Positive damage; undead and fiends gain Frightened condition
    - Margin 3: 12 damage + 4 Positive damage; condition applies with no save
  - Bite [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 6 damage (standard natural weapon)
    - Margin 2: 11 damage (6 + 5 Str)
Multiattack [Combat]: The Hound Archon makes one Sword attack and one Bite. Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 4).
Special Abilities:
  - Change Shape: The Hound Archon can assume the form of any Medium humanoid as a [Interact] action. Its stats do not change; the form is cosmetic only.
  - Magic Circle: Once per encounter, the Hound Archon can establish a 10-foot diameter zone of protection centered on a point within 30 feet. Fiends and corrupted creatures cannot enter this zone and cannot charm, frighten, or possess creatures within it. Duration 10 minutes.
Tactics: Hound Archons are guardians first. They position to protect the summoner and designated allies, using Magic Circle to establish a safe zone when under pressure. They engage threats directly with their multiattack, prioritizing undead and fiends. They can disguise themselves to blend into a crowd if needed for a protection mission.

### Solar Aspect (Celestial)
Threat Rating: 4
Size: Large
HP: 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
DR: 6 (celestial armor)
Speed: 50 ft, Fly 100 ft (Hover)
Attributes: Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 6 / Dex 5 / Int 7 / Wis 8 / Cha 7 / Luck 6
Skills: Melee Combat 7, Ranged Combat 6, Perception 8, Religion 8
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 120 ft
Initiative Bonus: +6 (Agi 6)
Creature Type: Outsider/Celestial (immune to poison, disease, fear, charm, necrotic damage; immune to non-magical weapons; Fortune on all saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Radiant Greatsword [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 16 damage + 16 Positive damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 23 damage (16 + 7 Str) + 16 Positive damage; fiends and corrupted creatures make a Will save or become Blinded until end of their next turn
    - Margin 3: 23 damage + 16 Positive damage; Blinded condition, no save
  - Radiant Arrow [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 6), Range: 120 ft
    - Margin 1: 12 damage + 12 Positive damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 17 damage + 12 Positive damage; target is Revealed (cannot gain Invisible, Hidden, or Concealed) for 1 minute
Multiattack [Combat]: Two Radiant Greatsword attacks or two Radiant Arrows. Shared Attribute Roll.
Special Abilities:
  - Blinding Presence: Fiends and corrupted creatures that begin their turn within 30 feet make a Fortitude save (1 success) or gain the Dazzled condition until they move out of range.
  - Divine Awareness: Cannot be surprised. Knows the nature and intent of any creature within 60 feet.
  - Empower Good (1/day): As 2 [Combat] actions, all allies within 60 feet gain temporary HP equal to 40 and Fortune on all attack rolls and saves for 1 minute.
  - Resilient Defense (3/day).
  - Celestial Compact: A Solar Aspect will not arrive for a Summoner it judges to be acting in bad faith. This is a purely GM determination — a Solar Aspect called by a character who has recently committed serious moral wrongs arrives only at Indifferent regardless of targeting roll, and may use its Divine Awareness to announce its assessment to the party before deciding whether to cooperate.
Tactics: Solar Aspects fight with authority and precision. Empower Good goes up first when allies need it; otherwise they alternate between suppressing the most dangerous enemy with Radiant Greatsword and denying concealment with Radiant Arrows. Their Blinding Presence passively disrupts fiends and corrupted opponents throughout the fight.

### Imp (Fiend)
Threat Rating: 1/4
Size: Tiny
HP: 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
DR: 2 (scaled skin)
Speed: 20 ft, Fly 40 ft
Attributes: Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 5 / Int 5 / Wis 3 / Cha 4 / Luck 3
Skills: Stealth 5, Deception 4, Perception 3, Melee Combat 2
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 20 ft
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Outsider/Fiend (resistant to fire, cold, lightning damage (+2 DR); immune to poison, Poisoned condition; Fortune on saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Sting [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 3 damage + Fortitude save (1 success) or Poisoned (Weak) for 1 minute
    - Margin 2: 4 damage (3 + 1 Str... effectively minimum) + Fortitude save or Poisoned (Strong) for 1 minute
Special Abilities:
  - Invisibility (At-Will): Imp can become invisible as a [Minor] action. Ends if it attacks.
  - Change Shape: Can assume the form of a small beast (rat, raven, spider) as a [Interact] action.
  - Devil's Sight: Sees through magical darkness.
  - Pocket Fiend: Imps are frequently used as spies and familiars by casters of dark intent. A Cooperative Imp will gather information reliably, though it exaggerates its own contribution significantly when reporting back.
Tactics: Imps avoid combat. They spy, report, and sting when they have an overwhelming advantage. A Summoner who treats an Imp like a combat asset will be disappointed; one who treats it like an intelligence resource will get more than expected, though the information will always have a slight self-serving editorial slant.

### Shadow Hound (Fiend)
Threat Rating: 1/2
Size: Medium
HP: 27 (Con 3 × 9, Tough)
DR: 0
Speed: 40 ft
Attributes: Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 6 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 4 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Stealth 5, Perception 4
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight (sees through magical darkness)
Initiative Bonus: +6 (Agi 6)
Creature Type: Outsider/Fiend (resistant to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR); immune to Poisoned, poison damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Bite [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 6 damage + 4 Negative damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 10 damage (6 + 4 Str) + 4 Negative damage; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains Weakened condition until end of their next turn
    - Margin 3: 10 damage + 4 Negative damage; Weakened condition, no save
Special Abilities:
  - Shadow Meld: In dim light or darkness, the Shadow Hound has Fortune on Stealth checks and attacks against it add 1 to both dice.
  - Pack Hunt: When an ally is within 5 feet of the target, the Shadow Hound subtracts 1 from both attack dice.
  - Death Sense: The Shadow Hound automatically detects creatures below half HP within 60 feet.
Tactics: Shadow Hounds hunt. They use Death Sense to identify the most vulnerable target, Shadow Meld to approach unseen, and converge on weakened enemies. They ignore the summoner's allies unless those allies attack them, instinctively prioritizing wounded prey. This is their nature and not something negotiable.

### Bone Devil (Fiend)
Threat Rating: 2
Size: Large
HP: 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
DR: 4 (bone armor)
Speed: 40 ft, Fly 40 ft
Attributes: Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 5 / Wis 4 / Cha 5 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Perception 5, Deception 5, Intimidate 5
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight, Truesight 30 ft
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Outsider/Fiend (resistant to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR); immune to poison, Poisoned condition; Fortune on saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Claw [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 10 damage (Large, standard natural)
    - Margin 2: 15 damage (10 + 5 Str)
  - Tail Sting [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 8 damage + Fortitude save (1 success) or Poisoned (Strong)
    - Margin 2: 8 damage + Poisoned (Strong) (no save) + Weakened condition for 1 minute
Multiattack [Combat]: The Bone Devil makes two Claw attacks and one Tail Sting. Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 4).
Special Abilities:
  - Fear Aura: Creatures within 10 feet that are not Fiends make a Will save at the start of their turn (1 success). On failure, they gain the Frightened condition until they succeed. Creatures immune to fear or charm are unaffected.
  - Wall of Ice (1/day): As 2 [Combat] actions, create a 60-foot-long, 20-foot-high wall of ice. Each section has HP 20 and DR 4. Duration until destroyed.
Tactics: Bone Devils are commanders and negotiators — they spend the first round assessing before fully committing. Fear Aura keeps weaker enemies at a distance while they use Multiattack on primary threats. A Bone Devil that has agreed to terms will execute those terms with precision and will always point out when you could have asked for more.

### Pit Fiend (Fiend)
Threat Rating: 5
Size: Large
HP: 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
DR: 6 (infernal hide)
Speed: 30 ft, Fly 60 ft
Attributes: Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 4 / Int 7 / Wis 6 / Cha 7 / Luck 5
Skills: Melee Combat 7, Perception 7, Deception 7, Intimidate 7
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 120 ft, Devil's Sight
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Outsider/Fiend (immune to fire and Negative damage; resistant to cold, lightning (+4 DR); immune to poison, Poisoned, Charmed, Frightened; Fortune on all saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Crushing Fist [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 10 ft
    - Margin 1: 14 damage (Large heavy natural: 12 + 2)
    - Margin 2: 22 damage (14 + 8 Str); target makes Fortitude save or is Grappled
    - Margin 3: 22 damage; target Grappled and Restrained (no save)
  - Hellfire [Combat]: Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 120 ft, 20-foot diameter
    - Each creature in area: Margin 1: 20 fire damage; Margin 2: 40 fire damage + Ignited condition; Half DR applies
Multiattack [Combat]: The Pit Fiend makes two Crushing Fist attacks or two Hellfire attacks. Shared Attribute Roll.
Special Abilities:
  - Infernal Command: The Pit Fiend can issue commands to any Fiend of lower TR within 300 feet as a [Free] action. Those Fiends must succeed on a Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) to refuse. If other Fiends are present on the battlefield from any source, they must make this save or follow the Pit Fiend's orders.
  - Regeneration 10: The Pit Fiend regains 10 HP at the start of its turn unless it took Positive damage this round.
  - Fear Presence: All non-Fiend creatures within 60 feet make a Will save at the start of combat (1 success). Failure: Frightened for 1 minute. Success: Immune to this Pit Fiend's Fear Presence for 24 hours.
  - Resilient Defense (3/day).
  - Binding Contract: Any Pit Fiend that agrees to be summoned expects something in return. This is a GM narrative element, not a mechanical one — but the Pit Fiend will not forget.
Tactics: A Pit Fiend enters a battle and immediately establishes hierarchy. Infernal Command suppresses any other Fiend present. Fear Presence scatters weaker opponents. It uses Hellfire on grouped enemies and Crushing Fists to control priority targets. A Summoner who has negotiated clearly will find it an extraordinarily capable ally. A Summoner who assumed good faith will find the agreement technically honored in ways they did not intend.

### Shadow (Shadow)
Threat Rating: 1/4
Size: Medium
HP: 16 (Con 2 × 8, Standard)
DR: 0 (but see Shadow Form)
Speed: 40 ft
Attributes: Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 3, Stealth 6, Perception 3
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Undead/Shadow Plane (immune to poison, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion; vulnerable to Positive damage; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Strength Drain [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 4 Negative damage (Ignore DR) + target's Strength reduced by 1 for 1 hour
    - Margin 2: 4 Negative damage + Strength reduced by 2 for 1 hour + target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains the Weakened condition
Special Abilities:
  - Shadow Form: While in dim light or darkness, the Shadow has DR 8 against all non-magical damage. Positive-energy damage ignores this entirely.
  - Amorphous: The Shadow can move through a space as narrow as 1 inch.
  - Sunlight Weakness: In bright light, the Shadow has Misfortune on all rolls.
  - Shadow Spawn: If a non-undead creature is killed by Strength Drain-induced Strength reduction (Strength reduced to 0), it rises as a Shadow under the controlling summoner's influence at the start of its next turn.
Tactics: Shadows avoid bright light and exploit dim areas. They stack Strength Drain against a single target, attempting to reduce them to 0 Strength. A Summoner who calls one should be prepared for it to ignore tactical nuance in favor of finding the darkest spot in the room and hunting from there.

### Shade Walker (Shadow)
Threat Rating: 1
Size: Medium
HP: 32 (Con 4 × 8, Standard)
DR: 2 (shadow substance)
Speed: 40 ft, Climb 40 ft
Attributes: Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 5, Stealth 6, Perception 4, Deception 3
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, See Invisibility
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Shadow Plane (immune to poison, Poisoned; resistant to cold damage (+2 DR); does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Shadow Strike [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 8 damage + 4 Negative damage (Ignore DR)
    - Margin 2: 12 damage (8 + 4 Str) + 4 Negative damage; target is Disoriented until start of their next turn (shadow obscures their vision)
    - Margin 3: 12 damage + 4 Negative damage; target Disoriented and loses the Hidden condition if they had it
Special Abilities:
  - Shadow Meld: In dim light or darkness, the Shade Walker has Fortune on Stealth. Attacks against it add 1 to both dice.
  - Planar Step (1/short rest): As a [Move] action, the Shade Walker steps briefly into the Shadow Plane and re-emerges up to 30 feet away in any dim or dark location it can see. This movement does not provoke opportunity attacks.
  - Sunlight Sensitivity: In bright light, the Shade Walker adds 1 to both attack dice.
Tactics: Shade Walkers are assassins. They use Planar Step to close distance, strike from darkness, and retreat before retaliation. A Cooperative Shade Walker follows target priority without complaint. An Indifferent one picks whoever is standing in the most shadow.

### Nightmare (Shadow)
Threat Rating: 2
Size: Large
HP: 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
DR: 2
Speed: 60 ft, Fly 90 ft
Attributes: Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 4 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 6, Perception 4, Intimidate 4, Athletics 4
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Devil's Sight
Initiative Bonus: +5 (Agi 5)
Creature Type: Shadow Plane (immune to poison, Poisoned, Frightened; resistant to fire (+2 DR); does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Flaming Hooves [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 12 damage (Large, standard natural) + 4 fire damage (Half DR)
    - Margin 2: 18 damage (12 + 6 Str) + 4 fire damage; target knocked Prone
    - Margin 3: 18 damage + 4 fire damage; target Prone and Stunned until end of their next turn (hoof strike to the head)
Special Abilities:
  - Ethereal Stride (1/day): The Nightmare can carry up to 3 riders into the Ethereal Plane for up to 1 hour, moving through solid objects during transit. It must return to the material plane within the duration or the effect ends suddenly and all passengers are ejected.
  - Smoke: The Nightmare's flaming hooves generate a thick smoke trail when running at full speed (40+ feet moved in a turn). The trail persists for 1 minute and creates a 10-foot-wide path of Difficult Terrain and heavy obscurement.
  - Terror Mount: A rider on a Nightmare adds 2 to both dice on Intimidate checks while mounted.
Tactics: Nightmares are mounts first and combatants second. In combat without a rider, they rear and strike with their hooves, using their speed to break through formations. As a summoner's mount they are exceptional — fast, terrifying, and capable of brief planar transit. A Cooperative Nightmare will carry the summoner wherever they indicate; an Indifferent one runs toward whatever frightens it least and expects to be chased.

### Gibbering Mouther (Aberration)
Threat Rating: 1/2
Size: Medium
HP: 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
DR: 0
