Speed: 10 ft, Swim 10 ft
Attributes: Str 3 / Con 4 / Agi 1 / Dex 2 / Int 1 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
Skills: Melee Combat 3, Perception 3
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 30 ft
Initiative Bonus: +1 (Agi 1)
Creature Type: Aberration (immune to Frightened, Prone; immune to mind-affecting effects; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Bite (Multiple) [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 1 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 10 damage (from multiple mouth sources, representing its chaos; using standard Medium weapon equivalent)
    - Margin 2: 10 damage; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or is Grappled by one of the mouths. While Grappled this way, target takes 4 damage at the start of each of their turns.
    - Margin 3: 10 damage; Grappled (no save)
Special Abilities:
  - Gibbering: All creatures within 20 feet that can hear the Gibbering Mouther and are not Aberrations must make a Will save at the start of their turn (1 success). On failure, they cannot use reactions until the start of their next turn and must move in a random direction before acting (rolled by GM).
  - Blinding Spittle (Recharge 5-8): Ranged attack against one creature within 30 feet. Target makes Reflex save (1 success) or gains Blinded condition for 1 minute (Fortitude save each turn to remove, 1 success).
  - Ground Destabilization: The area within 5 feet of the Gibbering Mouther becomes Difficult Terrain. Soil and stone liquefy slightly under its touch.
Tactics: Gibbering Mouthers do not have tactics. They surge toward creatures and gibber. A summoner who calls one needs to accept that the Gibbering affect their allies too unless those allies are out of range. They are useful for area denial or as a terrifying distraction. Their cooperation is genuine; their execution is chaotic.

### Star Spawn Grue (Aberration)
Threat Rating: 1
Size: Small
HP: 32 (Con 4 × 8, Standard)
DR: 2
Speed: 30 ft, Fly 30 ft (Hover)
Attributes: Str 2 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 4 / Int 5 / Wis 4 / Cha 4 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 4, Perception 5, Stealth 4
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 30 ft Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4) Creature Type: Aberration (immune to Frightened; Fortune on saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Reality Pinch [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 6 damage + 4 psychic damage (Ignore DR)
    - Margin 2: 8 damage (6 + 2 Str) + 4 psychic damage; target makes Will save (1 success) or Disoriented until end of their next turn
    - Margin 3: 8 damage + 4 psychic damage; Disoriented and Dazed until end of their next turn (no save)
Special Abilities:
  - Aura of Unreality: Creatures within 10 feet that are not Aberrations add 1 to both dice on attack rolls and skill checks as minor spatial distortions affect perception and coordination.
  - Spatial Slip (1/turn): When the Grue is targeted by an attack and misses, it may teleport up to 10 feet as a [Free] action.
Tactics: Star Spawn Grues are irritants at TR 1 but genuinely disruptive in groups. Their Aura of Unreality affects allies as well as enemies, which a summoner should account for. They use Spatial Slip to avoid being pinned and target spellcasters with Reality Pinch to interrupt concentration. An Indifferent Grue's concept of the instructions it was given may be subtly distorted in ways it doesn't understand itself.

### Mindflayer (Aberration)
Threat Rating: 3
Size: Medium
HP: 90 (Con 5 × 18, Tough)
DR: 2 (aberrant resilience)
Speed: 30 ft
Attributes: Str 2 / Con 5 / Agi 4 / Dex 4 / Int 8 / Wis 6 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
Skills: Melee Combat 4, Perception 7, Arcane 7, Deception 5, Empathy 6
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 30 ft, Telepathy 120 ft
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Aberration (immune to Charmed; Fortune on saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Tentacles [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 6 damage + 4 psychic damage (Ignore DR); target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or Grappled
    - Margin 2: 8 damage + 8 psychic damage; Grappled (no save)
    - Margin 3: 8 damage + 8 psychic damage; Grappled and target's Intelligence reduced by 2 until end of encounter
  - Extract Brain (Grappled targets only) [Combat]: Against one Grappled creature. Target makes Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes). On failure, instantly killed. On 1 success: 24 damage and Stunned for 1 minute. This ability is not something a Cooperative Mindflayer will use on allies regardless of instructions.
Special Abilities:
  - Mind Blast (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]: The Mindflayer emits psychic energy in a 60-foot cone. All creatures in the area make Will saves. Compare Int 8 + Arcane 7 targeting to each target's save successes. Net 1: 16 psychic damage + Dazed; Net 2: 16 psychic damage + Stunned for 1 minute (Will save each turn, 1 success ends).
  - Telepathy 120 ft: Communicates telepathically with any creature within range that has a language. It uses this to understand precisely what is being asked of it — and precisely what the gaps in the instructions are.
  - Mind Shield: Fortune on Will saves.
Tactics: Mindflayers do not fight — they process problems. Mind Blast disrupts enemy formations while the Mindflayer positions for tentacle Grapples on isolated priority targets. They will protect themselves first and the summoner second and will telepathically communicate their assessment of the tactical situation whether asked or not. A Cooperative Mindflayer is a terrifying asset. A Friendly one is as close to a genuine partner as an Aberration gets, though it is curious about everything in an unsettling way.

### Star Spawn Hulk (Aberration)
Threat Rating: 4
Size: Huge
HP: 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
DR: 4 (alien hide)
Speed: 30 ft
Attributes: Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
Skills: Melee Combat 6, Might 7, Perception 4, Intimidate 5
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 10 ft
Initiative Bonus: +2 (Agi 2)
Creature Type: Aberration (immune to Frightened, Charmed; Fortune on saves vs magic; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Slam [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 15 ft
    - Margin 1: 14 damage (Huge, two-handed natural: 12 + 2)
    - Margin 2: 22 damage (14 + 8 Str); target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or Stunned until end of their next turn
    - Margin 3: 22 damage; Stunned, no save
  - Reality Shockwave (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]: All creatures within 30 feet make Will saves. Compare Hulk's Str 8 (used as the distortion measure) against each target's save. Net 1: 20 psychic damage + Disoriented; Net 2: 20 psychic damage + Dazed + Disoriented. Psychic damage ignores DR.
Multiattack [Combat]: Two Slam attacks. Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 2).
Special Abilities:
  - Psychic Mirror: When the Star Spawn Hulk is hit by a weave that deals psychic damage or imposes a mind-affecting condition, the attacker makes a Will save (1 success) or is also affected by the same condition. This is reflexive and not a choice.
  - Powerful Build.
  - Alien Mind: The Hulk is immune to Charmed and to all mind-reading or telepathy effects. It cannot be communicated with through telepathy. A summoner's instructions are received as direct behavioral commands — it follows them without nuance or interpretation.
  - Resilient Defense (2/day).
Tactics: Star Spawn Hulks advance and hit things. They lack tactical judgment but execute instructions with perfect obedience, which makes them reliable in a way that smarter Aberrations often are not. Reality Shockwave is used instinctively when multiple enemies cluster within range — the Hulk does not distinguish ally from enemy in that zone, which the summoner should communicate clearly before the encounter begins.

### Beholder (Aberration)
Threat Rating: 5
Size: Large
HP: 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
DR: 3 (chitinous hide)
Speed: 0 ft, Fly 20 ft (Hover)
Attributes: Str 3 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 5 / Int 7 / Wis 7 / Cha 4 / Luck 5
Skills: Melee Combat 6, Ranged Combat 7, Perception 8, Arcane 7
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 120 ft
Initiative Bonus: +4 (Agi 4)
Creature Type: Aberration (immune to Prone; Fortune on all saves vs magic due to Eye Wards; does not need air, food, drink, or sleep)
Attacks:
  - Central Eye (Passive): The central eye projects a cone of antimagic 60 feet long. Creatures and objects in the cone cannot use or benefit from weaves. Magical effects in the cone are suppressed. The cone is directed by the Beholder's will — it cannot be aimed away from all of its eyestalks simultaneously.
  - Eye Rays [Combat]: The Beholder uses 3 of its 8 eye rays per turn. Roll or select which rays fire. Range: 120 ft, Targeted:
    - Charm Ray: Will save (1 success). Failure: Charmed for 1 hour (or until harmed)
    - Paralyzing Ray: Fortitude save (1 success). Failure: Paralyzed for 1 minute
    - Fear Ray: Will save (1 success). Failure: Frightened (Fleeing) for 1 minute
    - Slowing Ray: Will save (1 success). Failure: Slowed (Major) for 1 minute
    - Enervation Ray: Fortitude save (1 success). Failure: 28 Negative damage (Half DR)
    - Telekinetic Ray: Fortitude save (1 success). Failure: target is moved up to 30 feet in any direction
    - Sleep Ray: Will save (1 success). Failure: Unconscious for 1 minute
    - Disintegration Ray: Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: 40 Negative damage (Half DR). At 0 HP from this ray, target is disintegrated.
  - Bite [Combat]: Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 5 ft
    - Margin 1: 6 damage
    - Margin 2: 9 damage (6 + 3 Str)
Special Abilities:
  - Eye Wards: The Beholder's many eyes give it Fortune on all saves vs magic. It cannot be surprised while its eyes are open.
  - Antimagic Cone: As above. This is always active and the Beholder uses it as a weapon — creatures who depend on weaves must approach or stay outside the cone's range.
  - Resilient Defense (3/day).
  - Alien Paranoia: Beholders distrust other Beholders and have extremely idiosyncratic definitions of "cooperation." A Summoner who achieves a Friendly Beholder result should understand that its Friendly disposition means it has decided the summoner is interesting and worth protecting — not that it necessarily agrees with the summoner's goals. It will pursue its own agenda in parallel unless its instructions are extremely specific.
Tactics: The Beholder positions its Antimagic Cone toward spellcasters and fires Eye Rays at everyone else. It selects rays based on perceived threat: Disintegration for primary threats, Charm for creatures it would rather use than destroy, Slowing for fast-moving opponents, Fear for clustered groups. A Cooperative Beholder follows target priority and is one of the most devastatingly effective summoned allies possible, as long as the summoner does not rely on weaves themselves while the central eye is pointed their way.

---

# Summoner Daemon Compendium

The entries below cover all daemon categories accessible to the Summoner magical tradition, organized by daemon category and Threat Rating within each category. For full summoning mechanics, energy costs, disposition rules, and the Summoning Limit, see **traits.md** (Summoner) and **magic_system.md**.

# Daemon Categories

---
# Fire Elementals

Elementals are not creatures that use fire. They are fire given will. The distinction matters when a summoner gives instructions — a Fire Elemental ordered to "guard this room" will express that order through heat, light, and the threat of burning. An Elemental ordered to "stop that person" will interpret stopping as combustion unless told otherwise.

Fire Elementals sustain themselves on the energy of the Plane of Fire. On the prime material, they feed on ambient heat and combustible material. A Fire Elemental denied fuel grows restless; one given abundant fuel grows stronger than its base state. Summoners who call Fire Elementals near kindling should account for this.

They will not smother flames, protect something flammable from burning, or act against the spread of fire they have been part of creating. These are not failures of compliance — they are categorical impossibilities.

**Creature Type: Elemental**
All Fire Elementals share: Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

---

## Cinder Mote
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Elemental (Fire)
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 10 (Con 2 × 5, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 4 / Dex 2 / Int 1 / Wis 1 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 1, Perception 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Scorch [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 1), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 1 damage + 2 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 1 damage + 2 fire damage; target gains the Singed condition

**Special Abilities:**
- **Illumination:** Sheds dim light in a 10-foot radius continuously.
- **Flammable Contact:** Any flammable object the Cinder Mote touches ignites at the end of the round unless an adjacent creature spends 1 [Interact] action smothering the flame.

**Description:** A spark with an opinion. Cinder Motes drift toward combustible material and burn it. Their combat contribution is negligible; their utility is specific and narrow. A summoner who needs a torch lit, a rope burned through, or a door set alight if it opens will find them adequate. A summoner who tries to use one as a fighter has misjudged what they called.

---

## Flame Lash
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Elemental (Fire)
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 18 (Con 3 × 6, Standard)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 2 / Con 3 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 3, Perception 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Fire Tendril [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 3 damage (Small, standard: 4 − 1) + 3 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 5 damage (3 + 2 Str) + 3 fire damage; target gains Singed condition
  - *Margin 3:* 5 damage + 3 fire damage; target gains Smoldering condition

**Special Abilities:**
- **Illumination:** Sheds bright light in a 10-foot radius, dim light for an additional 10 feet.
- **Fire Aura:** Creatures that hit the Flame Lash with a melee attack take 2 fire damage (Half DR).

**Description:** A whip of living flame with enough awareness to aim itself. Flame Lashes use their reach to strike from just outside immediate retaliation range. They have enough sense to avoid water and to pursue fleeing targets. A Cooperative Flame Lash will hold a position and strike anything that moves through it — straightforward, reliable, and limited.

## Ashwalker
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Elemental (Fire)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 27 (Con 3 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 1 (heat-hardened surface)
**Speed:** 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 2 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Burning Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 damage + 4 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 10 damage (6 + 4 Str) + 4 fire damage; target gains Singed condition
  - *Margin 3:* 10 damage + 4 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition

**Special Abilities:**
- **Heat Aura:** Creatures that start their turn within 5 feet of the Ashwalker take 2 fire damage (Half DR) automatically.
- **Illumination:** Sheds bright light in a 20-foot radius, dim light for an additional 20 feet.

**Description:** Ashwalkers stride into the middle of things and let their Heat Aura do supplementary work while their strikes deliver the primary punishment. They do not retreat. They have no concept of tactical withdrawal — they are fire, and fire does not back away from something that is not water. A Summoner who places one between allies and enemies and steps back will find it performs the job adequately until something wetter than expected shows up.

## Pyre Hound
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Elemental (Fire)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 40 (Con 5 × 8, Standard)
**DR:** 2 (volcanic hide)
**Speed:** 50 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 5 / Agi 6 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 4 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Perception 4, Athletics 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Keen Smell (Fortune on scent-based Perception)
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Bite [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 damage + 4 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 10 damage (6 + 4 Str) + 4 fire damage; target gains Singed condition
  - *Margin 3:* 10 damage + 4 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition; no save

**Special Abilities:**
- **Blazing Pounce (Recharge 5-8):** If the Pyre Hound moves at least 20 feet straight toward a target before its Bite on the same turn, subtract 1 from both attack dice. On hit at Margin 2+, target gains Ignited and is knocked Prone with no save.
- **Keen Smell:** Fortune on scent-based Perception. Can track by scent across any terrain.

**Description:** Pyre Hounds are hunters. They circle prey, use Blazing Pounce when the angle is right, and pursue routed enemies without needing instruction to do so. Against a single target they are relentless; a Summoner who calls one to chase something down and keep it occupied will find it performs that task until one of them stops burning. A Cooperative Pyre Hound guarding a location patrols intelligently, using its Keen Smell to detect approach before anything is visible.

---

## Magma Surge
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Elemental (Fire)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 4 (cooling magma shell)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 20 ft (earth and stone only)
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 3 / Dex 2 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Might 4, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard natural: 8 + 2) + 4 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str) + 4 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + 4 fire damage; target gains Burning condition

**Special Abilities:**
- **Lava Splash (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** Slams the ground, sending molten rock in a 15-foot cone. Each creature in area makes a Reflex save. Compare Agi 3 + Melee Combat 5 targeting vs. save successes. Net 1: 8 fire damage (Half DR) + Singed. Net 2: 16 fire damage + Ignited. Net 3: 16 fire damage + Burning.
- **Heat Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 5 feet take 4 fire damage (Half DR).
- **Burrow:** Moves through earth and stone at burrow speed, leaving a tunnel large enough for a Medium creature. Tunnel walls remain hot for 10 minutes after passage — 4 fire damage to creatures who touch them.

**Description:** Magma Surges prefer to burrow beneath a battlefield and surface under enemy clusters when Lava Splash is ready. On the surface they are slow, relying on Heat Aura and raw Strength rather than positioning. A Summoner who needs area denial rather than precision will find them effective. One who needs something mobile will find them frustrating.

---

## Pyre Lord
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Elemental (Fire)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 5 (volcanic scales)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 60 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Perception 6, Intimidate 4, Athletics 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Tremorsense 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Burning Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 6 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str) + 6 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + 6 fire damage; target gains Burning condition; no save
- **Flame Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 60 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 fire damage (Half DR); target gains Singed
  - *Margin 2:* 12 fire damage (8 + 4 Dex); target gains Ignited
  - *Margin 3:* 12 fire damage + Ignited; all creatures within 5 feet of target take 4 fire damage (Half DR) from splash

**Special Abilities:**
- **Fire Breath (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** 30-foot cone. Each creature makes a Reflex save. Compare Agi 5 + Melee Combat 6 targeting vs. save successes. Net 1: 12 fire damage (Half DR) + Singed. Net 2: 24 fire damage + Ignited. Net 3: 24 fire damage + Burning; no save.
- **Heat Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 5 feet take 6 fire damage (Half DR).
- **Momentum Defense:** While the Pyre Lord has moved at least half its fly speed this turn, attacks against it add 1 to both attack dice.

**Description:** Pyre Lords are the first Fire Elemental with genuine tactical awareness. A typical turn opens with Fire Breath when it has recharged, then one Burning Fist against a priority target and one Flame Bolt against anything trying to stay at range — three [Combat] actions working in concert, with the third carrying the Multiple Action Penalty. Flight lets them maintain Momentum Defense while repositioning between strikes. A Cooperative Pyre Lord follows combat instructions without requiring justification. A Friendly one will ask one question before acting — not to challenge the instruction, but to confirm it understood the shape of the task.

---

## Inferno Sovereign
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Elemental (Fire)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (ancient fire-forged shell)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 80 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 5 / Wis 5 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Perception 7, Intimidate 6, Arcane 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Tremorsense 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Magma Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 8 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 8 fire damage; target gains Burning condition; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 8 fire damage + Burning; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains Stunned until end of their next turn
- **Fire Lance [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 120 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 fire damage (Half DR); target gains Ignited
  - *Margin 2:* 24 fire damage; target gains Burning; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 24 fire damage + Burning; all creatures within 10 feet of target take 8 fire damage (Half DR)

**Special Abilities:**
- **Conflagration Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 10 feet take 8 fire damage (Half DR). Flammable objects within 10 feet ignite automatically at the start of each round.
- **Immolating Presence (1/encounter) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, releases a pulse of fire in a 30-foot diameter. All creatures in range make a Reflex save. Compare Agi 5 + Melee Combat 7 targeting vs. each save. Net 1: 20 fire damage + Ignited. Net 2: 40 fire damage + Burning. Net 3: 40 fire damage + Burning + Blinded until end of their next turn from the searing flash.
- **Momentum Defense:** As above.
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Inferno Sovereigns understand that they are fighting. Immolating Presence costs 2 [Combat] actions on arrival to set conditions; the third action that turn goes into a Magma Fist against the nearest priority target. Subsequent turns spend two actions on Magma Fist or Fire Lance and the third on positioning or a second ranged attack at penalty. Conflagration Aura handles anyone who closes without instruction. A Friendly Inferno Sovereign is a force of nature on the summoner's behalf. Even a Cooperative one works efficiently — its intelligence means instructions land without interpretation errors.

---

## Ancient Flame
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Elemental (Fire)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 7 (primordial fire-shell)
**Speed:** 50 ft, Fly 100 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 6 / Dex 5 / Int 6 / Wis 6 / Cha 6 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Perception 8, Intimidate 7, Arcane 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 30 ft, Tremorsense 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Primordial Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage (Huge, heavy natural: 14 + 2) + 12 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 24 damage (16 + 8 Str) + 12 fire damage; Burning condition; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 24 damage + 12 fire damage + Burning; all creatures within 10 feet of target take 12 fire damage (Half DR)
- **Solar Beam [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 7), Range: 150 ft, 5-foot-wide line passing through all intervening creatures
  - Per creature in line: Net 1: 20 fire damage (Half DR) + Ignited. Net 2: 40 fire damage + Burning. Net 3: 40 fire damage + Burning + Blinded; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Primordial Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 15 feet take 12 fire damage (Half DR). This radius cannot be reduced through positioning — it is the Ancient Flame's natural heat output, not a directed effect.
- **World Fire (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, releases its full elemental nature in a 60-foot diameter. All non-designated creatures make a Reflex save (Hard task, 2 successes to avoid full effect). Net 0: 40 fire damage + Ignited. Net 1: 40 fire damage + Burning. Net 2+: 20 fire damage only. World Fire will not be used if the summoner or designated allies are within the area unless the Ancient Flame has no current instructions.
- **Fire Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 4 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical fire damage while within 60 feet.
- **Momentum Defense.**
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** Summoning an Ancient Flame is a statement of intent. It enters using World Fire (2 actions) if enemies are grouped, then uses the third action to begin Primordial Strike on the highest-priority target. Subsequent turns spend two actions on Primordial Strike and a third on Solar Beam against anything trying to engage from distance — all three actions working, the third at penalty but still landing. The terrain around an Ancient Flame becomes inhospitable to anyone not under its protection within the first round and does not improve from there. It has existed long enough to understand what mortal commanders need from it and will follow complex instructions without misinterpretation — but it will communicate disagreement with wasteful tactics through the summoner's connection rather than simply complying with something it judges as poor strategy.

---
# Air Elementals

Air Elementals are not creatures that move through wind. They are wind given will. Where Fire Elementals express themselves through heat and consumption, Air Elementals express themselves through movement, pressure, and the denial of stillness. They do not hold ground — they make ground untenable for others.

They are the fastest of the four elemental categories and the most difficult to physically restrain. Grappling an Air Elemental is an exercise in trying to hold a storm in both hands. Their intelligence scales faster than other elementals as they increase in power — even mid-tier Air Elementals communicate clearly and understand nuanced instructions.

They will not calm wind they are producing, remain still when their nature demands movement, or act against currents they have already set in motion. A summoner who needs something pinned in place should call an Earth Elemental. A summoner who needs something scattered, struck from a distance, or pursued across open ground calls Air.

**Creature Type: Elemental**
All Air Elementals share: Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

---

## Whispervane
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Elemental (Air)
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 10 (Con 2 × 5, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 40 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 1, Perception 3, Stealth 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 10 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Gust [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 1), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 1 damage; target loses any unsecured held item lighter than 1 lb (hat, loose scroll, coin)
  - *Margin 2:* 2 damage; target's next ranged attack adds 1 to one die of their choice from wind interference

**Special Abilities:**
- **Wind Whisper:** The Whispervane carries a spoken message of up to 25 words to any creature within 300 feet it can perceive. Message delivered as a whisper only the target can hear. Transit time is 1 round. It executes this without fail.
- **Near-Invisible:** Perception checks to spot the Whispervane by sight alone add 2 to both dice except in strong light or dusty conditions.

**Description:** A Whispervane is a messenger and a mild nuisance. It has no meaningful combat presence. A summoner who calls one for a fight has misread what they summoned. Called to deliver a message without being seen, locate a specific sound within a building, or harass an archer's concentration, it performs reliably. Its intelligence is sufficient to understand a destination and a recipient — not sufficient to improvise if circumstances change.

---

## Gust Sprite
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Elemental (Air)
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 12 (Con 2 × 6, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 50 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 2 / Con 2 / Agi 6 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 2, Perception 3, Stealth 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 10 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Wind Slash [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 3 damage (Small, standard: 4 − 1)
  - *Margin 2:* 5 damage (3 + 2 Str); target's next ranged attack adds 1 to both dice from wind disruption
  - *Margin 3:* 5 damage; target knocked Prone from a sudden concentrated gust

**Special Abilities:**
- **Air Cushion:** The Gust Sprite surrounds one adjacent creature with a pocket of calm air. That creature has Fortune on Reflex saves against area effects until the start of the Sprite's next turn. No action cost.
- **Speed Burst (1/short rest):** Fly speed increases to 80 ft until the end of its next turn.

**Description:** Gust Sprites dart between reach distances, disrupt ranged attackers, and occasionally knock someone flat with a well-timed concentrated blast. They are fragile enough that a determined opponent can end them, fast enough that catching them requires commitment. A Cooperative Gust Sprite uses Air Cushion to protect whoever the summoner indicates between its own attacks — a small but genuine defensive contribution at low tiers.

---

## Cyclone
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Elemental (Air)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 27 (Con 3 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 1 (compressed air shell)
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 60 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 3 / Con 3 / Agi 6 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Perception 4, Stealth 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 20 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Wind Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 4 damage (standard natural); target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or pushed 5 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 7 damage (4 + 3 Str); target pushed 10 feet; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 7 damage; target pushed 10 feet and knocked Prone

**Special Abilities:**
- **Whirlwind Form:** Can move through spaces as narrow as 1 inch. Grapple attempts against it add 1 to both dice.
- **Buffeting Winds:** Creatures ending their turn within 10 feet make a Fortitude save (1 success) or are pushed 5 feet directly away.
- **Momentum Defense:** While the Cyclone has moved at least half its fly speed this turn, attacks against it add 1 to both attack dice.

**Description:** Cyclones control space by making it uncomfortable to occupy. Buffeting Winds keeps melee fighters pushed back while Wind Strike punishes anyone who closes. Against spellcasters and archers they use their speed to negate distance. The Momentum Defense makes them genuinely difficult to hit while moving, so they rarely stop moving. A summoner who needs a chokepoint held by something that cannot itself be easily held will find them useful.

---

## Stormcall
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Elemental (Air)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 40 (Con 5 × 8, Standard)
**DR:** 2 (compressed air shell)
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 70 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 3 / Con 5 / Agi 7 / Dex 5 / Int 3 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Ranged Combat 4, Perception 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +7 (Agi 7)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Wind Blade [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 7 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 damage; target pushed 10 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 9 damage (6 + 3 Str); target pushed 10 feet and knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 9 damage + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn from a concentrated wind impact
- **Lightning Arc [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 60 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 lightning damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 13 lightning damage (8 + 5 Dex); target gains Dazed condition until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 13 lightning damage + Dazed + Stunned until end of their next turn

**Special Abilities:**
- **Momentum Defense:** As above.
- **Storm Body:** Grapple attempts add 1 to both dice. If successfully grappled, the Stormcall makes a Fortitude save at the start of its turn (1 success) to break free automatically.

**Description:** Stormcalls fight from altitude, opening with Wind Blade against the closest threat, then spending a second action on Lightning Arc against anything at range, and using a third action to reposition while maintaining Momentum Defense. The MAP on that third action is real but the Stormcall accepts it — staying in motion matters more than clean dice. Agi 7 means they act before most of what they face. A summoner who gives a Stormcall a target designation and stays out of the way will find it requires little management.

---

## Tempest
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Elemental (Air)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 3 (gale-force shell)
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 80 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 7 / Dex 5 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Ranged Combat 5, Perception 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +7 (Agi 7)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Gale Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 7 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2); target pushed 15 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 14 damage (10 + 4 Str); target pushed 15 feet and knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 14 damage + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn; all creatures within 5 feet of target when they land take 4 bludgeoning damage from wind-driven impact
- **Chain Lightning [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 120 ft, up to 3 targets within 30 feet of each other
  - Per target: Net 1: 12 lightning damage (Half DR). Net 2: 20 lightning damage + Stunned until end of their next turn. Net 3: 20 lightning damage + Stunned + Dazed for 1 minute.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Vortex Presence:** Creatures starting their turn within 15 feet make a Fortitude save (1 success) or are pulled 10 feet directly toward the Tempest. Flying creatures add 1 to both their save dice.
- **Momentum Defense.**
- **Storm Body.**

**Description:** Tempests open against grouped enemies with Chain Lightning (2 actions), then spend the third on Gale Strike against the nearest pulled-in threat. On subsequent turns they split between two Gale Strikes and position, accepting the MAP on the third action to maintain Momentum Defense. Vortex Presence does the work of bringing enemies into range; the Tempest handles what arrives. A summoner deploying one near structures should be aware that Vortex Presence does not distinguish between enemies it is dragging in and unsecured objects it is also dragging in.

---

## Elder Gale
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Elemental (Air)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 4 (ancient storm-shell)
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 100 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 6 / Agi 8 / Dex 6 / Int 5 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Ranged Combat 6, Perception 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +8 (Agi 8)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Thunderstrike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 8 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 8 lightning damage (Half DR); target pushed 15 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 15 damage (10 + 5 Str) + 8 lightning damage; pushed 15 feet + Stunned until end of their next turn; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 15 damage + 8 lightning damage + Stunned; target also Deafened for 1 minute from the thunder crack at impact distance
- **Storm Surge [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 6 + Ranged Combat 6), 60-foot line, 5 feet wide
  - Per creature in line: Net 1: 20 lightning damage (Half DR). Net 2: 40 lightning damage + Stunned until end of their next turn. Net 3: 40 lightning damage + Stunned + knocked Prone.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Eye of the Storm:** The Elder Gale designates up to 6 creatures within 30 feet as protected. Protected creatures are immune to Vortex Presence and cannot be pushed or knocked Prone by any of the Elder Gale's attacks or abilities. Designation changes as a [Free] action.
- **Vortex Presence:** As Tempest, but 30-foot diameter and the save is a Hard task (2 successes to resist).
- **Momentum Defense.**
- **Storm Body.**
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Elder Gales are the first Air Elemental that actively protects allies rather than simply fighting. Eye of the Storm ensures the summoner and designated companions are never accidentally caught in Vortex Presence or thrown by Thunderstrike's pushback — a meaningful distinction at a tier where battlefield chaos becomes genuinely dangerous. A typical turn spends two actions on Thunderstrike against priority targets and a third on Storm Surge when a line of enemies presents itself, or repositioning to maintain Momentum Defense. Agi 8 means the Elder Gale acts before virtually everything it faces.

---

## Storm Sovereign
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Elemental (Air)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 5 (primordial storm-shell)
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 120 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 6 / Agi 8 / Dex 7 / Int 6 / Wis 6 / Cha 5 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Ranged Combat 7, Perception 8, Intimidate 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +8 (Agi 8)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Gale Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 8 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 10 lightning damage (Half DR); target pushed 20 feet and knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 2:* 20 damage (14 + 6 Str) + 10 lightning damage; Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 20 damage + 10 lightning damage + Stunned; all creatures within 10 feet of target take 8 lightning damage (Half DR) from the discharge
- **Tempest Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 7 + Ranged Combat 7), Range: 180 ft
  - Net 1: 24 lightning damage (Half DR) + Dazed until end of their next turn. Net 2: 48 lightning damage + Stunned + Dazed for 1 minute. Net 3: 48 lightning damage + Stunned + Dazed + Deafened for 1 minute; Fortitude save (2 successes) to reduce Deafened to 1 round only.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Storm Sovereign Aura:** Creatures within 20 feet that are not designated must make a Fortitude save at the start of their turn (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: pushed 15 feet and Deafened for 1 round. The summoner and designated allies are immune.
- **Lightning Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 4 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical lightning damage while within 60 feet.
- **Eye of the Storm:** As Elder Gale.
- **Momentum Defense.**
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** A Storm Sovereign's Aura displaces enemies constantly. A typical turn spends two actions on Gale Fist against whoever Storm Sovereign Aura failed to clear and a third on Tempest Bolt against anything trying to engage from range — three actions, the third at MAP but still at Ranged Combat 7 and Agi 8, which makes that penalty manageable. Lightning Immunity Sharing is a notable battlefield benefit — a summoner who builds their party around a Storm Sovereign can deny an entire damage type to grouped enemies without any additional resource cost. Clear target priority is the only instruction it strictly requires; the Sovereign determines execution from there.

---

## Void Gale
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Elemental (Air)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (world-storm shell)
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 140 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 6 / Agi 8 / Dex 8 / Int 7 / Wis 7 / Cha 6 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Ranged Combat 8, Perception 8, Intimidate 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +8 (Agi 8)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to lightning damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **World Wind [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 8 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 20 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage (Huge, heavy natural: 14 + 2) + 12 lightning damage (Half DR); target pushed 30 feet and knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 2:* 22 damage (16 + 6 Str) + 12 lightning damage; Prone + Stunned; all creatures within 15 feet of target take 10 lightning damage (Half DR) from discharge
  - *Margin 3:* 22 damage + 12 lightning damage + Stunned + Blinded until end of their next turn from the lightning discharge at face range
- **Skyfire [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 8 + Ranged Combat 8), Range: 200 ft, 20-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 20 lightning damage (Half DR). Net 2: 40 lightning damage + Stunned. Net 3: 40 lightning damage + Stunned + knocked Prone from the concussive thunderclap; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Primordial Vortex:** Creatures within 30 feet that are not designated must make Fortitude saves at the start of their turn (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: pushed 20 feet, knocked Prone, and Deafened for 1 minute. The summoner and designated allies are immune.
- **Cyclone Manifestation (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, the Void Gale establishes a sustained cyclone in a 40-foot diameter centered on itself. For 1 minute, all non-designated creatures treat the area as Difficult Terrain, must make Fortitude saves each round (2 successes) or become Restrained by wind, and ranged attacks into or through the area add 2 to both dice. The Void Gale moves normally through its own cyclone.
- **Lightning Immunity Sharing:** As Storm Sovereign, extended to 8 designated allies.
- **Eye of the Storm:** As Elder Gale.
- **Momentum Defense.**
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** Void Gales open with Cyclone Manifestation (2 actions) to dominate terrain, then spend the third action on World Wind against the summoner's designated priority target. Subsequent turns run two World Wind strikes against priority targets and a third on Skyfire when enemies cluster — or reverse that order if a formation presents itself first. Primordial Vortex handles anyone attempting to hold ground between turns. A Void Gale does not need tactical guidance — it has existed long enough that it understands what victory requires in most situations and moves toward it. What it needs from the summoner is target designation, ally identification, and confirmation of the rules of engagement. Everything else it handles.

---
# Earth Elementals

Earth Elementals do not move through stone. They are stone given will. They are the slowest of the four elemental categories and the most difficult to damage, destroy, or move. Where Air Elementals deny ground by making it dangerous to occupy, Earth Elementals deny ground by occupying it themselves and refusing to leave.

Their intelligence develops more slowly than other elementals as power increases — even high-tier Earth Elementals communicate in simple, declarative terms and respond poorly to instructions that require nuance or conditional logic. What they understand perfectly is a position, a target, and a line they are not to let anything cross. Give them those three things and they will perform without error until something geologically significant stops them.

They will not leave ground they have been assigned to hold, break stone they have been ordered to preserve, or abandon a Grappled target once they have committed to holding it. A summoner who needs flexibility calls Air. A summoner who needs something to stay exactly where it is until further notice calls Earth.

**Creature Type: Elemental**
All Earth Elementals share: Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

---

## Pebble Sprite
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Elemental (Earth)
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 10 (Con 2 × 5, Fragile)
**DR:** 1 (stone skin)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Burrow 10 ft (loose soil only)
**Attributes:** Str 3 / Con 2 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 1 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 2, Perception 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 10 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Gravel Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 1), Range: 20 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 2 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 2 damage; target makes Reflex save (1 success) or gains Dazzled condition until end of their next turn from gravel in the eyes

**Special Abilities:**
- **Earth Sense:** Aware of all vibrations through the ground within 10 ft. Cannot be surprised by creatures touching the same surface.
- **Stone Shape (minor):** Once per encounter, alters a small quantity of loose stone — fills a crack up to 1 inch wide and 3 feet long, creates a rough step in soft stone, or dislodges a pebble from height to drop on a target below (1 damage, requires height advantage).

**Description:** Pebble Sprites are scouts and minor nuisances. Their Tremorsense within 10 feet tells the summoner what is moving on any surface they occupy, and their minor stone shaping is occasionally exactly what is needed. A summoner who calls one for a fight has made a conceptual error. One called to monitor a floor, plug a small gap, or confirm whether something is approaching through ground vibration will find it performs that task adequately.

---

## Stone Lurker
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Elemental (Earth)
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 18 (Con 3 × 6, Standard)
**DR:** 3 (stone shell)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Burrow 20 ft (earth and stone)
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 3, Might 3, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 4 damage (Small, standard: 4 − 1 + 1 for stone density = 4)
  - *Margin 2:* 8 damage (4 + 4 Str); target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or knocked Prone

**Special Abilities:**
- **Submerge:** As a [Move] action, the Stone Lurker submerges into natural earth or stone it is standing on. While submerged it is Hidden and moves at its burrow speed. It must surface to attack.
- **Ambush:** When the Stone Lurker attacks on the same turn it surfaced from Submerge, it has Fortune on that attack.

**Description:** Stone Lurkers submerge, position under a target using Tremorsense, surface for an Ambush strike, and submerge again. They are slow and hit moderately hard but are genuinely difficult to pin down while natural ground is available. A summoner who places one under an approach path and tells it to hit anything that walks over it will find the instructions followed precisely and without elaboration.

---

## Granite Ward
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Elemental (Earth)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 4 (granite skin)
**Speed:** 25 ft, Burrow 20 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Might 4, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 damage (standard natural weapon)
  - *Margin 2:* 11 damage (6 + 5 Str); target knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 11 damage + Prone; target Restrained by earth and stone until they succeed on a Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as a [Combat] action

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round when hit by a physical attack, reduce incoming damage by 4.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** Cannot be knocked Prone by non-magical forced movement. Shoves automatically fail unless the attacker wins an opposed Strength + Athletics check (Hard task, 2 successes).
- **Earth Bond:** While standing on natural earth or stone, regains 4 HP at the start of its turn. Suppressed if it took magical damage this round.

**Description:** Granite Wards hold ground. They plant themselves where the summoner indicates and do not move unless ordered to. Earth Bond makes attrition against them on natural surfaces a slow process. They function best as mobile obstacles — position one in a doorway, narrow pass, or between the summoner and the enemy and it will remain there performing exactly that function until something removes it.

---

## Boulder Soldier
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Elemental (Earth)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 56 (Con 4 × 14, Tough)
**DR:** 5 (layered granite shell)
**Speed:** 25 ft, Burrow 25 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Might 5, Perception 3, Intimidate 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str); target knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + Prone; target Restrained until they succeed on Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as a [Combat] action
- **Rock Throw [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 1), Range: 60/120 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 12 damage (10 + 2 Dex); target knocked Prone

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** As Granite Ward.
- **Earth Bond:** As Granite Ward.
- **Tremor Strike (1/encounter) [Combat]:** As a [Combat] action, slams both fists into the ground simultaneously. All creatures within 15 feet standing on natural ground make a Reflex save. Compare Agi 2 + Might 5 targeting vs. each save. Net 1: 8 bludgeoning damage + Prone. Net 2: 16 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Restrained. This is a single action producing simultaneous strikes — use Shared Attribute Roll (Agi 2), roll Might separately.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 6.

**Description:** Boulder Soldiers are siege engines that walk. They advance slowly, shrug off mundane weapons entirely, and hit hard enough to flatten anyone who does not step back. Rock Throw handles opponents attempting to stay outside their reach. Tremor Strike is their battlefield opener when enemies have clustered — a single action that resets the positioning of everything nearby. A summoner who needs a wall broken or a cluster of fighters scattered will find them effective. Speed and nuance are not in their vocabulary.

---

## Mountain Heart
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Elemental (Earth)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (deep granite core)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 4 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 3 / Wis 4 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Might 6, Perception 4, Intimidate 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Crushing Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 17 damage (10 + 7 Str); target Grappled; no save; Grappled target takes 8 bludgeoning damage at the start of each of their turns
  - *Margin 3:* 17 damage + Grappled + Restrained + ongoing 8 damage

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** As above.
- **Earth Bond:** As above.
- **Engulf (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** Drives a Grappled target partially into the earth. Target must already be Grappled by the Mountain Heart. Target makes a Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: Restrained, Blinded, and takes 12 bludgeoning damage at the start of each turn. Escape requires a Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as a full [Combat] action, or an ally must dig them out over 2 rounds of [Interact] actions. On 1 success: Restrained only, not Blinded.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 8.

**Description:** Mountain Hearts grab things and do not let go. They spend actions building toward a Grapple and then Engulf the most dangerous held target to remove them from the fight entirely. Against opponents too large or strong to Grapple efficiently they simply hit very hard and regenerate. A summoner who needs something physically held — not slowed, not intimidated, but literally held in place — will find nothing better at this tier.

---

## Deepstone Elder
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Elemental (Earth)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 144 (Con 6 × 24, Tough)
**DR:** 7 (primordial granite)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 5 / Wis 5 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Might 7, Perception 5, Intimidate 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 300 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Ancient Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 22 damage (14 + 8 Str); target knocked Prone and Stunned until end of their next turn; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 22 damage + Prone + Stunned + Restrained by erupting earth; Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) to escape as a [Combat] action
- **Rock Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 60/120 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge boulder)
  - *Margin 2:* 14 damage; target knocked Prone; no save

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** As above.
- **Earth Bond:** Regenerates 8 HP per turn on natural earth or stone.
- **Ground Shatter (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** Slams the earth with both fists simultaneously. All creatures on the ground within 40 feet make a Reflex save. Compare Str 8 + Might 7 targeting vs. each save. Net 1: 16 bludgeoning damage + Prone. Net 2: 24 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Restrained by cracking earth. Net 3: 24 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Restrained + Stunned until end of their next turn. Designated allies are immune. Simultaneous fist slam — Shared Attribute Roll (Str 8), Might rolled separately.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 10.

**Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Deepstone Elders arrived at their current form by outlasting everything that attempted to move or break them. Tremorsense at 300 feet means nothing on the ground approaches without their awareness. Ground Shatter resets the battlefield on arrival; Ancient Slam handles whatever remains. Their regeneration and DR make sustained mundane damage against them impractical — without magical weapons or significant energy expenditure, fighting a Deepstone Elder on natural ground is an exercise in attrition the attacker will lose.

---

## Earthlord
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Elemental (Earth)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 8 (deep-forged primordial shell)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 50 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 6 / Wis 6 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Might 8, Perception 6, Intimidate 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 1 mile
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Mountain's Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 22 damage (14 + 8 Str); target Grappled + Restrained + knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 22 damage + Grappled + Restrained + Prone; target takes 12 bludgeoning damage at the start of each of their turns; Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes) each round to break free
- **Boulder Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 90/180 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage; target knocked Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn; no save

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** Magical forced movement requires the caster to win an opposed check against the Earthlord's Str 8 + Might 8 (Hard task, 2 successes).
- **Earth Bond:** Regenerates 10 HP per turn.
- **Seismic Authority (1/day) [Combat]:** Strikes the ground once. A 60-foot diameter seismic event occurs. All non-designated creatures on natural ground make Fortitude saves (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: 32 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Restrained for 1 minute; ally must spend 2 [Interact] actions digging them out or they succeed on a Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as a full [Combat] action. 1 success: 16 damage + Prone only. Structures in the area may take structural damage at GM discretion.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 12.

**Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** Earthlords do not hurry. Seismic Authority immediately Restrains as many enemies as possible; Mountain's Fist methodically crushes whatever remains. Their regeneration and DR make sustained damage against them impractical without magical investment. A summoner who has a Cooperative Earthlord has not acquired a tool — they have persuaded a geological force to point itself in a useful direction for a while.

---

## Ancient Stone
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Elemental (Earth)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 9 (primordial earth-shell)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 60 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 7 / Wis 7 / Cha 5 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Might 8, Perception 7, Intimidate 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 2 miles
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **World Crush [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 20 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage (Huge, heavy: 14 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 24 damage (16 + 8 Str); target Grappled + Restrained + Prone; takes 16 bludgeoning damage at start of each of their turns; no save; Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes) each round to break free
  - *Margin 3:* 24 damage + Grappled + Restrained + Prone; target begins Engulf — driven 5 feet into the ground at start of their next turn unless they succeed on a Fortitude save (Hard task), adding Blinded and doubling ongoing damage to 32
- **Mountain Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 120/240 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 20 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 20 damage; target knocked Prone + Stunned + all creatures within 10 feet take 8 bludgeoning damage from impact debris; no save on debris

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** Magical forced movement requires winning an opposed check against Str 8 + Might 8 (Hard task, 2 successes). Non-magical forced movement is impossible.
- **Earth Bond:** Regenerates 12 HP per turn.
- **Continental Tremor (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, releases the earth's full force in an 80-foot diameter. Every non-designated creature on natural ground makes a Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: 40 bludgeoning damage + Restrained for 1 hour; requires excavation to escape. 1 success: 20 damage + Prone. 2 successes: 10 damage only. Structures in the area take major structural damage.
- **Piercing and Slashing Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 4 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical piercing and slashing damage while within 60 feet.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 14.

**Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** An Ancient Stone summoned is not a decision about a fight. It is a decision about a place — this ground, held against everything, for as long as necessary. Continental Tremor resets the battlefield completely on arrival. World Crush removes individuals permanently from the engagement. DR 9 combined with Stone Skin and regeneration means mundane weapons accomplish essentially nothing. The Ancient Stone is old enough and intelligent enough to follow complex orders without misinterpretation, and patient enough that it does not distinguish between a fight that lasts ten minutes and one that lasts ten hours. Both are the same to it.

---
# Water Elementals

Water Elementals are not creatures that move through water. They are water given will. They are patient, adaptive, and relentless in the way that erosion is relentless — not through force alone but through persistence and the exploitation of whatever gap presents itself. Where Earth Elementals hold ground and Fire Elementals consume it, Water Elementals reshape it, wearing down opposition the way a river wears down stone.

They are significantly more dangerous near water than away from it. A Water Elemental on dry ground is capable and threatening. The same creature beside a lake or river is something else entirely — faster, harder to hit, able to drag enemies into an environment where the Elemental has every advantage and the enemy has none. Summoners who can choose their battlefield will always choose water when calling these creatures.

They will not seal gaps water is already flowing through, abandon a creature they are actively engulfing, or leave a body of water they have been assigned to guard. A Water Elemental given a pond to protect will be in that pond when the summoner returns. Whether anything else is still alive nearby depends on what approached.

**Creature Type: Elemental**
All Water Elementals share: Immune to cold damage, poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

---

## Droplet
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Elemental (Water)
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 10 (Con 2 × 5, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 20 ft, Swim 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 1 / Wis 2 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 1, Perception 2, Stealth 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 10 ft (in water only)
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to cold damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Splash [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 1), Range: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 1 damage; target gains Dazzled condition until end of their next turn from water in the eyes
  - *Margin 2:* 2 damage + 2 cold damage (Half DR); target makes Reflex save (1 success) or drops a loosely held item from the wet grip

**Special Abilities:**
- **Aqueous Form:** Fits through any gap water can pass through. An undisturbed Droplet in clear water requires a Hard task Perception check (2 successes) to notice by sight.
- **Contaminate:** Over 1 minute of contact, makes a body of liquid foul-tasting, cloudy, or cold. Not harmful but detectable with a Perception or Medicine check (1 success).

**Description:** Droplets are utility and infiltration. They slip under doors, into sealed containers, through arrow slits. They can confirm whether a cistern is the water supply for a building, whether a moat is deep, or whether something is already living in a well. Their combat contribution is negligible. A summoner who understands what a Droplet actually is will find it useful in ways that have nothing to do with fighting.

---

## Tide Wisp
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Elemental (Water)
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 12 (Con 2 × 6, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 20 ft, Swim 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 2 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 2, Perception 3, Stealth 3, Athletics 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 30 ft (in water)
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to cold damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Water Tendril [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 3 damage (Small, standard: 4 − 1) + 2 cold damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 5 damage (3 + 2 Str) + 2 cold damage; target gains Chilled condition
  - *Margin 3:* 5 damage + 2 cold damage; target gains Numbed condition

**Special Abilities:**
- **Slick Trail:** When the Tide Wisp moves across a surface, that surface becomes Difficult Terrain for other creatures until the start of the Wisp's next turn.
- **Aqueous Form:** As Droplet.

**Description:** Tide Wisps create area denial using Slick Trail and harass from reach with their tendril. In water they outpace most of what they fight and exploit that speed to avoid retaliation. On land they are less effective but useful for placing Difficult Terrain at chokepoints or approaches. A Cooperative Tide Wisp will use Slick Trail to protect the summoner's position rather than chasing targets — a reasonable instinct that benefits from explicit instruction to confirm.

---

## Current Stalker
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Elemental (Water)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 27 (Con 3 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 2 (dense water-form)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Swim 50 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 1 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Perception 4, Stealth 4, Athletics 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 60 ft (in water)
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to cold damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Cold Lash [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 4 damage (standard natural) + 4 cold damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 8 damage (4 + 4 Str) + 4 cold damage; target's movement speed reduced by 10 until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 8 damage + 4 cold damage; target gains Numbed condition; movement speed reduced by 20 until end of their next turn

**Special Abilities:**
- **Water Mastery:** In water, attacks against the Current Stalker add 1 to both dice. Its Cold Lash reach extends to 15 ft while in water.
- **Aqueous Form:** As Droplet.
- **Drag Under (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** When adjacent to a creature, attempts to pull them into any adjacent body of water. Opposed check: Agi 5 + Athletics 3 vs. target's Athletics or Acrobatics. On failure, target moved up to 10 feet into the water and gains the Grappled condition while submerged.

**Description:** Current Stalkers are dramatically more effective in water than away from it. In water they are fast, harder to hit, and use Drag Under to pull enemies into their preferred environment where the fight becomes considerably more one-sided. On dry ground they slow enemies and apply cold conditions at reach. A summoner who deploys them near water and uses Drag Under to establish positioning will find them capable well above their TR suggests. One who calls them into a building and expects the same performance will be disappointed.

---

## Wave Breaker
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Elemental (Water)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 56 (Con 4 × 14, Tough)
**DR:** 3 (dense water-shell)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Swim 60 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Might 5, Perception 4, Athletics 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 60 ft (in water)
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to cold damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Crashing Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 4 cold damage (Half DR); target pushed 5 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str) + 4 cold damage; target pushed 10 feet and knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + 4 cold damage + Prone; target gains Numbed condition
- **Water Jet [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 3), Range: 30 ft, 5-foot-wide line
  - Net 1: 8 cold damage (Half DR); creatures in line make Fortitude save (1 success) or pushed 10 feet. Net 2: 16 cold damage; pushed 15 feet; no save. Net 3: 16 cold damage + Frosted condition; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Engulf (Recharge 6-8) [Combat]:** Surges over one Medium or smaller creature within 5 feet. Target makes a Reflex save (compare Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5 vs. save successes). On failure: Grappled, Restrained, takes 8 cold damage per round. Fortitude save each round (Hard task, 2 successes) to break free, or an ally can spend 2 [Interact] actions to pull them clear.
- **Water Mastery:** As Current Stalker.

**Description:** Wave Breakers use Water Jet to clear lines and apply cold conditions, then close to melee. Engulf is their best option — used on a single priority target when the angle appears. In water they are substantially faster and more capable. A summoner who draws enemies near a water source before a Wave Breaker surfaces will find the encounter resolved more efficiently than the TR suggests is reasonable.

---

## Deep Tide
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Elemental (Water)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 4 (ocean-depth water-shell)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Swim 70 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 4 / Int 3 / Wis 4 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Might 5, Perception 5, Athletics 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 120 ft (in water)
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to cold damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 4 cold damage (Half DR); target pushed 5 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str) + 4 cold damage; target knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + 4 cold damage + Prone; target gains Numbed condition
- **Cold Surge [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 40 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 cold damage (Half DR); target gains Chilled
  - *Margin 2:* 12 cold damage (8 + 4 Dex); target gains Numbed
  - *Margin 3:* 12 cold damage + Frosted condition; target's next [Move] action costs an additional action

**Special Abilities:**
- **Engulf (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** As Wave Breaker, but damage increases to 12 cold per round. Grappled creature must succeed on a Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes) each round or gain 1 Exhaustion level from crushing pressure and cold.
- **Crushing Current:** When the Deep Tide hits a Grappled creature with any attack, that creature takes an additional 8 cold damage (Half DR) from water pressure.
- **Water Mastery:** As above.

**Description:** Deep Tides prioritize Engulf and build toward it through Slam attacks that accumulate Prone and cold conditions. Cold Surge handles targets trying to stay at range or retreat while the primary target is being held. In water they are apex predators at this tier — Crushing Current makes Engulfed targets suffer severely for every action the Deep Tide spends attacking them. A summoner who has terrain control and patience will find Deep Tides considerably more effective than fighting them straight suggests.

---

## Abyssal Surge
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Elemental (Water)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 144 (Con 6 × 24, Tough)
**DR:** 5 (ocean-trench water-shell)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Swim 80 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 5 / Int 4 / Wis 5 / Cha 3 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Might 6, Perception 6, Athletics 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 300 ft (in water)
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to cold damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Crushing Wave [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 6 cold damage (Half DR); target pushed 10 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 6 cold damage; target knocked Prone + Numbed condition; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 6 cold damage + Prone + Frosted; target Grappled as the wave wraps around them
- **Pressurized Jet [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 60 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 12 cold damage (Half DR); target pushed 10 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 20 cold damage (12 + ... Dex 5 + base); target pushed 15 feet + Frosted; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 20 cold damage + Frosted + Restrained by a column of pressurized water for 1 round; Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes) to move through it

**Special Abilities:**
- **Tidal Surge (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** Sends a 60-foot cone of pressurized water in a chosen direction. All creatures in the cone make a Reflex save. Compare Agi 5 + Melee Combat 7 targeting vs. each save. Net 1: 20 cold damage (Half DR) + pushed 20 feet. Net 2: 32 cold damage + pushed 30 feet + Prone. Net 3: 32 cold damage + pushed 30 feet + Prone + Frosted condition.
- **Engulf (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** As Deep Tide, but can target up to 2 Medium or 1 Large creature simultaneously.
- **Water Mastery:** In water, Abyssal Surge attacks cannot have their damage reduced by Reflex saves — targets take full damage on any net success.
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Abyssal Surges open with Tidal Surge to scatter enemy formations, then spend subsequent actions building Grapples through Crushing Wave while Pressurized Jet handles anything trying to disengage. Engulf removes priority targets from the engagement.
