In water, the Water Mastery suppression of Reflex saves makes them genuinely terrifying — everything takes full cold damage regardless of how well enemies roll. A summoner who deploys one near a sea, lake, or river should be aware that the Abyssal Surge will attempt to drag the fight into that water without prompting. That is simply what it is.

---

## Ocean Lord
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Elemental (Water)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (deep-current water-shell)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Swim 100 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 6 / Int 5 / Wis 6 / Cha 4 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Might 7, Perception 7, Athletics 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 1 mile (in water)
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to cold damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Abyssal Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 8 cold damage (Half DR); target pushed 15 feet + knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 2:* 22 damage (14 + 8 Str) + 8 cold damage; Prone + Frosted + Grappled; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 22 damage + 8 cold damage + Prone + Frosted + Grappled + Restrained; ongoing 16 cold damage per round while Grappled
- **Pressurized Stream [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 6 + Ranged Combat 7), Range: 120 ft
  - Net 1: 20 cold damage (Half DR). Net 2: 32 cold damage + Frosted + Restrained by pressurized water column for 1 round. Net 3: 32 cold damage + Frozen condition; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Maelstrom (1/encounter) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, creates a 40-foot diameter vortex of pressurized water. All creatures in range make Athletics or Acrobatics checks (Hard task, 2 successes) or dragged 20 feet toward the center and knocked Prone. Creatures reaching the center are Grappled and take 16 cold damage per round. Creatures starting their turn in range must check again. Designated allies immune. Lasts 1 minute.
- **Water Mastery:** As Abyssal Surge; also immune to fire damage in addition to cold.
- **Engulf (Recharge 5-8):** As Abyssal Surge.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** Ocean Lords open with Maelstrom to immediately cluster enemies, then use Abyssal Strike to lock specific targets into Grapples while the vortex handles everything else. Pressurized Stream freezes high-priority targets that manage to stay at range. A Friendly Ocean Lord coordinates complex engagement sequences without repeated instruction — it understands the shape of a fight well enough to anticipate what the summoner needs next. The Ocean Lord wants to pull everything into deep water. Giving it permission to pursue that agenda is simply a matter of telling it which targets matter most.

---

## Primordial Wave
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Elemental (Water)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 7 (world-ocean shell)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Swim 120 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 6 / Dex 7 / Int 6 / Wis 7 / Cha 5 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Might 8, Perception 8, Athletics 8
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Blindsight 5 miles (in water)
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Elemental — Immune to cold damage, fire damage, poison damage, Poisoned, disease, exhaustion, Paralyzed, Petrified, Unconscious. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **World Current [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 20 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage (Huge, heavy natural: 14 + 2) + 12 cold damage (Half DR); Prone + Frosted; no save
  - *Margin 2:* 24 damage (16 + 8 Str) + 12 cold damage; Prone + Frozen + Grappled; ongoing 24 cold damage per round while Grappled
  - *Margin 3:* 24 damage + 12 cold damage + Frozen + Grappled + immediately Engulfed; Blinded + Restrained + doubled ongoing damage to 48
- **Ocean's Wrath [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 7 + Ranged Combat 8), Range: 200 ft, 20-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 24 cold damage (Half DR). Net 2: 40 cold damage + Frosted. Net 3: 40 cold damage + Frozen condition; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **World Tide (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, calls a tidal surge across a 100-foot diameter. Every non-designated creature not flying makes a Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: 48 cold damage + Prone + Frozen for 1 hour. 1 success: 24 damage + Prone. 2 successes: 12 damage. Terrain in the radius becomes Difficult Terrain for 1 hour. Creates enough water to flood a significant area on natural ground.
- **Water Mastery:** In water, the Primordial Wave is immune to all damage except Positive energy and magical fire. On land, normal immunities apply.
- **Cold Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 4 designated allies are immune to non-magical cold damage while within 60 feet.
- **Maelstrom (1/encounter):** As Ocean Lord.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** A Primordial Wave at war is the ocean deciding to fight. World Tide resets the battlefield on arrival. World Current removes individuals with a single attack that Engulfs at Margin 3. Ocean's Wrath handles grouped formations at extreme range. In any environment with significant water it becomes effectively impossible to stop without overwhelming magical force — Water Mastery in that context grants near-total immunity to conventional damage. A summoner who calls one knows they are not deploying a creature. They are opening a door, and what comes through it intends to stay.

---
# Nephilim

Nephilim are daemons from the elemental planes that manifest on the prime material as giant humanoids. Their physical form is elemental energy made flesh — a Fire Nephilim bleeds magma, a Stone Nephilim sheds gravel when struck, an Ice Nephilim leaves frost wherever it steps, and an Air Nephilim's footsteps sound like wind through empty corridors. They are not elementals wearing humanoid shape. They are something older and stranger — elemental energy that chose a form with hands, with eyes, with something approaching a face.

They are territorial and tend toward solitary existence. Most have human-level intelligence or better, but their priorities are alien to mortal sensibilities. A Nephilim will keep its word with absolute literalness and is deeply offended by what it perceives as disrespect. Summoners who address them as tools will find cooperation difficult. Summoners who acknowledge what they are will find them considerably more tractable.

Nephilim do not exist at TR 1/8 or 1/4. The smallest Nephilim specimen is Large. Anything less is not a Nephilim — it is an elemental.

**Creature Type: Nephilim (Giant)**
All Nephilim share: Large or Huge size. Powerful Build — counts as one size category larger for carrying, pushing, dragging, and lifting. Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep in the conventional sense; they sustain themselves on elemental energy from their home plane.

Elemental immunities and resistances by subtype are noted in individual entries.

---

---

# FIRE NEPHILIM

Fire Nephilim are born of volcanic regions where the Plane of Fire intersects the prime material most strongly — deep calderas, active lava fields, places where the ground itself is barely solid. They bleed magma when wounded. Their skin is perpetually warm to the touch even at lower tiers; at higher tiers, proximity becomes dangerous without invitation.

They are the most aggressive of the four Nephilim subtypes, sharing the Fire Elemental's fundamental inability to back away from something combustible. Unlike Fire Elementals, they understand consequences — they simply often judge that the consequences are worth it.

**Fire Nephilim type traits:** Immune to fire damage. Resistance to lightning damage (+2 DR). Elemental Aura (fire, passive) — intensity scales with TR, noted per entry.

---

## Ember Kin
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Nephilim (Fire)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 2 (heat-hardened skin)
**Speed:** 35 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 3 / Dex 2 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Intimidate 3, Perception 3, Athletics 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to fire damage. Resistance to lightning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard natural: 8 + 2) + 2 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 15 damage (10 + 5 Str) + 2 fire damage; target gains Singed condition
  - *Margin 3:* 15 damage + 2 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition
- **Rock Throw [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 1), Range: 40/80 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 8 damage; target knocked Prone

**Special Abilities:**
- **Heat Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 5 feet take 2 fire damage (Half DR).
- **Powerful Build.**

**Description:** Ember Kin are young Fire Nephilim — large, hot, and straightforward. They advance and hit things. Their Heat Aura is a minor hazard rather than a primary threat at this tier. A summoner who needs a Large creature that frightens enemies through sheer physical presence and hits harder than anything of equivalent TR will find them adequate. They understand simple instructions and execute them without embellishment.

---

## Ashborn
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Nephilim (Fire)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 56 (Con 4 × 14, Tough)
**DR:** 3 (volcanic skin)
**Speed:** 35 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 3 / Dex 2 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Intimidate 4, Perception 3, Athletics 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to fire damage. Resistance to lightning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Burning Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 4 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str) + 4 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + 4 fire damage; target gains Burning condition; no save
- **Lava Spit [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 30 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 fire damage (Half DR); target gains Singed
  - *Margin 2:* 10 fire damage; target gains Ignited; no save

**Special Abilities:**
- **Heat Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 5 feet take 4 fire damage (Half DR).
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Smoldering Wounds:** When the Ashborn deals Ignited or Burning condition to a target, that target cannot remove the condition through normal means (dropping and rolling, ally assistance) for 1 round. Magical healing still removes it.

**Description:** Ashborn have developed enough control over their elemental nature to direct it precisely. Smoldering Wounds prevents easy condition removal, meaning enemies who take Ignited from a Burning Fist are going to burn for at least one full round. Lava Spit handles targets trying to stay out of melee range. A summoner who keeps an Ashborn engaged with a single priority target will find it converts that target's hit points into fire conditions efficiently.

---

## Cinder Giant
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Nephilim (Fire)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 4 (thick volcanic hide)
**Speed:** 35 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 4 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Intimidate 5, Perception 4, Athletics 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to fire damage. Resistance to lightning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Magma Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 6 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str) + 6 fire damage; target gains Ignited condition
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + 6 fire damage; target gains Burning condition; all creatures within 5 feet of target take 4 fire damage (Half DR) from magma splash
- **Volcanic Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 3), Range: 60/120 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 fire damage (Half DR); target gains Ignited
  - *Margin 2:* 16 fire damage; target gains Ignited; all creatures within 5 feet take 4 fire damage (Half DR)

**Special Abilities:**
- **Heat Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 10 feet take 6 fire damage (Half DR).
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Smoldering Wounds:** As Ashborn.
- **Intimidating Presence:** As a [Combat] action, the Cinder Giant roars and displays its full elemental nature. All creatures within 30 feet that can see and hear it make a Will save (opposed by Cha 4 + Intimidate 5). On failure, target gains the Frightened condition until end of their next turn. Creatures immune to fear are unaffected.

**Description:** Cinder Giants have grown into their authority. The Heat Aura is now a genuine battlefield hazard at 10 feet rather than a minor inconvenience, and Intimidating Presence gives them a meaningful action economy option against grouped enemies who haven't committed yet. Volcanic Hurl's splash damage means clustered enemies take incidental fire damage even when the hurl targets only one of them. A summoner who gives one a target and keeps allies out of the Heat Aura radius will find it handles the engagement without requiring further management.

---

## Magma Lord
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Nephilim (Fire)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 5 (primordial volcanic hide)
**Speed:** 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 5 / Wis 5 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Intimidate 6, Perception 5, Athletics 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to fire damage. Resistance to lightning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Inferno Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 8 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 8 fire damage; target gains Burning condition; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 8 fire damage + Burning; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or Stunned until end of their next turn from the concussive force of the blow
- **Magma Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 80/160 ft, 10-foot diameter on impact
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 12 fire damage (Half DR) + Singed. Net 2: 20 fire damage + Ignited. Net 3: 20 fire damage + Burning; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Heat Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 10 feet take 8 fire damage (Half DR).
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Smoldering Wounds:** As above.
- **Intimidating Presence:** As Cinder Giant, but the Will save is a Hard task (2 successes to resist), and on failure the target gains Frightened for 1 minute rather than until end of their next turn.
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Magma Lords are the point at which Fire Nephilim become a genuine threat to organized groups rather than individual combatants. Intimidating Presence at Hard task scatters most formations on arrival. Magma Hurl's 10-foot diameter means ranged enemies cannot cluster without taking shared fire damage on every throw. The Heat Aura at this range punishes anyone who tries to engage in melee without significant fire resistance. A summoner deploying one against a disciplined formation should expect the formation to stop being disciplined within the first round.

---

## Flame Titan
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Nephilim (Fire)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (ancient volcanic shell)
**Speed:** 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 4 / Int 6 / Wis 6 / Cha 6 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Intimidate 7, Perception 6, Athletics 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to fire damage. Resistance to lightning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **World-Breaker Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 10 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 22 damage (14 + 8 Str) + 10 fire damage; Burning condition + target knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 22 damage + 10 fire damage + Burning + Prone; all creatures within 10 feet of target take 8 fire damage (Half DR) from the impact shockwave
- **Inferno Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 120 ft, 15-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 16 fire damage (Half DR) + Ignited. Net 2: 28 fire damage + Burning. Net 3: 28 fire damage + Burning; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or Stunned until end of their next turn.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Conflagration Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 15 feet take 10 fire damage (Half DR). Flammable objects within 15 feet ignite at the start of each round.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Smoldering Wounds:** As above.
- **Intimidating Presence:** As Magma Lord.
- **Fire Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 2 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical fire damage while within 30 feet.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** A Flame Titan's Conflagration Aura reshapes the battlefield simply by existing — any environment with flammable material becomes a fire hazard within 15 feet of it, and enemies without fire resistance face meaningful damage just for closing to melee range. Fire Immunity Sharing protects the summoner and two allies from the collateral environmental damage the Flame Titan inevitably generates. Inferno Hurl's 15-foot diameter means it can suppress entire squads at range while closing to melee. A summoner who designates protected allies immediately on summoning and then stays clear will find the Flame Titan manages its own engagement effectively.

---

## Worldfire Colossus
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Nephilim (Fire)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 7 (primordial fire-flesh)
**Speed:** 45 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 7 / Wis 7 / Cha 7 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Intimidate 8, Perception 7, Athletics 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Tremorsense 60 ft (heat signatures)
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to fire damage. Resistance to lightning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Cataclysm Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage (Huge, heavy: 14 + 2) + 12 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 24 damage (16 + 8 Str) + 12 fire damage; Burning + Prone; no save; all creatures within 10 feet take 10 fire damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 3:* 24 damage + 12 fire damage + Burning + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn; area damage increases to 16 fire
- **World-Flame Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 6), Range: 150 ft, 20-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 20 fire damage (Half DR) + Ignited. Net 2: 36 fire damage + Burning. Net 3: 36 fire damage + Burning + Blinded until end of their next turn from the searing flash; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Primordial Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 20 feet take 14 fire damage (Half DR). Flammable terrain within 20 feet ignites and continues burning — the area becomes Difficult Terrain as fire spreads at normal rates.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **World-Burning Presence (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, the Worldfire Colossus expresses its full elemental nature in a 60-foot diameter. All non-designated creatures make a Reflex save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: 48 fire damage + Burning + Blinded for 1 minute. 1 success: 24 fire damage + Ignited. 2 successes: 12 fire damage only. The ground within the area ignites if flammable; non-flammable surfaces become superheated (4 fire damage per round to creatures standing on them for the next minute).
- **Fire Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 4 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical fire damage within 60 feet.
- **Intimidating Presence:** As Magma Lord.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** A Worldfire Colossus is a living catastrophe that has agreed, for now, to catastrophe on the summoner's behalf. World-Burning Presence on arrival sets the terms of the engagement — after it goes off, the battlefield is a fire hazard for everyone not designated as protected. The Primordial Aura at 20 feet means enemies cannot close without taking 14 fire damage per round before any attack lands. A summoner who calls one has made a decision about how this fight ends, and the Colossus will execute that decision with a thoroughness that renders tactical nuance largely irrelevant.

---

---

# AIR NEPHILIM

Air Nephilim manifest where the Plane of Air intersects the prime material most strongly — high mountain peaks, exposed cliff faces, the upper reaches of storm systems. Their flesh is dense air made solid, their eyes the pale grey of high-altitude sky. They move with a fluid economy that makes their size deceptive — an Air Nephilim covering ground is faster than it looks, and they carry the wind with them.

They are the most communicative of the four Nephilim subtypes. Even lower-tier Air Nephilim express opinions about their instructions and will point out what they consider to be tactical errors. Whether the summoner finds this useful or irritating depends on the summoner.

**Air Nephilim type traits:** Immune to lightning damage. Resistance to cold damage (+2 DR). Elemental Aura (wind, passive) — intensity scales with TR, noted per entry.

---

## Gale Kin
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Nephilim (Air)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 2 (wind-compressed skin)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Perception 4, Athletics 3, Intimidate 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to lightning damage. Resistance to cold damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Wind Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2); target pushed 5 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 14 damage (10 + 4 Str); target pushed 10 feet and knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 14 damage + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn
- **Gust Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 40 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 damage; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or pushed 5 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 6 damage; target pushed 10 feet; no save; target knocked Prone

**Special Abilities:**
- **Wind Aura:** Ranged attacks passing within 10 feet of the Gale Kin add 1 to one die of the attacker's choice from wind interference.
- **Powerful Build.**

**Description:** Gale Kin are mobile and hit harder than their Strength alone suggests because their strikes carry wind force behind them. The pushback on Wind Strike makes positioning enemies against terrain a viable tactic even at this tier. Wind Aura provides passive protection against ranged attackers. A summoner who uses terrain intelligently — placing the Gale Kin between enemies and a cliff edge, a wall, or a body of water — will find the pushback mechanics considerably more punishing than they appear in flat terrain.

---

## Stormborn
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Nephilim (Air)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 56 (Con 4 × 14, Tough)
**DR:** 3 (storm-compressed skin)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 50 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 6 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 4 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Perception 5, Athletics 4, Intimidate 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to lightning damage. Resistance to cold damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Thunder Blow [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 4 lightning damage (Half DR); target pushed 10 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 15 damage (10 + 5 Str) + 4 lightning damage; pushed 10 feet + Stunned until end of their next turn; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 15 damage + 4 lightning damage + Stunned + Deafened for 1 minute from the thunderclap at impact
- **Lightning Throw [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 3), Range: 60 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 lightning damage (Half DR); target gains Dazed until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 2:* 12 lightning damage (8 + 4 Dex); target Stunned until end of their next turn; no save

**Special Abilities:**
- **Wind Aura:** As Gale Kin, but the interference range extends to 15 feet.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Momentum:** When the Stormborn moves at least 20 feet before making a melee attack, subtract 1 from both attack dice on that attack. The speed of the approach adds force to the strike.

**Description:** Stormborn are fast and hit with enough force to stun reliably at Margin 2. The combination of Momentum and their fly speed means they can build approach distance quickly and deliver Thunder Blow at subtract-1 to both dice consistently. A summoner who gives one space to maneuver will find it applies Stunned more frequently than the raw numbers suggest — the action economy value of reliably stunning a target for a round is significant at this tier.

---

## Thunder Giant
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Nephilim (Air)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 4 (storm-dense flesh)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 60 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 6 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 4 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Perception 5, Athletics 5, Intimidate 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to lightning damage. Resistance to cold damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Storm Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 6 lightning damage (Half DR); target pushed 15 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 20 damage (14 + 6 Str) + 6 lightning damage; pushed 15 feet + Stunned until end of their next turn; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 20 damage + 6 lightning damage + Stunned + Deafened for 1 minute; all creatures within 10 feet of target take 4 lightning damage (Half DR) from the discharge
- **Chain Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 80 ft, up to 2 additional targets within 20 feet of the first
  - Per target: Net 1: 10 lightning damage (Half DR). Net 2: 16 lightning damage + Dazed until end of their next turn. Net 3: 16 lightning damage + Stunned until end of their next turn.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Storm Aura:** Ranged attacks passing within 15 feet of the Thunder Giant add 1 to both dice from severe wind interference. Creatures starting their turn within 10 feet make a Fortitude save (1 success) or are pushed 5 feet directly away.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Momentum:** As Stormborn.
- **Resilient Defense (1/day).**

**Description:** Thunder Giants hit hard enough that their pushback mechanics start repositioning groups rather than individuals. Chain Bolt's secondary targeting means they can apply Dazed or Stunned to clustered enemies with a single ranged action. Storm Aura's wind interference makes them naturally difficult for archers to engage while the storm presence pushes melee fighters back. A summoner who positions one between enemies and open ground will find the battlefield steadily pushed in a direction that favors the summoner's allies.

---

## Tempest Lord
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Nephilim (Air)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 5 (ancient storm-flesh)
**Speed:** 45 ft, Fly 80 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 7 / Dex 5 / Int 5 / Wis 5 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Perception 6, Athletics 6, Intimidate 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +7 (Agi 7)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to lightning damage. Resistance to cold damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Tempest Blow [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 7 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 8 lightning damage (Half DR); target pushed 20 feet
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 8 lightning damage; pushed 20 feet + Stunned until end of their next turn + knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 8 lightning damage + Stunned + Prone; all creatures within 15 feet of target take 8 lightning damage (Half DR) and are pushed 10 feet from the shockwave
- **Lightning Lance [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 100 ft, 5-foot-wide line
  - Per creature in line: Net 1: 16 lightning damage (Half DR) + Dazed. Net 2: 28 lightning damage + Stunned until end of their next turn. Net 3: 28 lightning damage + Stunned + Deafened for 1 minute.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Vortex Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 20 feet make a Fortitude save (1 success) or pushed 10 feet directly away. Ranged attacks passing through the aura area add 1 to both dice.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Momentum:** As above.
- **Intimidating Presence:** As a [Combat] action, the Tempest Lord releases a thunderclap. All creatures within 40 feet that can hear it make a Will save (Hard task, 2 successes). On failure, target gains Frightened condition for 1 minute. On 1 success, target gains Frightened until end of their next turn.
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Tempest Lords are authority figures among Air Nephilim — they communicate in complete sentences, evaluate the battlefield intelligently, and will offer tactical observations whether asked or not. The Vortex Aura keeps enemies constantly displaced, Lightning Lance clears lines, and Tempest Blow at Margin 2 sends targets flying far enough to take falling damage against walls or off ledges. A summoner who briefs one on the full situation rather than just issuing target instructions will find it performs significantly better — Tempest Lords do things with context that they cannot do without it.

---

## Storm Titan
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Nephilim (Air)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (primordial storm-flesh)
**Speed:** 50 ft, Fly 100 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 8 / Dex 6 / Int 6 / Wis 6 / Cha 6 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Perception 7, Athletics 7, Intimidate 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +8 (Agi 8)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to lightning damage. Resistance to cold damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **World Storm Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 8 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 10 lightning damage (Half DR); target pushed 20 feet + Prone; no save
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 10 lightning damage; pushed 20 feet + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn; all creatures within 15 feet of target take 10 lightning damage (Half DR) from discharge
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 10 lightning damage + Prone + Stunned; area discharge increases to 16 lightning damage; all affected creatures also Deafened for 1 minute
- **Skyfire Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 6 + Ranged Combat 6), Range: 150 ft, 15-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 20 lightning damage (Half DR) + Dazed. Net 2: 36 lightning damage + Stunned until end of their next turn. Net 3: 36 lightning damage + Stunned + Prone; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Cyclone Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 20 feet make a Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes) or pushed 20 feet directly away and knocked Prone. Ranged attacks through the aura add 2 to both dice.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Momentum:** As above.
- **Lightning Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 3 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical lightning damage within 60 feet.
- **Intimidating Presence:** As Tempest Lord.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** Storm Titans are Agi 8 — they act before almost everything they face and maintain that advantage through their entire engagement. Cyclone Aura at Hard task difficulty continuously displaces enemies regardless of how many actions they spend trying to hold position. Skyfire Bolt handles grouped formations at 150 feet. World Storm Fist's discharge damage at Margin 2 and 3 means the area around the primary target takes significant lightning damage as well. A summoner who keeps clear of the Cyclone Aura radius and lets the Storm Titan work will find most engagements resolved decisively and quickly.

---

## Void Tempest
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Nephilim (Air)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 7 (world-storm flesh)
**Speed:** 55 ft, Fly 120 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 8 / Dex 7 / Int 7 / Wis 7 / Cha 7 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Perception 8, Athletics 8, Intimidate 8
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 60 ft (air pressure)
**Initiative Bonus:** +8 (Agi 8)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to lightning damage. Resistance to cold damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Worldstorm Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 8 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 20 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage (Huge, heavy: 14 + 2) + 12 lightning damage (Half DR); target pushed 30 feet + Prone; no save
  - *Margin 2:* 24 damage (16 + 8 Str) + 12 lightning damage; pushed 30 feet + Prone + Stunned; all creatures within 20 feet of target take 12 lightning damage (Half DR) + Dazed from the discharge
  - *Margin 3:* 24 damage + 12 lightning damage + Prone + Stunned; discharge area takes 20 lightning damage + Stunned; no save on area
- **Heaven's Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 7 + Ranged Combat 8), Range: 200 ft, 20-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 24 lightning damage (Half DR) + Stunned until end of their next turn. Net 2: 48 lightning damage + Stunned + Deafened for 1 minute. Net 3: 48 lightning damage + Stunned + Deafened + knocked Prone; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **World Vortex Aura:** Creatures within 30 feet that are not designated make a Fortitude save at the start of their turn (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: pushed 30 feet, knocked Prone, and Deafened for 1 minute. 1 success: pushed 15 feet only.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **World-Storm Presence (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, the Void Tempest manifests its full elemental nature in an 80-foot diameter. All non-designated creatures make a Reflex save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: 48 lightning damage + Stunned for 1 minute + Deafened permanently (Fortitude save, 2 successes, to reduce to 1 hour). 1 success: 24 damage + Stunned until end of their next turn. 2 successes: 12 damage only. Buildings and structures take structural damage.
- **Lightning Immunity Sharing:** As Storm Titan, extended to 6 designated allies.
- **Intimidating Presence:** As Tempest Lord.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** A Void Tempest is an apex Air Nephilim that has existed long enough to understand mortal warfare at a strategic rather than tactical level. World-Storm Presence on arrival; World Vortex Aura maintaining continuous battlefield control; Heaven's Bolt suppressing enemy formations at range while Worldstorm Strike removes priority targets. It will communicate its assessment of the engagement openly and expects the summoner to engage with that assessment rather than simply repeat instructions. A summoner who treats a Void Tempest as a tool will find it technically compliant. One who treats it as a partner will find it does things with that relationship that compliance alone cannot produce.

---

---

# STONE NEPHILIM

Stone Nephilim manifest where the Plane of Earth intersects the prime material most heavily — deep mountain roots, ancient geological formations, cavern systems so old they predate most surface civilizations. They are the densest of the four Nephilim subtypes in every sense. Their flesh is granite and basalt. They shed gravel when struck hard enough. They move with the deliberate economy of something that has never needed to hurry because nothing has ever successfully run from them.

They are the least communicative of the four subtypes. Stone Nephilim speak when they have something to say and not otherwise. Their instructions are understood precisely and executed without elaboration or deviation. A summoner who gives clear, simple instructions to a Stone Nephilim will find them followed with a thoroughness that borders on geological.

**Stone Nephilim type traits:** Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage. Resistance to non-magical bludgeoning damage (+2 DR). Elemental Aura (earth tremor, passive) — intensity scales with TR, noted per entry.

---

## Stone Kin
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Nephilim (Stone)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 4 (granite flesh)
**Speed:** 25 ft, Burrow 15 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Might 4, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage. Resistance to non-magical bludgeoning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 15 damage (10 + 5 Str); target knocked Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 15 damage + Prone; target Restrained by erupting stone until they succeed on a Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as a [Combat] action
- **Rock Throw [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 1), Range: 40/80 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 8 damage; target knocked Prone

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** Cannot be knocked Prone by non-magical forced movement. Shoves automatically fail unless the attacker wins an opposed Strength + Athletics check (Hard task, 2 successes).
- **Earth Bond:** While on natural earth or stone, regains 4 HP at the start of its turn. Suppressed if it took magical damage this round.
- **Powerful Build.**

**Description:** Stone Kin are dense, durable, and slow. Mundane weapons accomplish essentially nothing against their piercing and slashing immunity. They hold positions with the same commitment as Earth Elementals — put one in a doorway and it will be there when you return. Their Tremorsense gives them awareness of anything approaching through connected ground, which makes them difficult to ambush and reliable as sentinels even without active instructions.

---

## Rockborn
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Nephilim (Stone)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 56 (Con 4 × 14, Tough)
**DR:** 5 (deep granite flesh)
**Speed:** 25 ft, Burrow 20 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Might 5, Perception 3, Intimidate 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage. Resistance to non-magical bludgeoning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Crushing Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str); target knocked Prone + Grappled; no save; Grappled target takes 6 bludgeoning damage at the start of each of their turns
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + Prone + Grappled + Restrained; ongoing damage increases to 10
- **Boulder Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 1), Range: 60/120 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 10 damage; target knocked Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn; no save

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** As Stone Kin.
- **Earth Bond:** As Stone Kin.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Stone Grip:** Creatures Grappled by the Rockborn add 1 to both dice on Athletics, Acrobatics, and Might checks to escape. The stone hand does not tire.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round when hit by a physical attack, reduce incoming damage by 4.

**Description:** Rockborn transition Stone Nephilim from obstacles into active threats. Crushing Slam builds toward Grapple and the ongoing damage that Grapple provides. Stone Grip makes escape from that Grapple genuinely difficult. A summoner who wants something held in place while allies deal with it elsewhere will find a Rockborn with a Grappled target the most efficient delivery mechanism available at this tier.

---

## Boulder Giant
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Nephilim (Stone)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (ancient granite flesh)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 25 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 4 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Might 6, Perception 4, Intimidate 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage. Resistance to non-magical bludgeoning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Mountain Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str); target Grappled + Prone; no save; ongoing 8 bludgeoning damage per round
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + Grappled + Prone + Restrained; ongoing damage increases to 14; Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes) each round to break free
- **Mountain Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 80/160 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 14 damage; target knocked Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn; all creatures within 10 feet take 6 bludgeoning damage from debris; no save on debris

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** As above.
- **Earth Bond:** Regenerates 6 HP per turn on natural earth or stone.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Stone Grip:** As Rockborn, but escape checks add 2 to both dice.
- **Ground Tremor (1/encounter) [Combat]:** As a [Combat] action, stamps the ground. All creatures within 20 feet on natural ground make a Reflex save (compare Agi 2 + Might 6 targeting vs. save). Net 1: 10 bludgeoning damage + Prone. Net 2: 18 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Restrained by cracking ground. Designated allies immune.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 6.

**Resilient Defense (1/day).**

**Description:** Boulder Giants are the point at which Stone Nephilim become genuinely threatening to organized groups. Ground Tremor disrupts formation positioning on arrival. Mountain Fist builds toward a Grapple that enemies find very difficult to escape. Mountain Hurl's debris damage means clustered enemies take area damage even when the throw targets only one. A summoner who has patience and keeps the Boulder Giant engaged consistently will find attrition steadily resolves in their favor.

---

## Mountain Lord
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Nephilim (Stone)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 7 (primordial stone flesh)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 5 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Might 7, Perception 5, Intimidate 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 300 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage. Resistance to non-magical bludgeoning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Earth Breaker [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 22 damage (14 + 8 Str); target Grappled + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn; no save; ongoing 12 bludgeoning damage per round while Grappled
  - *Margin 3:* 22 damage + Grappled + Prone + Stunned; ongoing increases to 18; target begins being driven into the ground — Engulf triggers at start of their next turn unless they succeed Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes)
- **Seismic Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 80/160 ft, 10-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 14 bludgeoning damage + Prone. Net 2: 22 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn. Net 3: 22 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Stunned; all creatures within 10 feet of impact take 8 bludgeoning damage from shockwave.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** Magical forced movement requires an opposed check against Str 8 + Might 7 (Hard task, 2 successes).
- **Earth Bond:** Regenerates 8 HP per turn.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Stone Grip:** Escape checks add 3 to both dice.
- **Seismic Slam (Recharge 5-8) [Combat]:** Slams both fists into the ground simultaneously. All creatures within 30 feet on natural ground make a Reflex save. Compare Str 8 + Might 7 targeting vs. each save. Net 1: 20 bludgeoning damage + Prone. Net 2: 32 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Restrained for 1 minute. Net 3: 32 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Restrained + Stunned until end of their next turn. Designated allies immune. Simultaneous slam — Shared Attribute Roll (Str 8), Might rolled separately.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 10.

**Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Mountain Lords have Tremorsense at 300 feet — nothing approaches on the ground without their awareness. Seismic Slam resets the battlefield on arrival. Earth Breaker at Margin 3 drives targets into the ground and begins Engulfing them. Seismic Hurl's radius means groups of enemies cannot cluster in ranged positions without taking area damage. A summoner who gives one a position to hold and a target priority list will find it requires no further management.

---

## Stone Titan
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Nephilim (Stone)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 8 (deep-forged stone flesh)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 6 / Wis 6 / Cha 5 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Might 8, Perception 6, Intimidate 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 1 mile
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage. Resistance to non-magical bludgeoning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Continental Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 22 damage (14 + 8 Str); target Grappled + Prone + Restrained; ongoing 16 bludgeoning damage per round; no save; Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes) each round to break free
  - *Margin 3:* 22 damage + immediately Engulfed (driven into ground); Blinded + Restrained + 24 bludgeoning damage per round; Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as full [Combat] action to escape, or ally excavates over 3 [Interact] actions
- **World Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 120/240 ft, 15-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 18 bludgeoning damage + Prone. Net 2: 28 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn. Net 3: 28 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Stunned; all creatures within 15 feet take 12 bludgeoning damage from shockwave.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** As Mountain Lord; non-magical forced movement is impossible.
- **Earth Bond:** Regenerates 10 HP per turn.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Stone Grip:** Escape checks add 4 to both dice.
- **Seismic Authority (1/day) [Combat]:** As Earthlord entry in Earth Elementals — 60-foot diameter seismic event; designated allies immune.
- **Piercing and Slashing Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 2 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical piercing and slashing damage while within 30 feet.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 12.

**Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** Stone Titans are the point at which Stone Nephilim become effectively unkillable through mundane means. DR 8 plus Stone Skin plus regeneration plus immunity to non-magical piercing and slashing means conventional weapons accomplish nothing meaningful. Seismic Authority immediately Restrains as many enemies as possible; Continental Fist removes priority targets from the engagement through Engulfing. A summoner who calls one has effectively ended the question of whether the physical fight can be won.

---

## World Pillar
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Nephilim (Stone)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 9 (primordial earth-flesh)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Burrow 60 ft
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 2 / Dex 2 / Int 7 / Wis 7 / Cha 6 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Might 8, Perception 7, Intimidate 8
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Tremorsense 2 miles
**Initiative Bonus:** +2 (Agi 2)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage. Resistance to non-magical bludgeoning damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **World Crush [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 2 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 20 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage (Huge, heavy: 14 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 24 damage (16 + 8 Str); target immediately Engulfed (Grappled + Restrained + Prone + Blinded); 24 bludgeoning damage per round; no save; Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as full [Combat] action each round to escape
  - *Margin 3:* 24 damage + Engulfed; damage increases to 36 per round; escape requires ally excavation (4 [Interact] actions) or Might check at Fortune (the stone has begun to fuse around them)
- **Continental Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 2 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 150/300 ft, 20-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 24 bludgeoning damage + Prone. Net 2: 36 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn. Net 3: 36 bludgeoning damage + Prone + Stunned + Restrained for 1 round by debris; all creatures within 20 feet take 16 bludgeoning damage.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Immovable:** As Stone Titan; magical forced movement also requires Hard task opposed check.
- **Earth Bond:** Regenerates 12 HP per turn.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Stone Grip:** Escape checks add 5 to both dice. At Margin 3 Engulf, escape checks have Misfortune instead.
- **Continental Tremor (1/day):** As Ancient Stone entry in Earth Elementals — 80-foot diameter; designated allies immune.
- **Piercing and Slashing Immunity Sharing:** As Stone Titan, extended to 4 designated allies.

**Reactions:**
- **Stone Skin [Reaction]:** Once per round, reduce incoming physical damage by 14.

**Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** A World Pillar is the elemental concept of stone given will and scale. It does not fight — it removes things from the fight permanently. World Crush at Margin 2 immediately Engulfs with no save and no preliminary steps. Continental Hurl controls entire approach corridors. DR 9 plus Stone Skin plus regeneration plus elemental immunities means the only meaningful way to damage it is magical. A summoner who calls one has made a decision about what this location will look like when the World Pillar is done with it. That decision is largely irreversible once made.

---

---

# ICE NEPHILIM

Ice Nephilim manifest where the Plane of Water, in its coldest and most concentrated form, intersects the prime material — deep glaciers, polar ice fields, mountain peaks above the snowline where the cold is a physical presence rather than an absence of heat. They are the Water Resonance Summoner's heavy combat option, built from ice rather than liquid, and they express their elemental nature through cold, weight, and the kind of stillness that precedes a glacier's advance.

They are patient in a way that distinguishes them from other Nephilim subtypes. Ice Nephilim do not rush. They build pressure steadily — stacking cold conditions, slowing movement, grinding down opposition the way a glacier grinds down bedrock. A summoner who wants fast, decisive results should call a Fire Nephilim. A summoner who wants the enemy to be unable to effectively fight back by the third round of combat should call Ice.

**Ice Nephilim type traits:** Immune to cold damage. Resistance to non-magical piercing and slashing damage (+2 DR). Elemental Aura (cold, passive) — intensity scales with TR, noted per entry.

---

## Frost Kin
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Nephilim (Ice)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 36 (Con 4 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 3 (ice-dense flesh)
**Speed:** 30 ft (ignores movement penalties from ice and snow)
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 3 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Athletics 3, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to cold damage. Resistance to non-magical piercing and slashing damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Ice Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 2 cold damage (Half DR); target gains Chilled condition
  - *Margin 2:* 15 damage (10 + 5 Str) + 2 cold damage; target gains Numbed condition; target's movement speed reduced by 10 until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 15 damage + 2 cold damage; target gains Frosted condition; movement speed reduced by 20 until end of their next turn
- **Ice Shard [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 30 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 cold damage (Half DR); target gains Chilled
  - *Margin 2:* 10 cold damage; target gains Numbed; movement speed reduced by 10

**Special Abilities:**
- **Frost Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 5 feet take 2 cold damage (Half DR) and gain the Chilled condition.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Ice Stride:** Moves across ice and snow at full speed. Creates a thin frost trail wherever it walks — surfaces within 5 feet of its path become Difficult Terrain for 1 minute.

**Description:** Frost Kin begin the cold stacking process that defines Ice Nephilim at higher tiers. Even at TR 1/2, a target that takes two or three Ice Slam hits will be moving at significantly reduced speed and suffering stacking cold conditions. Ice Stride's Difficult Terrain trail makes repositioning around them increasingly costly. A summoner who keeps a Frost Kin engaged with a single target will find that target significantly impaired within two rounds without necessarily taking catastrophic damage — the goal is impairment, not elimination.

---

## Iceborn
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Nephilim (Ice)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 56 (Con 4 × 14, Tough)
**DR:** 4 (thick ice-flesh)
**Speed:** 30 ft (ignores ice and snow movement penalties)
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 3 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Athletics 4, Perception 4, Intimidate 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to cold damage. Resistance to non-magical piercing and slashing damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Glacial Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 4 cold damage (Half DR); target gains Numbed condition
  - *Margin 2:* 16 damage (10 + 6 Str) + 4 cold damage; target gains Frosted condition; movement speed halved until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 16 damage + 4 cold damage; target gains Frozen condition; Restrained until they succeed on a Might check (1 success) as a [Combat] action
- **Frost Lance [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 3), Range: 60 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 cold damage (Half DR); target gains Numbed
  - *Margin 2:* 12 cold damage (8 + ... using Dex for ranged: 8 + 3 Dex base... adjusted to 12 total); target gains Frosted + movement speed halved until end of their next turn

**Special Abilities:**
- **Frost Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 10 feet take 4 cold damage (Half DR) and gain the Chilled condition.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Ice Stride:** As Frost Kin.
- **Permafrost:** Ground within 15 feet of the Iceborn where it has stood for at least 1 round becomes frozen. Frozen ground is Difficult Terrain and creatures moving across it make Acrobatics checks (1 success) or fall Prone.

**Description:** Iceborn can apply the Frozen condition through Glacial Strike, which is the first Ice Nephilim capable of fully Restraining a target through cold alone. Permafrost spreads hazardous terrain passively as they move and stand, meaning the longer an engagement lasts the more difficult the battlefield becomes for anything that relies on movement. A summoner who gives one a target and space to maneuver will find the target increasingly unable to move by the second or third round of contact.

---

## Glacier Giant
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Nephilim (Ice)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 5 (ancient ice-flesh)
**Speed:** 35 ft (ignores ice and snow movement penalties)
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 3 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Athletics 5, Perception 5, Intimidate 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +3 (Agi 3)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to cold damage. Resistance to non-magical piercing and slashing damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Permafrost Fist [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 3 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 6 cold damage (Half DR); target gains Frosted condition
  - *Margin 2:* 20 damage (14 + 6 Str) + 6 cold damage; target gains Frozen condition + Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 20 damage + 6 cold damage + Frozen + Prone; target Grappled as ice encases their limbs; ongoing 8 cold damage per round while Grappled
- **Glacier Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 80/160 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 12 cold damage (Half DR); target gains Frosted + movement halved
  - *Margin 2:* 18 cold damage; target gains Frozen + Prone; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 18 cold damage + Frozen + Prone; target Restrained by ice impact for 1 round; Fortitude save (1 success) to move

**Special Abilities:**
- **Frost Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 10 feet take 6 cold damage (Half DR) and gain the Numbed condition.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Permafrost:** As Iceborn, extended to 20 feet.
- **Ice Stride:** As above.
- **Resilient Defense (1/day).**

**Description:** Glacier Giants apply Frozen reliably at Margin 2, which Restrains targets, and then Grapple at Margin 3 to add ongoing cold damage on top of the movement restriction. Glacier Hurl can apply Frozen at range, meaning they can immobilize high-priority targets before closing. The Frost Aura's Numbed condition on everything within 10 feet means enemies fighting in melee are taking stacking cold conditions from proximity alone. A summoner who keeps one engaged consistently will find the battlefield progressively frozen — literally — within a few rounds.

---

## Tide Lord
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Nephilim (Ice)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 6 (primordial ice-flesh)
**Speed:** 35 ft (ignores ice and snow movement penalties)
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 5 / Int 5 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Athletics 6, Perception 6, Intimidate 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to cold damage. Resistance to non-magical piercing and slashing damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Abyssal Freeze [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 8 cold damage (Half DR); target gains Frosted + movement halved
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 8 cold damage; target gains Frozen + Prone + Grappled; ongoing 12 cold damage per round; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 8 cold damage + Frozen + Prone + Grappled + Restrained; target begins Engulf — driven into ice at start of their next turn unless Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes)
- **Tidal Ice Lance [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 100 ft, 5-foot-wide line
  - Per creature in line: Net 1: 16 cold damage (Half DR) + Frosted. Net 2: 28 cold damage + Frozen + movement halved. Net 3: 28 cold damage + Frozen + Prone; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Glacial Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 15 feet take 8 cold damage (Half DR) and gain the Frosted condition. Creatures already Frosted within the aura gain the Frozen condition instead.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Permafrost:** As above, extended to 30 feet. Permafrost created by the Tide Lord persists for 1 hour after it leaves the area.
- **Ice Stride:** As above.
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Tide Lords make the Glacial Aura genuinely punishing — Frosted creatures within 15 feet immediately become Frozen, which means any enemy who has taken one hit from the Tide Lord and remains adjacent is automatically Restrained by the aura alone. Tidal Ice Lance applies cold conditions across entire lines of enemies simultaneously. Abyssal Freeze at Margin 3 begins Engulfing, encasing targets in ice rather than earth. A summoner deploying one against a formation will find the formation frozen — in every literal and tactical sense — within two rounds of engagement.

---

## Ice Titan
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Nephilim (Ice)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 7 (ancient glacial flesh)
**Speed:** 40 ft (ignores ice and snow movement penalties)
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 4 / Dex 6 / Int 6 / Wis 6 / Cha 5 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Athletics 7, Perception 7, Intimidate 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to cold damage. Resistance to non-magical piercing and slashing damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **World Freeze [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Huge, standard: 12 + 2) + 10 cold damage (Half DR); target Frozen + Prone; no save
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 10 cold damage; Frozen + Prone + Grappled + Restrained; ongoing 16 cold damage per round; no save; Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes) each round to break free
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 10 cold damage + immediately Engulfed in ice; Blinded + Restrained + ongoing 24 cold damage; Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as full [Combat] action to escape, or ally must melt or break free (2 Interact actions with fire or 3 without)
- **Glacial Barrage [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 6 + Ranged Combat 6), Range: 120 ft, up to 3 targets within 30 feet of each other
  - Per target: Net 1: 20 cold damage (Half DR) + Frosted. Net 2: 32 cold damage + Frozen + movement halved. Net 3: 32 cold damage + Frozen + Prone; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Absolute Zero Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 20 feet take 10 cold damage (Half DR). Frosted creatures in this range become Frozen. Frozen creatures in this range take an additional 8 cold damage (Half DR) from the intensifying cold.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Permafrost:** Extended to 40 feet; persists for 8 hours after the Ice Titan leaves.
- **Ice Stride:** As above.
- **Cold Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 3 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical cold damage within 60 feet.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** Ice Titans apply Frozen on any hit at Margin 1 — there is no preliminary Chilled or Numbed step. Absolute Zero Aura compounds existing cold conditions automatically, meaning Frozen enemies adjacent to the Ice Titan take additional damage from the aura every round on top of whatever the Titan is actively doing to them. Glacial Barrage applies Frozen to multiple targets simultaneously at range. A summoner who has a Cooperative Ice Titan targeting a formation will find that formation effectively unable to take offensive action within two rounds — too cold, too slow, too Restrained to threaten anyone who isn't also standing in the aura.

---

## Worldsea Colossus
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Nephilim (Ice)
**Size:** Huge
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 8 (primordial glacial flesh)
**Speed:** 40 ft (ignores ice and snow movement penalties)
**Attributes:** Str 8 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 7 / Int 7 / Wis 7 / Cha 6 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Athletics 8, Perception 8, Intimidate 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Blindsight 60 ft (cold detection)
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Nephilim (Giant) — Immune to cold damage. Resistance to non-magical piercing and slashing damage (+2 DR). Powerful Build. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Glacial Apocalypse [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 20 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 16 damage (Huge, heavy: 14 + 2) + 12 cold damage (Half DR); target immediately Frozen + Prone; no save
  - *Margin 2:* 24 damage (16 + 8 Str) + 12 cold damage; immediately Engulfed in ice; Blinded + Grappled + Restrained; ongoing 28 cold damage per round; no save; Might check (Hard task, 2 successes) as full [Combat] action each round to escape
  - *Margin 3:* 24 damage + 12 cold damage + Engulfed; escape requires Might check with Misfortune, or ally intervention (4 [Interact] actions with fire, 6 without); ongoing damage increases to 40
- **World Ice Storm [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 7 + Ranged Combat 8), Range: 200 ft, 30-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 28 cold damage (Half DR) + Frozen + Prone. Net 2: 48 cold damage + Frozen + Prone + Restrained for 1 round. Net 3: 48 cold damage + Frozen + Prone + Restrained + Stunned until end of their next turn; no save on any effect.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Primordial Cold Aura:** Creatures starting their turn within 25 feet take 14 cold damage (Half DR). Frosted creatures become Frozen. Frozen creatures take additional 12 cold damage and become Restrained. Restrained creatures take additional 8 cold damage as ice continues accumulating.
- **World Glaciation (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, releases the cold of the world's deepest ice in an 80-foot diameter. All non-designated creatures make a Fortitude save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: 56 cold damage + Frozen for 1 hour + Restrained for 1 hour; escape requires fire or an ally's sustained effort. 1 success: 28 damage + Frozen for 1 minute. 2 successes: 14 damage only. The radius becomes permanent permafrost until magically cleared.
- **Cold Immunity Sharing:** The summoner and up to 6 designated allies gain immunity to non-magical cold damage within 60 feet.
- **Powerful Build.**
- **Permafrost:** Permanent within 50 feet while present; persists for 24 hours after departure.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** A Worldsea Colossus does not freeze things. It converts the local environment into ice and then continues from there. World Glaciation on arrival creates permanent permafrost across an 80-foot diameter and Restrains everything within it for an hour. Primordial Cold Aura compounds cold conditions through multiple stages automatically — a Restrained enemy in the aura takes 34 cold damage per round from aura effects alone before the Colossus attacks them. Glacial Apocalypse Engulfs at Margin 2 with no save. A summoner who calls one has determined that the fight ends in ice, and what the Worldsea Colossus determines is where the ice begins.

---
# Fae

Fae are creatures of the elemental planes whose courts have spread across those realms over millennia. They are not defined by a single element — a Fae may be found in the courts of Fire as readily as in the courts of Water, and the same creature may have allegiances that span multiple planes simultaneously. What defines them is not their element but their nature: mischievous, capricious, bound by ancient rules of obligation and exchange that mortals rarely understand completely and almost never understand in time.

Fae honor the letter of agreements with absolute precision and the spirit of them with considerable flexibility. A summoner who gives a Fae imprecise instructions will receive precise execution of something other than what they intended. This is not malice — it is the Fae's fundamental relationship with language, which they treat as a medium for exact meaning rather than approximate communication. A Fae told to "deal with" an enemy has been given genuine latitude to interpret "deal with" however seems most interesting.

Low-tier Fae are mischievous and small, their power more disruptive than destructive. Mid-tier Fae are capable combatants and considerably more alien in their reasoning. High-tier Fae are beings of genuine power whose cooperation represents a significant advantage and whose displeasure tends to persist across multiple encounters, multiple years, and occasionally multiple generations.

Pure Fae have no inherent moral orientation. Corrupted Fae — those that have spent extended time near Negative energy ley lines — are a different matter and are noted where relevant.

**Creature Type: Fey**
All Fae share: Fortune on saving throws against charm effects. Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep in the conventional sense — they sustain themselves on elemental energy and the ambient magic of whatever plane they currently inhabit.

---

## Wisp
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Fae (Water)
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 8 (Con 2 × 4, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 40 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Perception 3, Stealth 4, Deception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fey — Fortune on saves vs charm effects. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Mote Sting [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 1), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 1 damage; target must make Will save (1 success) or become briefly distracted — adds 1 to one die on their next action
  - *Margin 2:* 1 damage; distraction applies with no save; target also drops any item they were holding loosely

**Special Abilities:**
- **Blink Light:** The Wisp can appear to be a torch, candle, or lantern to casual observation. Creatures actively examining it make a Perception check (Hard task, 2 successes) to recognize it as something other than a light source. It can vary its brightness from dim to moderately bright at will.
- **Invisibility (At-Will):** As a [Minor] action, the Wisp becomes invisible. Invisibility ends if it attacks or uses Blink Light to produce bright illumination.
- **Lead Astray:** When a creature is following the Wisp believing it to be a light source, the Wisp can guide them in any direction. The creature makes a Wisdom check (1 success) each minute to realize they are being led rather than following a fixed light. This ability only works on creatures who have not identified the Wisp as a Fae.

**Description:** Wisps are navigational hazards given will. In wilderness or dungeon environments they lead travelers in circles, away from their destinations, or toward something the Wisp finds interesting — which may or may not align with the traveler's interests. A summoner who calls one is acquiring a scout with a strong editorial opinion about where scouting should happen and what constitutes relevant information. Precise instructions, carefully worded, will be followed. Vague instructions will be interpreted. The Wisp will report back whatever it decided was worth reporting.

---

## Sprite
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Fae (Earth)
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 12 (Con 2 × 6, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 20 ft, Fly 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 5 / Int 3 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Perception 4, Stealth 4, Ranged Combat 4, Wilderness 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fey — Fortune on saves vs charm effects. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Shortbow [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 40/80 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 2 damage; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains Poisoned (Weak) for 1 minute from the needle-tip
  - *Margin 2:* 2 damage; target gains Poisoned (Weak) for 1 hour; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 2 damage; target gains Poisoned (Strong) for 1 hour; no save; target also gains the Slowed (Minor) condition for 1 minute as the poison affects their coordination

**Special Abilities:**
- **Heart Sight:** Once per encounter when the Sprite looks directly into a creature's eyes within 30 feet, it automatically discerns that creature's emotional state and whether they are currently speaking a deliberate lie. The Sprite can communicate this to the summoner as a [Free] action on its next turn.
- **Nature's Ally:** The Sprite communicates with beasts and plants as if sharing a language. Plants convey recent events in their vicinity; beasts describe what they have seen or sensed. The information is accurate but filtered through each creature's limited perspective.
- **Diminutive Target:** Attacks against the Sprite add 1 to both dice due to its tiny size.

**Description:** Sprites are scouts and poison delivery systems. They shoot from concealment, apply poison conditions, and retreat before retaliation. Heart Sight makes them genuinely valuable as truth-detection assets — a summoner who needs to know whether an NPC is lying during a negotiation and has a Cooperative Sprite available has an advantage that most participants in the negotiation will not notice. Nature's Ally extends their intelligence-gathering to the natural environment. A summoner who understands what Sprites are good at will use them for information, not damage.

---

## Boggart
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Fae (Air)
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 27 (Con 3 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 2 (thick hide)
**Speed:** 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Stealth 4, Deception 3, Intimidate 3, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Fey — Fortune on saves vs charm effects. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Claws [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 5 damage (Small, standard: 6 − 1)
  - *Margin 2:* 9 damage (5 + 4 Str); target makes Will save (1 success) or gains Frightened condition until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 9 damage; Frightened condition; no save; target also gains Disoriented until end of their next turn as the Boggart's appearance burns into their perception

**Special Abilities:**
- **Frightful Visage:** As a [Combat] action, the Boggart distorts its face into something fundamentally wrong. One creature within 30 feet that can see it makes a Will save (opposed by Cha 3 + Intimidate 3). On failure, target gains Frightened until end of their next turn.
- **Shadow Meld:** In dim light or darkness, the Boggart has Fortune on Stealth checks.
- **Troublemaker:** Once per encounter, the Boggart can spend 1 minute interacting with an unattended object to sabotage it in a minor way — a door latch that sticks, a buckle that releases under pressure, a torch that goes out at the worst moment. The GM determines when the sabotage activates. The Boggart cannot sabotage magical items.

**Description:** Boggarts ambush from shadows, apply Frightened conditions through Frightful Visage to scatter formation fighters, then close for claw strikes on isolated targets. They are selfish and not suicidal — a Boggart that is clearly losing will attempt to flee unless held by Cooperative or Friendly disposition. Troublemaker is their most distinctively Fae ability, producing minor environmental sabotage that compounds the chaos of an encounter in ways that are difficult to anticipate. A summoner who wants a fight disrupted rather than won directly will find Boggarts more effective than their TR suggests.

---

## Redcap
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Fae (Fire)
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 40 (Con 5 × 8, Tough)
**DR:** S: 3, P: 2, B: 4 (dense body and iron-soled boots)
**Speed:** 35 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 5 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 2 / Cha 3 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Intimidate 4, Athletics 3, Perception 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Fey — Fortune on saves vs charm effects. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Scythe [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage [Slashing]
  - *Margin 2:* 13 damage (8 + 5 Str) [Slashing]; target gains 1 Bleeding stack
  - *Margin 3:* 13 damage + 2 Bleeding stacks; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or movement speed reduced by 10 until the Bleeding is removed
- **Boot Stomp [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft — only usable against Prone targets
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage [Bludgeoning]
  - *Margin 2:* 13 damage [Bludgeoning]; target Pinned until the Redcap moves away
  - *Margin 3:* 13 damage + Pinned; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains 1 Exhaustion level from the impact

**Special Abilities:**
- **Blood Thirst:** The Redcap's cap must be soaked in fresh blood or it loses its power. When the Redcap deals a Bleeding stack to any creature, it gains temporary HP equal to 4. This is both its motivation and its obsession — a Redcap given no targets will eventually find some. A summoner who calls one and then gives it nothing to fight will find it has made its own decisions about target selection within 1 round.
- **Iron Boots:** The Redcap's kicks and stomps deal full damage to constructs that would otherwise be immune to bludgeoning damage.

**Description:** Redcaps charge the most vulnerable target they can reach, stack Bleeding as quickly as possible, and stomp downed targets with their iron boots.
