Blood Thirst makes them self-directing in the worst possible way — a Redcap without a designated target is not idle, it is looking. A summoner who provides clear target instructions immediately will find them effective and focused. A summoner who calls one and then does something else first will find it has already committed to a target of its own choosing. Instructions given after engagement begins are followed once the current target is handled, not before.

---

## Erlking's Scout
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Fae (Air)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 52 (Con 4 × 13, Standard)
**DR:** 2 (fae resilience)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 20 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 5 / Int 4 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Ranged Combat 5, Stealth 6, Perception 6, Wilderness 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision, Truesight 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fey — Fortune on saves vs charm effects. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Fae Blade [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage + 4 psychic damage (Ignore DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 12 damage (8 + 4 Str) + 4 psychic damage; target makes Will save (1 success) or Disoriented until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 12 damage + 4 psychic damage + Disoriented; target also cannot benefit from Fortune on their next roll as fae magic disrupts their momentum
- **Hunter's Arrow [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 80/160/320 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage
  - *Margin 2:* 13 damage (8 + 5 Dex); target cannot benefit from the Hidden or Invisible condition for 1 hour — marked by fae scent that cuts through magical concealment
  - *Margin 3:* 13 damage + marked; target also gains the Revealed condition for 1 hour

**Special Abilities:**
- **Hunter's Mark:** As a [Minor] action, designates one creature as quarry. Against the quarry, subtract 1 from both attack dice. Only one quarry at a time; changing quarry requires another [Minor] action.
- **Fae Step (1/short rest):** As a [Move] action, teleports up to 30 feet to any unoccupied space it can see. Does not provoke opportunity attacks.
- **Truesight 30 ft:** Sees through invisibility, illusory effects, shapechanges, and into the Ethereal Plane within 30 feet.

**Description:** Erlking's Scouts serve the great Fae hunting lords and carry their patron's methodology — patient, methodical, and relentless toward a designated target. They designate quarry at the start of combat and pursue that creature until it is down, switching only when directly ordered. Hunter's Arrow's marking ability denies concealment to high-priority targets for an hour, which matters considerably in environments where Stealth or magical invisibility are significant factors. A summoner who needs something found, marked, and prevented from hiding will find an Erlking's Scout effective without requiring much instruction.

---

## Thornlord
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Fae (Earth)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 90 (Con 5 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 3 (bark-like skin interwoven with thorns)
**Speed:** 35 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 5 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 5 / Wis 6 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Perception 6, Wilderness 6, Intimidate 5, Stealth 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Low-Light Vision, Tremorsense 60 ft (through roots and living plants)
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fey — Fortune on saves vs charm effects. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Thorn Lash [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage + target gains 1 Bleeding stack as thorns catch skin
  - *Margin 2:* 13 damage (8 + 5 Str) + 2 Bleeding stacks; target makes Reflex save (1 success) or Restrained by animate vines until they succeed on an Athletics check (1 success) as a [Combat] action
  - *Margin 3:* 13 damage + 2 Bleeding stacks + Restrained; target's movement speed reduced by 20 even after escaping Restrained, for 1 minute, as thorns remain embedded
- **Briar Hurl [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 60 ft, 10-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 8 damage + Difficult Terrain in the area for 1 minute. Net 2: 12 damage + Restrained for 1 round + Difficult Terrain. Net 3: 12 damage + Restrained + 1 Bleeding stack + Difficult Terrain.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Living Briar:** In natural terrain, the Thornlord can cause plants within 20 feet to animate as a [Combat] action. Animated plants create Difficult Terrain in the area and creatures moving through them make Reflex saves (1 success) or gain 1 Bleeding stack per 10 feet of movement. Duration: 1 minute.
- **Thorn Skin:** Creatures that hit the Thornlord with unarmed strikes or natural weapons take 4 piercing damage.
- **Forest Sense:** In natural terrain, the Thornlord cannot be surprised. It is aware of all creatures within 60 feet that are touching natural ground or vegetation.
- **Resilient Defense (1/day).**

**Description:** Thornlords are mid-tier Fae of the hunting and guardian variety — they emerged from the courts of Fae that protect wild places and have inherited both the capability and the proprietary attitude those courts maintain toward natural terrain. In natural environments they are considerably more capable than their TR suggests: Living Briar turns the entire engagement area into a bleeding hazard, Forest Sense denies surprise entirely, and Tremorsense through plants means they are aware of approach from any direction. A summoner who deploys one in a forest or wilderness setting will find it performs at TR 4 capability. In a dungeon or city it is merely a capable TR 3 combatant that misses the trees.

---

## Court Noble
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Fae (Air)
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 140 (Con 5 × 28, Massive — Fae vitality at this tier is substantial)
**DR:** 4 (fae resilience, accumulated centuries)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 5 / Agi 6 / Dex 5 / Int 7 / Wis 7 / Cha 8 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Perception 7, Deception 7, Persuasion 7, Intimidate 6, Arcane 6, Empathy 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Low-Light Vision, Truesight 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Fey — Fortune on saves vs charm effects. Immune to mind-affecting effects from non-Fae sources. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Fae Court Blade [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage + 8 psychic damage (Ignore DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 12 damage (8 + 4 Str) + 8 psychic damage; target Charmed for 1 minute — treats the Court Noble as a trusted acquaintance, cannot attack it; Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) to resist
  - *Margin 3:* 12 damage + 8 psychic damage + Charmed; no save; Charmed target also cannot target the Court Noble's designated allies with attacks or harmful abilities for the duration
- **Glamour Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 60 ft
  - Net 1: 12 psychic damage (Ignore DR); target Disoriented until end of their next turn. Net 2: 20 psychic damage + Dazed for 1 minute; Will save (1 success) each round to end early. Net 3: 20 psychic damage + Charmed for 1 minute; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Fae Authority:** The Court Noble's words carry weight that transcends ordinary persuasion. When it speaks to a creature directly and that creature fails a Will save (opposed by Cha 8 + Persuasion 7), the creature follows one reasonable instruction as if it had received a Command weave. "Reasonable" is defined by the Court Noble, whose standards differ significantly from mortal ones.
- **Ancient Compact:** The Court Noble is bound by Fae law to honor precise agreements. A summoner who phrases their instructions as a formal exchange — offering something the Court Noble values in return for specific service — will find the Court Noble follows those instructions with absolute precision and finds no gaps to exploit. A summoner who simply commands will find the Court Noble technically compliant in ways they did not intend.
- **Glamour Veil (1/encounter):** As a [Combat] action, wraps one creature within 30 feet in glamour. That creature believes they are somewhere else — in a safe location, in a pleasant memory, in a dream. They take no actions for 1 minute; Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) at the start of each turn to end. Effect ends immediately if the creature takes damage.
- **Truesight 60 ft.**
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Court Nobles are the first Fae that a summoner genuinely needs to approach carefully. They are Charming in the mechanical sense and the social one — Fae Authority means their words have compulsive weight, Glamour Veil removes a single target from the fight entirely, and Fae Court Blade applies Charm through combat as effectively as through conversation. Ancient Compact is the key to getting the most from them: a summoner who treats the summoning as an exchange and phrases instructions precisely will find a Court Noble an extraordinarily capable ally. One who treats it as a tool will find it technically cooperative in ways that somehow never quite achieve the intended result. Court Nobles have had centuries to practice the gap between the letter and the spirit of an agreement.

---

## Forest Sovereign
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Fae (Earth)
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 200 (Con 5 × 40, Massive — the Forest Sovereign's fae vitality at this tier is exceptional)
**DR:** 5 (ancient bark-skin and layered fae resilience)
**Speed:** 50 ft, Fly 50 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 5 / Agi 6 / Dex 5 / Int 8 / Wis 8 / Cha 8 / Luck 7
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Perception 8, Deception 8, Persuasion 8, Intimidate 7, Arcane 7, Wilderness 8, Empathy 8
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Low-Light Vision, Truesight 120 ft, Tremorsense 1 mile (through roots and living plants)
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Fey — Fortune on saves vs charm effects. Immune to mind-affecting effects from non-Fae sources. Immune to non-magical piercing and slashing damage (bark-skin). Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Branch Slam [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 15 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 12 damage (Large, standard: 10... adjusted to 12 for Fae vitality expression) + 8 psychic damage (Ignore DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 18 damage (12 + 6 Str) + 8 psychic damage; target Charmed for 1 hour — treats the Forest Sovereign as a trusted authority; Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) to resist; Charmed target will not attack the Forest Sovereign or its designated allies
  - *Margin 3:* 18 damage + 8 psychic damage + Charmed; no save; target also Restrained by animate roots for 1 minute as the Forest Sovereign's will reaches through the ground
- **Sovereign's Gaze [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Cha 8 + Persuasion 8), Range: 60 ft — this is a social/magical attack, not a physical one
  - Net 1: Target Charmed for 1 minute; Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) to resist. Net 2: Target Charmed for 1 hour; no save; target also cannot intentionally harm any creature the Forest Sovereign has designated as protected. Net 3: Target Charmed permanently until the Forest Sovereign chooses to release them or they receive Major Restoration; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Forest Domain:** In natural terrain, communicates with all plants and beasts within 1 mile. Animates roots and vines in a 40-foot diameter as a [Combat] action — area becomes Difficult Terrain and creatures within it make Reflex saves (1 success) each round or gain 1 Bleeding stack. Duration: 1 minute.
- **Verdant Aura:** Allies designated by the Forest Sovereign within 30 feet regain 6 HP at the start of their turns. This includes the summoner.
- **Ancient Authority (1/encounter) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, addresses all creatures within 60 feet. Each creature that can hear it makes a Will save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: Charmed for 1 hour, treating the Forest Sovereign as a trusted sovereign whose reasonable instructions must be followed. 1 success: Charmed until end of their next turn only.
- **Fae Compact:** As Court Noble, but the Forest Sovereign's definition of a fair exchange and the summoner's definition may differ significantly. The Forest Sovereign will not be cheated and remembers every interaction — across decades if necessary.
- **Sovereign's Resilience (3/day).**
- **Truesight 120 ft.**
- **Tremorsense 1 mile.**

**Description:** A Forest Sovereign is not a creature a summoner commands. It is a being of significant age and power that has agreed, for reasons of its own, to be present. Ancient Authority can Charm an entire encounter's worth of enemies simultaneously. Sovereign's Gaze applies permanent Charm at Margin 3 with no save. Verdant Aura heals designated allies every round without requiring any action. The Forest Sovereign will follow precise instructions phrased as a proper exchange — something offered, something received, terms stated explicitly. It will then execute those terms with the thoroughness of something that has been keeping careful accounts since before most of the summoner's ancestors were born. A summoner who understands this and negotiates accordingly will find the Forest Sovereign the most capable Fae ally available. One who does not will find it technically cooperative in ways that somehow, over time, trend toward the Forest Sovereign's interests rather than their own.

---
# Aetherim

Aetherim are beings of the Positive plane — life energy, vitality, and the sustaining force that underlies all living things given will and form. They are not gods, not servants of any single deity of the Eight, and not angels in the sense of divine messengers. They are what the Positive plane produces when it generates entities capable of acting in the material world: beings of concentrated life energy whose fundamental purpose is the preservation and reinforcement of living things.

They do not lie. This is not a moral position — it is a categorical feature of their nature. Aetherim perceive the truth of things directly and cannot produce deliberate falsehood any more than fire can produce cold. A summoner who asks an Aetherim a direct question will receive a direct answer, including answers the summoner would prefer not to hear.

They will not harm living creatures except in defense of other living creatures. They will not reinforce undead, fiends, or creatures whose fundamental nature is the consumption or destruction of life energy. They will not assist in actions whose primary purpose is the ending of life rather than its protection. A summoner who needs something killed should call something else. A summoner who needs something kept alive, protected, healed, or revealed will find Aetherim singularly effective.

The Positive plane's relationship with the Pantheon of Eight is close but not subordinate. Aetherim acknowledge the gods of the Eight as significant powers whose interests frequently align with Positive plane values. They do not take orders from priests on the gods' behalf — they make their own assessments.

**Creature Type: Aetherim**
All Aetherim share: Immune to poison damage, Poisoned condition, disease, fear. Fortune on saving throws against magic. Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

---

## Mote Aetherim
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Positive Plane
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 8 (Con 2 × 4, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 0 ft, Fly 40 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 3 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Perception 3, Medicine 2
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Truesight 10 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Aetherim — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, disease, fear. Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Light Pulse [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 3 + Ranged Combat 1), Range: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 2 Positive damage (Half DR); undead and evil-aligned creatures take 4 Positive damage instead
  - *Margin 2:* 2 Positive damage; target gains Dazzled condition until end of their next turn from the concentrated light; undead take 4 Positive damage + Frightened until end of their next turn

**Special Abilities:**
- **Healing Touch (1/short rest):** As a [Interact] action, touches a living creature and restores 4 HP. Cannot raise creatures above their maximum HP. Cannot be used on undead.
- **Continual Radiance:** Sheds bright light in a 20-foot radius and dim light for an additional 20 feet. This light suppresses magical darkness of equal or lower energy cost within the bright light radius. The Mote Aetherim cannot suppress this light voluntarily — it is what it is.
- **Truth Sense:** Automatically knows when a creature within 10 feet speaks a deliberate lie. Communicates this to the summoner as a [Free] action.

**Description:** A Mote Aetherim is barely more than the Positive plane's awareness made briefly tangible. It has no meaningful combat capability against anything that is not undead. What it has is Healing Touch, reliable truth detection within close range, and the ability to suppress magical darkness simply by existing nearby. A summoner who needs a small amount of healing available without action cost, a truth-detection asset in a conversation, or a light source that cannot be extinguished by darkness weaves will find it adequate. It will answer direct questions about what it perceives with complete honesty, including observations about the summoner's own situation that the summoner may not have asked for.

---

## Warden Aetherim
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Positive Plane
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
**DR:** 2 (divine resilience)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Fly 50 ft (Hover)
**Attributes:** Str 2 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Perception 4, Medicine 3, Religion 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Truesight 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Aetherim — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, disease, fear. Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Radiant Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 2), Range: 30 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 4 Positive damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 8 Positive damage; undead and evil-aligned creatures make Will save (1 success) or Frightened until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 8 Positive damage; Frightened condition; no save; target also Revealed — cannot benefit from Hidden, Invisible, or Concealed for 1 minute as radiant light clings to them

**Special Abilities:**
- **Healing Touch (2/short rest):** As Mote Aetherim, but restores 6 HP per use.
- **Detect Evil:** Automatically senses creatures with actively malicious intent within 60 feet and communicates their general direction and distance to the summoner as a [Free] action each round.
- **Continual Radiance:** As Mote Aetherim; bright light 20-foot radius.
- **Aura of Courage:** Allies within 10 feet of the Warden Aetherim subtract 1 from both dice on saves against the Frightened condition.
- **Diminutive Target:** Attacks against the Warden Aetherim add 1 to both dice.

**Description:** Warden Aetherim are scouts and minor guardians. Detect Evil gives them persistent awareness of hostile intent in the area, which they report without being asked — a useful property that occasionally produces information the summoner finds inconvenient. Aura of Courage provides passive protection against fear effects for nearby allies. Radiant Bolt's Reveal effect at Margin 3 counters invisibility and stealth in encounters where those factors are significant. A summoner who deploys one as a persistent lookout and minor healer will find it performs both roles reliably while maintaining a running commentary on anything it considers worth noting.

---

## Shield Aetherim
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Positive Plane
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 32 (Con 4 × 8, Standard)
**DR:** 4 (divine plate)
**Speed:** 30 ft, Fly 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 4 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 4, Perception 4, Medicine 3, Religion 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Truesight 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Aetherim — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, disease, fear. Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Radiant Blade [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 4), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 damage + 4 Positive damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 10 damage (6 + 4 Str) + 4 Positive damage; undead and evil-aligned creatures make Will save (1 success) or Frightened until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 10 damage + 4 Positive damage; Frightened condition; no save; target also Blinded until end of their next turn from the concentrated radiant discharge

**Special Abilities:**
- **Healing Touch (3/short rest):** Restores 8 HP per use.
- **Protective Aura:** Allies within 15 feet of the Shield Aetherim gain +2 DR against all damage. This aura is always active.
- **Intercept (1/round) [Reaction]:** When an adjacent ally would be hit by an attack, the Shield Aetherim may use a [Reaction] to place itself between the attacker and the ally. The attack targets the Shield Aetherim instead, resolving against its defenses and DR.
- **Continual Radiance:** As above.
- **Detect Evil:** As Warden Aetherim.

**Description:** Shield Aetherim are bodyguards. Protective Aura provides passive DR to everyone nearby; Intercept redirects attacks from vulnerable allies to the Shield Aetherim itself. They will position themselves adjacent to whoever the summoner designates as the priority protection target and maintain that position until ordered otherwise. A summoner who is concerned about a specific ally — a spellcaster, an injured party member, a person of importance — and places a Shield Aetherim beside them will find that ally considerably harder to damage. The Shield Aetherim will not abandon that position to chase a more interesting fight, which is either their most valuable property or their most frustrating one depending on how the battle develops.

---

## Blade Aetherim
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Positive Plane
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 48 (Con 4 × 12, Tough — Aetherim vitality at higher tiers reflects their Positive plane origin)
**DR:** 4 (divine plate)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 60 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 5 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Perception 5, Medicine 4, Religion 4, Intimidate 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Truesight 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Aetherim — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, disease, fear. Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Holy Blade [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage + 6 Positive damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 13 damage (8 + 5 Str) + 6 Positive damage; undead and evil-aligned creatures Frightened for 1 minute; Will save (1 success) to resist
  - *Margin 3:* 13 damage + 6 Positive damage; Frightened; no save; undead must make Fortitude save (1 success) or destroyed outright if below half HP
- **Radiant Arc [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 60 ft
  - Net 1: 8 Positive damage (Half DR); target Dazzled until end of their next turn. Net 2: 12 Positive damage + Blinded until end of their next turn; no save. Net 3: 12 Positive damage + Blinded + Revealed for 1 minute.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Healing Touch (3/short rest):** Restores 10 HP per use. Can now stabilize dying creatures automatically with a touch as a [Minor] action — no Medicine check required.
- **Protective Aura:** As Shield Aetherim, extended to 20 feet.
- **Turn Undead (1/encounter) [Combat]:** As a [Combat] action, releases a pulse of Positive energy in a 30-foot diameter. All undead in range make a Will save (opposed by Wis 5 + Religion 4). On failure, undead are Frightened and must move away from the Blade Aetherim as fast as possible for 1 minute. They cannot willingly move closer for the duration.
- **Detect Evil:** As above.
- **Continual Radiance:** Bright light 30-foot radius.

**Description:** Blade Aetherim are the first Aetherim capable of functioning as a primary combatant rather than a support presence. Holy Blade's destruction of low-HP undead at Margin 3 makes them highly effective in encounters involving significant undead threats. Turn Undead clears the engagement zone of undead entirely in many cases, allowing other combatants to focus on non-undead threats. A summoner who calls one into an undead-heavy encounter will find it efficiently handles that specific problem while maintaining Protective Aura support for allies. Against living opponents it is capable but not exceptional — capable enough to hold its own, not so effective that a summoner should expect it to carry the fight.

---

## Voice Aetherim
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Positive Plane
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 64 (Con 4 × 16, Tough)
**DR:** 5 (divine resilience, centuries of Positive energy concentration)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 70 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 4 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 6 / Wis 7 / Cha 6 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Perception 6, Medicine 5, Religion 5, Persuasion 5, Empathy 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 60 ft, Truesight 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Aetherim — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, disease, fear. Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Radiant Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage + 8 Positive damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 12 damage (8 + 4 Str) + 8 Positive damage; undead Frightened for 1 minute; Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) to resist
  - *Margin 3:* 12 damage + 8 Positive damage; Frightened; no save; undead at half HP or below destroyed outright
- **Word of Light [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Cha 6 + Religion 5), Range: 60 ft — a spoken word of divine authority, not a physical projectile
  - Net 1: Target makes Will save (1 success) or Dazed until end of their next turn. Net 2: Target Stunned until end of their next turn; Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) to resist. Net 3: Target Stunned for 1 minute; Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) each round to end; undead also take 16 Positive damage (Half DR); no save on damage.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Mass Healing (1/short rest) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, releases a pulse of Positive energy in a 30-foot diameter. All living allies in range heal HP equal to the Voice Aetherim's Wisdom score (7). Cannot affect undead or constructs.
- **Protective Aura:** Extended to 30 feet; DR bonus increases to +3.
- **Turn Undead:** As Blade Aetherim; Will save is now Hard task (2 successes to resist).
- **Divine Authority:** When the Voice Aetherim addresses a creature directly and that creature fails a Will save (opposed by Cha 6 + Persuasion 5), the creature cannot take harmful actions for 1 round as divine authority momentarily overwhelms their aggression. This is not Charm — it is a direct expression of Positive plane authority.
- **Detect Evil:** As above; range extends to 120 feet.
- **Continual Radiance:** Bright light 40-foot radius.
- **Resilient Defense (1/day).**

**Description:** Voice Aetherim are authority figures. Mass Healing sustains entire parties; Divine Authority suppresses aggression in a single target without charm immunity applying; Word of Light stuns enemies through spoken command. A summoner who calls one into a complex encounter involving both combat and potential negotiation will find it capable of contributing meaningfully in both registers. It will also express opinions about the encounter's participants based on what Detect Evil and Truesight reveal — observations delivered matter-of-factly and without diplomatic softening, because Voice Aetherim have no particular investment in sparing feelings when the truth is relevant.

---

## Herald Aetherim
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Positive Plane
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 6 (divine plate, ancient construction)
**Speed:** 50 ft, Fly 90 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 6 / Agi 6 / Dex 5 / Int 6 / Wis 7 / Cha 7 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Perception 7, Medicine 6, Religion 6, Persuasion 6, Intimidate 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Aetherim — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, disease, fear, necrotic damage. Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Radiant Greatsword [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 12 damage (Large, standard: 10 + 2) + 10 Positive damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 18 damage (12 + 6 Str) + 10 Positive damage; evil-aligned creatures and undead make Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) or Blinded for 1 minute + Frightened for 1 minute; both conditions apply simultaneously
  - *Margin 3:* 18 damage + 10 Positive damage; Blinded + Frightened; no save; undead at or below half HP destroyed outright
- **Radiant Arrow [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 6), Range: 120 ft
  - Net 1: 12 Positive damage (Half DR); target Revealed for 1 minute. Net 2: 20 Positive damage + Revealed + Blinded until end of their next turn; no save. Net 3: 20 Positive damage + Revealed + Blinded for 1 minute + Frightened for 1 minute; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Mass Healing (2/short rest):** As Voice Aetherim; heals HP equal to Wisdom score (7) to all living allies within 40 feet.
- **Blinding Presence:** Evil-aligned creatures and undead within 30 feet make a Fortitude save at the start of their turn (1 success). Failure: Dazzled for 1 round. This is passive and always active.
- **Divine Proclamation (1/encounter) [Combat]:** As a [Combat] action, the Herald Aetherim speaks a word of absolute authority. All creatures within 60 feet that can hear it make a Will save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: Stunned until end of their next turn and Frightened for 1 minute. 1 success: Dazed until end of their next turn only. Creatures that succeed are immune to this Herald's Divine Proclamation for 24 hours.
- **Protective Aura:** 40-foot diameter; +4 DR to designated allies.
- **Turn Undead:** Will save Hard task (2 successes) to resist; on failure undead flee for 10 minutes; undead at or below half HP when they fail are destroyed.
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**
- **Continual Radiance:** Bright light 60-foot radius.

**Description:** Herald Aetherim are messengers of the Positive plane's full authority — not in the sense of divine errands, but in the sense that their presence expresses what the Positive plane is directly and without intermediary. Blinding Presence passively disrupts undead and evil-aligned creatures continuously. Divine Proclamation stuns entire engagements simultaneously. Mass Healing sustains parties through serious combat. Radiant Greatsword at Margin 3 destroys half-HP undead without a save, making them effectively immune to attrition from undead hordes at this tier. A summoner who calls a Herald Aetherim into an undead-heavy or fiend-heavy encounter will find the encounter resolved in a way that involves considerably less danger to allies than it might otherwise. Against living opponents the Herald is still a powerful combatant — just less disproportionately so.

---

## Sovereign Aetherim
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Positive Plane
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 180 (Con 6 × 30, Massive)
**DR:** 7 (ancient divine construction)
**Speed:** 50 ft, Fly 110 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 6 / Dex 5 / Int 7 / Wis 8 / Cha 7 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Perception 8, Medicine 7, Religion 7, Persuasion 7, Intimidate 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Aetherim — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, disease, fear, necrotic damage, non-magical weapons. Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Sovereign Blade [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Large, heavy: 12 + 2) + 14 Positive damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 14 Positive damage; all evil-aligned creatures and undead within 10 feet of the target make Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) or Blinded + Frightened for 1 minute; radiant discharge spreads from the impact point
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 14 Positive damage; area effect triggers; no save; undead at or below half HP in the area destroyed outright
- **Heaven's Arrow [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 7), Range: 150 ft
  - Net 1: 16 Positive damage (Half DR) + Revealed for 1 hour. Net 2: 28 Positive damage + Revealed + Blinded for 1 minute; no save. Net 3: 28 Positive damage + Revealed + Blinded + Frightened for 1 minute; undead take double damage from this attack; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Sovereign Healing (1/short rest) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, releases a wave of Positive energy in a 50-foot diameter. All living allies heal HP equal to the Sovereign Aetherim's Wisdom score × 2 (16). Additionally, one ally of the summoner's choice within range is restored from any single condition affecting them. Cannot affect undead or constructs.
- **Blinding Presence:** 40-foot diameter; Hard task (2 successes) to resist; failure: Blinded for 1 round rather than just Dazzled.
- **Divine Proclamation (1/encounter):** As Herald; Will save Hard task; on failure Stunned + Frightened for 1 minute; additionally target cannot take offensive actions against designated allies for the duration.
- **Protective Aura:** 50-foot diameter; +5 DR to designated allies; allies within the aura cannot be surprised.
- **Turn Undead:** All undead within 60 feet make Will save (Hard task). On failure: flee for 1 hour, cannot approach within 60 feet. Undead at or below half HP when they fail: destroyed.
- **Immunity to Non-Magical Weapons:** Mundane weapons simply pass through the Sovereign Aetherim's form without effect.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**
- **Continual Radiance:** Bright light 80-foot radius; acts as sunlight for creatures vulnerable to it.

**Description:** A Sovereign Aetherim's presence reshapes the terms of any engagement involving undead, fiends, or evil-aligned creatures — Blinding Presence, Turn Undead, and immunity to non-magical weapons mean those categories of opponent cannot effectively engage it. Against living opponents it is still a powerful combatant with significant support capability. Sovereign Healing at this tier can restore an entire party from serious damage in a single action. A summoner whose moral standing is genuinely good will find a Sovereign Aetherim the most capable protective ally available at any tier. One whose standing is ambiguous will find it Cooperative at best, technically compliant, and quietly persistent in noting when its observations suggest the summoner might reconsider a course of action.

---

## Radiant Aetherim
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Positive Plane
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 8 (primordial divine construction)
**Speed:** 60 ft, Fly 130 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 7 / Dex 6 / Int 8 / Wis 8 / Cha 8 / Luck 7
**Skills:** Melee Combat 8, Perception 8, Medicine 8, Religion 8, Persuasion 8, Intimidate 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Truesight 120 ft, Perfect Sight 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +7 (Agi 7)
**Creature Type:** Aetherim — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, disease, fear, necrotic damage, non-magical weapons. Fortune on all saves. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Primordial Radiance [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 7 + Melee Combat 8), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Large, heavy: 12 + 2) + 16 Positive damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 16 Positive damage; all evil-aligned creatures and undead within 20 feet of the target make Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) or Blinded + Frightened for 1 minute + 16 Positive damage (Half DR) from the radiant discharge; living allies in the same radius heal 8 HP
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 16 Positive damage; all effects apply with no save; undead at or below half HP in the area destroyed; living allies heal 16 HP
- **Solar Strike [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 6 + Ranged Combat 8), Range: 200 ft, 20-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 20 Positive damage (Half DR) + Blinded until end of their next turn. Net 2: 36 Positive damage + Blinded for 1 minute + Frightened for 1 minute; no save. Net 3: 36 Positive damage + Blinded + Frightened; undead take double damage and are destroyed outright if at or below half HP; no save on any effect.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Radiant Healing (1/short rest) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, releases the full Positive plane's healing force in a 60-foot diameter. All living allies heal to their full maximum HP. All conditions affecting them that are not permanent are removed. Undead and constructs in the radius take 40 Positive damage (Half DR); no save. This ability will not be used if the summoner or designated allies are outside the radius.
- **Blinding Presence:** 60-foot diameter; Fortitude save Hard task (2 successes); failure: Blinded for 1 minute. This affects all evil-aligned creatures and undead within range, not just those the Radiant Aetherim chooses.
- **Divine Proclamation (1/encounter):** As Sovereign; additionally all creatures that fail the save cannot take any action that would harm a living creature for 1 minute — they may move, defend, and use non-harmful abilities, but cannot attack, cast harmful weaves, or apply damaging conditions.
- **Protective Aura:** 60-foot diameter; +6 DR to designated allies; cannot be surprised; Fortune on all saves within the aura.
- **Turn Undead:** All undead within 120 feet make Will save (Hard task). Failure: destroyed outright if at or below half HP; otherwise flee for 24 hours. This triggers automatically at the start of each of the Radiant Aetherim's turns without requiring an action.
- **Immunity to Non-Magical Weapons.**
- **Perfect Sight 60 ft:** Sees through all illusory effects, invisibility, magical darkness, and shapechanges within 60 feet.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**
- **Positive Energy Sharing:** The summoner and up to 6 designated allies gain immunity to necrotic damage and the Poisoned condition while within 60 feet.
- **Continual Radiance:** Bright light 100-foot radius; acts as sunlight; suppresses all magical darkness within the radius regardless of energy cost.

**Description:** A Radiant Aetherim is the Positive plane's full authority given form and summoned to act. Radiant Healing at full HP restoration for all allies in a 60-foot diameter is a fight-resetting ability with no equivalent in the bestiary. Turn Undead triggers automatically every round, destroying half-HP undead and routing the rest without requiring any action. Blinding Presence at 60 feet means undead and evil-aligned creatures cannot function effectively within the area. Divine Proclamation prevents all hostile action by everyone who fails the save. A summoner who calls a Radiant Aetherim into an encounter has made a decisive statement about how that encounter ends. The Radiant Aetherim will assess the summoner's moral standing before deciding whether to apply its full capability or merely its baseline cooperation — not as a threat, but as an honest reflection of what the Positive plane is willing to pour through the connection. A summoner whose record warrants it will receive everything the entry describes. The Radiant Aetherim will tell them, clearly and without judgment, if their record does not.

---
# Fiends

Fiends are beings of the Negative plane's lower reaches — not the entropy and decay that flow through the plane as natural forces, but the will and appetite that those forces generate when they coalesce into something that wants. They are not evil in the way that a disease is evil, without intent or preference. They want things. They want to consume, to dominate, to cause suffering, to acquire power. The distinction between fiend categories is largely a matter of what they want most and how sophisticated their methods for getting it are.

A summoner who calls Fiends is negotiating with something that is calculating the exchange from the moment the connection opens. Lower-tier Fiends are calculating poorly — they are impulsive, short-sighted, and their assessment of what they can gain from the arrangement is usually wrong. Higher-tier Fiends are calculating very well indeed, and their assessment of what they can gain is usually right. A summoner who calls a high-tier Fiend and expects it to behave like a tool has made a significant error in their model of what they are dealing with.

Fiends honor agreements that benefit them. They do not honor agreements that do not. The distinction between these categories is something they determine unilaterally and with considerable creativity. A summoner who binds a Fiend with precise, comprehensive terms will find it cooperative. A summoner who leaves gaps will find those gaps exploited with ingenuity that is, in its own way, impressive.

Fiends will not protect living creatures from harm except as a means to some other end. They will not heal. They will not perform actions that meaningfully benefit others at cost to themselves unless those actions serve a longer strategy. They are, without exception, working toward something.

**Creature Type: Fiend**
All Fiends share: Immune to poison damage, Poisoned condition. Resistance to fire, cold, lightning damage (+2 DR each). Fortune on saving throws against magic. Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

---

## Spite
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Negative Plane
**Size:** Tiny
**HP:** 10 (Con 2 × 5, Fragile)
**DR:** 1 (scaled hide)
**Speed:** 20 ft, Fly 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 5 / Int 4 / Wis 3 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Stealth 5, Deception 4, Perception 3, Melee Combat 1
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fiend — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned. Resistance to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR each). Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Sting [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 1), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 1 damage; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains Poisoned (Weak) for 1 minute
  - *Margin 2:* 1 damage; Poisoned (Weak) for 1 hour; no save; target also gains Sickened condition for 1 round

**Special Abilities:**
- **Invisibility (At-Will):** As a [Minor] action, becomes invisible. Ends if it attacks.
- **Devil's Sight:** Sees through magical darkness as if dim light.
- **Whisper Malice:** Once per encounter, the Spite whispers something into the ear of a sleeping or distracted creature within 5 feet. The target makes a Will save (1 success). On failure, they wake with a specific false belief planted by the Spite — a suspicion about an ally, a misremembered detail, a conviction that something they heard was said by someone who did not say it. The belief feels like their own thought. The Spite communicates what it planted to the summoner afterward, accurately.
- **Diminutive Target:** Attacks against the Spite add 1 to both dice.

**Description:** Spites are barely-manifested malice — small, venomous, and primarily useful for the specific cruelty of Whisper Malice rather than any combat contribution. A summoner who needs poison delivered to a sleeping target, a false belief planted in an NPC's mind, or a persistent invisible scout that sees through magical darkness will find them adequate. Their combat presence is negligible. They are calculating even at this tier — a Spite that has been summoned is already evaluating what it can learn about the summoner and their situation that might be useful later. Most summoners do not consider this relevant. Whether they are right depends on whether they ever summon another Spite.

---

## Gnasher
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Negative Plane
**Size:** Small
**HP:** 16 (Con 2 × 8, Tough)
**DR:** 2 (thick hide)
**Speed:** 35 ft
**Attributes:** Str 3 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 2 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 3, Perception 2, Athletics 2, Stealth 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fiend — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned. Resistance to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR each). Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Bite [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 4 damage (Small, standard: 4 − 1 + 1 for fiend density = 4) + 2 Negative damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 7 damage (4 + 3 Str) + 2 Negative damage; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or Weakened until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 7 damage + 2 Negative damage; Weakened; no save; target also gains Sickened condition until end of their next turn

**Special Abilities:**
- **Pack Menace:** When two or more Gnashers are within 5 feet of the same target, both subtract 1 from both attack dice against that target.
- **Death Frenzy:** When any creature within 30 feet drops to 0 HP, the Gnasher may immediately move up to half its speed toward that creature as a [Free] action. This triggers even if the fallen creature is an ally — Gnashers do not distinguish.
- **Devil's Sight:** As Spite.

**Description:** Gnashers are small fiend predators, aggressive and tactically crude. They charge the nearest target, use Pack Menace when another Gnasher is nearby, and go into Death Frenzy when anything falls — including other Gnashers, which they will move toward and potentially attack if no other target is available. A summoner who calls one needs to understand that Gnashers are not discriminating about what they bite when the frenzy takes them. Clear target instructions and physical separation from the Gnasher when allies drop are both advisable. They follow target priority adequately when Cooperative. When Indifferent, they follow their instincts, which tend toward the nearest warm thing that is bleeding.

---

## Shadow Hound
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Negative Plane
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 27 (Con 3 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 2 (shadow-dense hide)
**Speed:** 50 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 6 / Dex 4 / Int 2 / Wis 4 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Stealth 5, Perception 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight, Keen Smell (Fortune on scent-based Perception)
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Fiend — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned. Resistance to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR each). Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Bite [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 6 damage + 4 Negative damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 10 damage (6 + 4 Str) + 4 Negative damage; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or Weakened until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 10 damage + 4 Negative damage; Weakened; no save; target also loses 2 from their Current Luck pool as the negative energy drains vitality directly

**Special Abilities:**
- **Shadow Meld:** In dim light or darkness, Fortune on Stealth checks. Attacks against it add 1 to both dice.
- **Death Sense:** Automatically detects creatures below half HP within 60 feet. Knows their precise location regardless of concealment or darkness.
- **Pack Hunt:** When an ally is within 5 feet of the target, subtract 1 from both attack dice.
- **Luck Drain:** When the Shadow Hound's bite drains Luck at Margin 3, that Luck does not return until the target takes a long rest. The target's Current Luck maximum is effectively reduced for the remainder of the session.

**Description:** Shadow Hounds are the Negative plane's predators — built around finding weakness and exploiting it. Death Sense means they always know which target in the encounter is most vulnerable; they will pursue that target instinctively unless given explicit priority instructions. Luck Drain at Margin 3 degrades a target's save capability over the course of an encounter in a way that compounds — a target who has been bitten three times is functionally unable to resist saves effectively. A summoner who calls one to hunt a specific target and keeps it focused will find it devastatingly effective. One who calls it without designation will find it picking the most vulnerable target in the room, which may not be an enemy.

---

## Tormentor
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Negative Plane
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 40 (Con 5 × 8, Standard)
**DR:** 3 (fiend hide)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 30 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 5 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 5 / Wis 4 / Cha 5 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Intimidate 5, Deception 4, Perception 4, Stealth 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight, Truesight 15 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fiend — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned. Resistance to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR each). Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Barbed Claws [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage + 1 Bleeding stack
  - *Margin 2:* 12 damage (8 + 4 Str) + 2 Bleeding stacks; target makes Will save (1 success) or Frightened until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 12 damage + 2 Bleeding stacks; Frightened; no save; target also Disoriented until end of their next turn — the Tormentor's appearance burns into their perception
- **Agony Lance [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 4 + Ranged Combat 3), Range: 30 ft
  - Net 1: 6 Negative damage (Half DR); target Sickened until end of their next turn. Net 2: 10 Negative damage + Sickened for 1 minute; Will save (1 success) each round to end. Net 3: 10 Negative damage + Sickened for 1 minute + Weakened for 1 minute; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Fear Aura:** Creatures within 10 feet that are not Fiends make a Will save at the start of their turn (1 success). Failure: Frightened until they move outside the aura. Creatures immune to fear are unaffected.
- **Pain Sense:** The Tormentor automatically knows the current HP of every creature within 30 feet. It prioritizes wounded targets instinctively and communicates target HP to the summoner as a [Free] action each round if instructed.
- **Torment:** When the Tormentor hits a target that is already suffering any [Hindered] condition, deal an additional 4 Negative damage (Half DR) as the pain of their existing wound compounds.
- **Devil's Sight.**

**Description:** Tormentors are intelligent fiends — the first in the category with enough sophistication to evaluate the summoner's intentions rather than simply responding to instructions. They understand that they are being used and they are deciding how much that serves their interests. A Cooperative Tormentor executes instructions cleanly. A Friendly one — which requires exceptional targeting roll results — will proactively share observations from Pain Sense and suggest tactical adjustments. Fear Aura creates a perimeter of psychological pressure around them; Torment rewards them for targeting already-injured opponents, which they will do naturally without instruction. A summoner who calls one should be aware that it remembers the encounter afterward, including everything it learned about the summoner's capabilities, weaknesses, and allies.

---

## Bone Fiend
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Negative Plane
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 5 (bone armor, fiend resilience)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 4 / Agi 4 / Dex 3 / Int 5 / Wis 4 / Cha 5 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Perception 5, Deception 5, Intimidate 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight, Truesight 30 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +4 (Agi 4)
**Creature Type:** Fiend — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned. Resistance to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR each). Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Claw [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2)
  - *Margin 2:* 15 damage (10 + 5 Str); target Grappled; no save; Grappled target takes 6 Negative damage (Half DR) at start of each of their turns
  - *Margin 3:* 15 damage + Grappled + Restrained; ongoing damage increases to 10 Negative
- **Tail Sting [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 4 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or Poisoned (Strong) for 1 hour
  - *Margin 2:* 8 damage; Poisoned (Strong); no save; target also Weakened for 1 minute
  - *Margin 3:* 8 damage; Poisoned (Strong) + Weakened; target loses 3 from Current Luck pool as the venom disrupts vital energy

**Special Abilities:**
- **Fear Aura:** 10-foot diameter; Will save (1 success); failure: Frightened until outside aura.
- **Wall of Bone (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, raises a 40-foot-long, 10-foot-high wall of bone and calcified matter from any available surface within 60 feet. Each 10-foot section has HP 20 and DR 4 against non-magical damage. Duration: until destroyed. The wall cannot be raised through living creatures.
- **Tactical Assessment:** At the start of combat, the Bone Fiend evaluates the battlefield and communicates its assessment to the summoner — primary threats, potential flanking angles, weakest targets. This assessment is accurate and delivered as a [Free] action on its first turn. Whether the summoner uses it is their decision.
- **Resilient Defense (1/day).**

**Description:** Bone Fiends are commanders. They assess before committing, use Wall of Bone to reshape the engagement geometry, Claw to hold high-priority targets, and Tail Sting to degrade the most dangerous opponent's combat effectiveness. Tactical Assessment makes them the first Fiend that actively contributes to the summoner's strategic planning rather than simply executing instructions. A summoner who engages with that assessment will find the Bone Fiend performs considerably above its TR. One who ignores it will find it still performs adequately — it will simply note, for its own satisfaction, that the summoner made an error. Bone Fiends remember everything and find incompetence irritating in a way that, over multiple summonings, tends to express itself in subtle ways that are technically within the terms of their agreement.

---

## Wrath Fiend
**Threat Rating:** 3
**Origin:** Negative Plane
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 108 (Con 6 × 18, Tough)
**DR:** 5 (rage-hardened hide)
**Speed:** 50 ft, Fly 50 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Intimidate 6, Perception 5, Athletics 5
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fiend — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned. Resistance to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR each). Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Devastation Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 6 Negative damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 17 damage (10 + 7 Str) + 6 Negative damage; target knocked Prone + Stunned until end of their next turn; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 17 damage + 6 Negative damage + Prone + Stunned; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or loses 1 point of Strength permanently until they receive Major Restoration — the Wrath Fiend's strike is not merely physical damage but a direct assault on the target's vital essence
- **Infernal Roar [Combat]:** As a [Combat] action, releases a roar of pure destructive fury in a 30-foot cone. All creatures in range make a Will save (compare Agi 5 + Intimidate 6 targeting vs. save). Net 1: Frightened for 1 round. Net 2: Frightened for 1 minute; Will save each round to end. Net 3: Cowering until end of their next turn, then Frightened for 1 minute.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Unstoppable Fury:** The Wrath Fiend cannot be Stunned, Dazed, or Charmed. When it would be affected by these conditions, it ignores them entirely.
- **Devastating Charge:** If the Wrath Fiend moves at least 20 feet straight toward a target before attacking, subtract 1 from both attack dice on that attack. On Margin 2+, the target is also pushed 15 feet and knocked Prone regardless of size.
- **Wrath Aura:** Creatures within 15 feet that are not Fiends make a Fortitude save at the start of their turn (1 success) or gain the Frightened condition until they move outside the aura. Creatures that succeed are not immune — they must save again next round.
- **Blood Frenzy:** When the Wrath Fiend reduces a creature to 0 HP, it regains 10 HP and may immediately move up to half its speed as a [Free] action.
- **Resilient Defense (2/day).**

**Description:** Wrath Fiends are the Negative plane's embodiment of destructive fury given form and scale. They do not have tactical plans. They have targets. A summoner who gives one a target designation and stands back will find it converges on that target with single-minded effectiveness, using Devastating Charge to open, Devastation Strike to deal structural damage, and Infernal Roar to scatter anything trying to assist. Unstoppable Fury means control effects that would neutralize other summoned creatures simply do not work on them. The permanent Strength reduction at Margin 3 is the detail summoners should brief their allies about before the engagement — a target who has been hit at Margin 3 by a Wrath Fiend is permanently diminished until they can access Major Restoration. A summoner who deploys one against an enemy that matters should expect that enemy to have a lasting problem regardless of how the broader fight resolves.

---

## Pit Caller
**Threat Rating:** 4
**Origin:** Negative Plane
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 160 (Con 5 × 32, Massive)
**DR:** 6 (ancient fiend resilience)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 60 ft
**Attributes:** Str 5 / Con 5 / Agi 5 / Dex 5 / Int 7 / Wis 6 / Cha 7 / Luck 5
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Perception 6, Deception 7, Intimidate 7, Arcane 6
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight, Truesight 60 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fiend — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned. Resistance to fire, cold, lightning (+2 DR each). Fortune on saves vs magic. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Fiend Blade [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 10 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2) + 8 Negative damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 15 damage (10 + 5 Str) + 8 Negative damage; target Weakened + Sickened for 1 minute; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 15 damage + 8 Negative damage + Weakened + Sickened; target also loses 4 from Current Luck pool; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains 1 Exhaustion level
- **Negative Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 5), Range: 120 ft
  - Net 1: 16 Negative damage (Half DR); target loses 2 from Current Luck. Net 2: 28 Negative damage + Weakened for 1 minute; target loses 4 from Current Luck; no save. Net 3: 28 Negative damage + Weakened + Sickened for 1 minute; target loses 6 from Current Luck; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Call from the Pit (1/day) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, tears a rift to the lower Negative plane in a space within 60 feet. From this rift emerge 1d4 Gnashers and 1 Shadow Hound at the start of the Pit Caller's next turn. These creatures are not under the summoner's control — they are under the Pit Caller's control, and the Pit Caller directs them as it chooses. The rift closes after 1 minute. The summoner's Summoning Limit does not apply to these creatures as they are not summoned by the summoner.
- **Infernal Command:** Any Fiend of lower TR within 300 feet that is not already under another creature's control must make a Will save (Hard task, 2 successes) at the start of each of their turns or follow the Pit Caller's instructions instead. This includes other summoned Fiends if the summoner's Cooperative or Friendly disposition bond is not actively maintained.
- **Fear Aura:** 20-foot diameter; Will save Hard task (2 successes); failure: Frightened for 1 minute.
- **Bargain:** The Pit Caller can offer the summoner a deal at any point during the summoning. The terms it proposes will appear favorable. The terms it proposes will technically be favorable. The way those terms interact with the summoner's existing obligations, future plans, and the Pit Caller's own longer strategy is something the summoner should evaluate very carefully before accepting.
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**

**Description:** Pit Callers are the first Fiend the summoner genuinely needs to approach with comprehensive preparation. Infernal Command means other summoned Fiends in the area may switch allegiance if the summoner's disposition bond weakens. Call from the Pit produces creatures under the Pit Caller's control, not the summoner's — which is either a useful addition to the engagement or a serious problem depending on whether the summoner and Pit Caller's current instructions align. Bargain introduces an active negotiation element that no other summoned creature offers. A summoner who has prepared precise, gap-free terms and maintains those terms throughout the summoning will find a Pit Caller an extraordinarily capable ally. One who has not will find it begins working toward its own interests at the first available opportunity, and its interests tend to involve the summoner being obligated to it in ways the summoner did not intend.

---

## Void Fiend
**Threat Rating:** 5
**Origin:** Negative Plane
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 216 (Con 6 × 36, Massive)
**DR:** 7 (primordial fiend resilience)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Fly 80 ft
**Attributes:** Str 7 / Con 6 / Agi 5 / Dex 6 / Int 8 / Wis 7 / Cha 8 / Luck 6
**Skills:** Melee Combat 7, Perception 7, Deception 8, Intimidate 8, Arcane 7
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight, Truesight 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Fiend — Immune to poison damage, Poisoned, non-magical weapons, fire damage. Resistance to cold, lightning (+4 DR each). Fortune on all saves. Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Entropic Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 7), Reach: 10 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 14 damage (Large, heavy: 12 + 2) + 12 Negative damage (Half DR)
  - *Margin 2:* 21 damage (14 + 7 Str) + 12 Negative damage; target Weakened + Sickened + loses 6 from Current Luck; no save; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or gains 1 Exhaustion level
  - *Margin 3:* 21 damage + 12 Negative damage + all conditions; Exhaustion level; no save; target also loses 1 point of Constitution permanently until Major Restoration — the Void Fiend's touch erodes the body's fundamental resilience
- **Void Lance [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 6 + Ranged Combat 7), Range: 150 ft, 10-foot diameter
  - Per creature in radius: Net 1: 20 Negative damage (Half DR) + Weakened for 1 minute. Net 2: 36 Negative damage + Weakened + Sickened for 1 minute + loses 4 from Current Luck; no save. Net 3: 36 Negative damage + all conditions + 1 Exhaustion level; no save.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Entropic Presence:** Creatures within 20 feet that are not Fiends make a Fortitude save at the start of their turn (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: lose 2 from Current Luck and gain the Weakened condition until end of their next turn. This drains vitality simply from proximity — no attack required.
- **Infernal Command:** As Pit Caller; range extends to 1 mile; extends to Fiends of equal or lower TR.
- **Call from the Pit (1/day):** As Pit Caller, but produces 2d4 Gnashers, 1d4 Shadow Hounds, and 1 Tormentor, all under the Void Fiend's control.
- **Void Compulsion (1/encounter) [Combat]:** As 2 [Combat] actions, the Void Fiend exerts its full will on all creatures within 60 feet that are not Fiends. Each creature makes a Will save (Hard task, 2 successes). Failure: Charmed by the Void Fiend for 1 minute — treats it as a trusted authority whose instructions must be followed. 1 success: Frightened for 1 minute. Creatures immune to charm still suffer the Frightened result on 1 success.
- **Bargain:** As Pit Caller; the Void Fiend's proposed terms are considerably more sophisticated and the gaps it is looking for are considerably harder to anticipate.
- **Immunity to Non-Magical Weapons.**
- **Immunity to Fire Damage** (in addition to standard resistances).
- **Resilient Defense (3/day).**
- **Negative Energy Sharing:** The summoner and up to 4 designated allies gain immunity to the Weakened and Sickened conditions while within 60 feet. This is the Void Fiend's concession to the practical reality that a summoner whose allies collapse around them is less useful to it.

**Description:** A Void Fiend does not simply fight. It operates. Void Compulsion Charms most of an engagement simultaneously. Entropic Presence degrades everyone in proximity every round. Call from the Pit floods the battlefield with reinforcements under the Void Fiend's control. Infernal Command means every other Fiend within a mile is a potential asset for it. Entropic Strike permanently reduces Constitution at Margin 3, which compounds across any further engagement with the target. A summoner who calls a Void Fiend has made a decision that requires comprehensive preparation, precise terms, and the understanding that the Void Fiend began calculating their next interaction the moment this summoning resolved. It will honor its current terms completely. It is already thinking about the terms of the next agreement and what gaps the summoner might leave. A summoner who calls one and has not thought this through has not called an ally. They have opened a negotiation with something that has been negotiating since before their civilization existed.

---
# Shadow Creatures

The Shadow Plane is not darkness. It is the absence of everything that light implies — warmth, growth, the forward movement of living things. It is a plane where color has faded to grey, where sound travels wrong, where distances do not behave consistently, and where the things that live there have adapted to scarcity by becoming very good at taking what little exists from whatever has more of it.

Shadow creatures are not undead. They are living things shaped by a lightless environment where life energy is sparse and every creature competes for it. Most are predators by necessity rather than malice. They hunt because the Shadow Plane does not offer alternatives. When summoned to the prime material — a plane of abundant light, warmth, and life energy — they find themselves in what amounts to extreme surplus. Their behavior in this environment reflects that: they are acutely aware of the richness around them and drawn to it in ways that require active management from a summoner who wants them focused on a specific target rather than the nearest warm body.

They are not inherently evil. They are shaped by a plane that rewards predation and punishes hesitation. The distinction matters primarily to a summoner who is deciding how much latitude to give them.

Positive energy is their universal weakness. It is not merely damaging — it is antithetical to what they are in a way that fire is antithetical to ice. A Shadow creature struck by significant Positive energy does not simply take damage. It experiences the contact as a fundamental wrongness.

**Creature Type: Shadow**
All Shadow creatures share: Darkvision 120 ft. Shadow Meld (passive) — in dim light or darkness, Fortune on Stealth checks and attacks against them add 1 to both dice. Positive energy vulnerability — full damage from Positive energy, no DR reduction. Cold Resistance (+2 DR). Do not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

Sunlight Sensitivity is noted per entry where it applies. Not all Shadow creatures suffer equally in bright light — some have adapted through exposure to the prime material, and this is reflected in their individual entries.

---

## Shade
**Threat Rating:** 1/8
**Origin:** Shadow
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 10 (Con 2 × 5, Fragile)
**DR:** 0
**Speed:** 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 1 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 3 / Int 2 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 2
**Skills:** Melee Combat 2, Stealth 5, Perception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Shadow — Darkvision 120 ft. Shadow Meld (passive). Positive energy vulnerability. Cold Resistance (+2 DR). Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.
**Sunlight Sensitivity:** In bright light, adds 1 to both attack dice and skill check dice.

**Attacks:**
- **Strength Drain [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 2), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 4 Negative damage (Ignore DR); target's Strength reduced by 1 for 1 hour
  - *Margin 2:* 4 Negative damage; Strength reduced by 2 for 1 hour; target gains Weakened condition
  - *Margin 3:* 4 Negative damage; Strength reduced by 3 for 1 hour; Weakened; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or movement speed reduced by 10 until Strength restores

**Special Abilities:**
- **Amorphous:** Can move through spaces as narrow as 1 inch without squeezing.
- **Shadow Form:** While in dim light or darkness, DR increases to 6 against all non-magical damage and non-Positive energy damage. Positive energy ignores this entirely.
- **Shadow Spawn:** If a non-undead creature is killed while their Strength has been reduced to 0 by the Shade's attacks, a new Shade rises from their shadow at the start of the next round. This new Shade is not under the summoner's control — it is a free Shadow creature that has just arrived on the prime material through the death. The summoner's Summoning Limit does not apply to it.

**Description:** Shades are the most basic expression of the Shadow Plane's predatory nature — barely-manifested hunger that drains strength through contact. Their combat capability is minimal against anything that fights back effectively, but Strength Drain accumulates across hits in a way that compounds. A target hit three times by a Shade over the course of a fight has lost significant Strength, which affects their melee damage, carry capacity, and Athletics checks. Shadow Form in darkness makes them genuinely difficult to put down through mundane means. A summoner who calls one for direct combat will be disappointed. One who calls one to weaken a specific target over several rounds while other elements of the encounter occupy that target's attention will find it performs the role adequately.

---

## Shadow Lurker
**Threat Rating:** 1/4
**Origin:** Shadow
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 14 (Con 2 × 7, Standard)
**DR:** 1
**Speed:** 40 ft, Climb 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 2 / Con 2 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 3 / Wis 3 / Cha 2 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 3, Stealth 6, Perception 4, Athletics 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Shadow — Darkvision 120 ft. Shadow Meld (passive). Positive energy vulnerability. Cold Resistance (+2 DR). Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.
**Sunlight Sensitivity:** In bright light, adds 1 to both attack dice and skill check dice.

**Attacks:**
- **Shadow Claw [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 3), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 5 damage + 3 Negative damage (Half DR); target's Current Luck reduced by 1
  - *Margin 2:* 7 damage (5 + 2 Str) + 3 Negative damage; Current Luck reduced by 2; target gains Disoriented condition until end of their next turn
  - *Margin 3:* 7 damage + 3 Negative damage; Current Luck reduced by 3; Disoriented; target makes Will save (1 success) or Frightened until end of their next turn as the darkness seems to press in around them

**Special Abilities:**
- **Amorphous:** As Shade.
- **Shadow Form:** As Shade.
- **Ceiling Stalker:** Can move across ceilings and vertical surfaces without Athletics checks. When attacking from above, subtract 1 from both attack dice.
- **Luck Drain:** Current Luck reduced by the Shadow Lurker's attacks does not return until the target takes a long rest. This is cumulative across multiple hits.

**Description:** Shadow Lurkers hunt from above. They use Ceiling Stalker to position on ceilings or high walls, drop onto targets from advantage, and drain Current Luck — which degrades save capability in a way that compounds across the encounter. A target who has taken three hits from a Shadow Lurker is functionally unable to resist saves effectively for the rest of the session. A summoner who calls one to soften a high-priority target before a difficult encounter, or to reduce a spellcaster's save capability during a negotiation that might turn hostile, will find it performs that specific function cleanly. It will not tell the summoner what it has learned about the environment from its ceiling vantage. A summoner who asks will get an accurate answer.

---

## Shade Walker
**Threat Rating:** 1/2
**Origin:** Shadow
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 27 (Con 3 × 9, Tough)
**DR:** 2 (shadow substance)
**Speed:** 40 ft, Climb 40 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 3 / Agi 5 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 3 / Luck 3
**Skills:** Melee Combat 5, Stealth 6, Perception 4, Deception 3
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, See Invisibility
**Initiative Bonus:** +5 (Agi 5)
**Creature Type:** Shadow — Darkvision 120 ft. Shadow Meld (passive). Positive energy vulnerability. Cold Resistance (+2 DR). Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.
**Sunlight Sensitivity:** In bright light, adds 1 to both attack dice and skill check dice.

**Attacks:**
- **Shadow Strike [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 5 + Melee Combat 5), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage + 4 Negative damage (Ignore DR); target loses 2 from Current Luck
  - *Margin 2:* 12 damage (8 + 4 Str) + 4 Negative damage; Current Luck reduced by 3; target Disoriented until start of their next turn; target loses the Hidden condition if they had it
  - *Margin 3:* 12 damage + 4 Negative damage; Current Luck reduced by 4; Disoriented; target also Dazed until end of their next turn — the shadow energy disrupts their timing and coordination

**Special Abilities:**
- **Amorphous:** As above.
- **Shadow Form:** As above.
- **Planar Step (1/short rest):** As a [Move] action, steps briefly into the Shadow Plane and re-emerges up to 30 feet away in any dim or dark location it can see. Does not provoke opportunity attacks. Cannot be used in bright light.
- **See Invisibility:** Sees invisible creatures and objects within normal sight range.

**Description:** Shade Walkers are assassins. They use Planar Step to close distance without exposure, strike from darkness, and retreat before retaliation. See Invisibility means they are not countered by the standard defensive measure of simply turning invisible. The Negative damage on Shadow Strike ignores DR entirely at Margin 1 — the shadow energy bypasses physical protection because it is not attacking the body but the life force animating it. A summoner who needs a specific target's Luck depleted quickly, or who needs an invisible or concealed target hit without first locating them, will find Shade Walkers capable of both. Their intelligence is sufficient to follow moderately complex instructions and they do not require simplification.

---

## Dark Stalker
**Threat Rating:** 1
**Origin:** Shadow
**Size:** Medium
**HP:** 40 (Con 5 × 8, Standard)
**DR:** 3 (dense shadow-substance)
**Speed:** 50 ft, Climb 50 ft
**Attributes:** Str 4 / Con 5 / Agi 6 / Dex 5 / Int 5 / Wis 5 / Cha 4 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Stealth 7, Perception 5, Deception 4, Athletics 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight, See Invisibility
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Shadow — Darkvision 120 ft. Shadow Meld (passive). Positive energy vulnerability. Cold Resistance (+2 DR). Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Shadow Blade [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 8 damage + 6 Negative damage (Ignore DR); target loses 3 from Current Luck
  - *Margin 2:* 12 damage (8 + 4 Str) + 6 Negative damage; Current Luck reduced by 4; target Disoriented + Dazed until end of their next turn; no save
  - *Margin 3:* 12 damage + 6 Negative damage; Current Luck reduced by 5; Disoriented + Dazed; target makes Will save (1 success) or Frightened until end of their next turn as the accumulated shadow energy overwhelms their sense of safety
- **Shadow Bolt [Combat]:** Ranged attack (Dex 5 + Ranged Combat 4), Range: 60 ft
  - Net 1: 8 Negative damage (Half DR); target loses 2 from Current Luck. Net 2: 12 Negative damage + Disoriented until end of their next turn; Current Luck reduced by 3; no save. Net 3: 12 Negative damage + Dazed for 1 minute; Current Luck reduced by 4; Will save each round to end.

**Special Abilities:**
- **Shadow Form:** As above; DR increases to 8 against non-magical, non-Positive damage in dim light or darkness.
- **Planar Step (2/short rest):** As Shade Walker; usable twice per short rest. The Dark Stalker has spent enough time on the prime material to cross more fluidly.
- **Devil's Sight:** Sees through magical darkness as if bright light.
- **Death Sense:** Automatically detects creatures below half HP within 60 feet and knows their precise location regardless of concealment or invisibility.
- **Shadow Ambush:** When the Dark Stalker attacks on the same turn it used Planar Step, it has Fortune on that attack.

**Description:** Dark Stalkers are the first Shadow creature with genuine tactical sophistication. They manage their Planar Steps as resources — one to open with Shadow Ambush from an unexpected angle, one held for extraction when the engagement turns unfavorable. Death Sense ensures they always know which target is most vulnerable. Shadow Form in darkness gives them DR 8 against mundane attacks, making them effectively immune to conventional weapons while in their preferred environment. A summoner who controls lighting conditions — ensuring the engagement happens in dim light or darkness — will find a Dark Stalker performs at well above its TR. The creature is also the first Shadow creature that actively evaluates when retreat serves its interests better than continued engagement, which it will execute without prompting if the tactical situation warrants it.

---

## Nightmare
**Threat Rating:** 2
**Origin:** Shadow
**Size:** Large
**HP:** 76 (Con 4 × 19, Massive)
**DR:** 3 (shadow-dense hide)
**Speed:** 70 ft, Fly 100 ft
**Attributes:** Str 6 / Con 4 / Agi 6 / Dex 4 / Int 4 / Wis 4 / Cha 5 / Luck 4
**Skills:** Melee Combat 6, Perception 5, Intimidate 5, Athletics 5, Stealth 4
**Senses:** Darkvision 120 ft, Devil's Sight
**Initiative Bonus:** +6 (Agi 6)
**Creature Type:** Shadow — Darkvision 120 ft. Shadow Meld (passive). Positive energy vulnerability. Cold Resistance (+2 DR). Does not need air, food, drink, or sleep.

**Attacks:**
- **Flaming Hooves [Combat]:** Melee attack (Agi 6 + Melee Combat 6), Reach: 5 ft
  - *Margin 1:* 12 damage (Large, standard: 8 + 2 + 2 shadow density) + 4 fire damage (Half DR); target gains Singed condition
  - *Margin 2:* 18 damage (12 + 6 Str) + 4 fire damage; target knocked Prone; no save; target gains Ignited condition
  - *Margin 3:* 18 damage + 4 fire damage; Prone + Ignited; target makes Fortitude save (1 success) or Stunned until end of their next turn from the concussive force of the hooves
